### [42] [Where Does Authorship Signal Emerge in Encoder-Based Language Models?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19908)
*Francis Kulumba,Guillaume Vimont,Laurent Romary,Florian Cafiero*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文通过机械可解释性分析揭示，作者归属模型性能差异的关键在于评分机制引导编码器整合特征的路径不同，而非表示质量的差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探讨为何基于相同预训练编码器、数据和损失函数的作者归属模型，仅因评分机制不同就会导致性能产生高达四倍的差异，并试图揭示这种性能差距背后的深层可解释性机理。

Method: 使用了机械可解释性（Mechanistic Interpretability）工具进行分析，通过因果干预（Causal Intervention）探究评分机制如何影响编码器中作者信号的整合位置，并从评分器的梯度结构（Gradient Structure）和训练动力学（Training Dynamics）层面推导出性能差异的根本原因。

Result: 实验发现，均值池化（Mean Pooling）强制模型在较早至中间层整合信息，而后期交互（Late Interaction）则将整合过程推迟到更深层。不同评分机制导致了截然不同的梯度结构和训练轨迹，决定了编码器如何处理和整合作者风格特征。

Conclusion: 研究表明，作者归属模型的性能差距主要源于评分机制（Scoring Mechanism）对特征整合路径的差异化引导，而非编码器表示能力本身的差异。通过理解这种机制，研究者可以更好地优化模型架构以适配特定的下游任务。

Abstract: Authorship attribution models fine-tuned with the same pretrained encoder, data, and loss can differ four-fold in performance depending only on their scoring mechanism. We use mechanistic interpretability tools to explain this gap. Stylistic features such as word length, punctuation density, and function-word frequency are equally available at every layer in every model, including in an off-the-shelf control encoder, hence the gap not coming from representation quality. Instead, causal intervention shows that the scorer determines where the encoder consolidates authorship signal. Mean pooling forces consolidation by early to mid layers, while late interaction defers it to later layers. We further derive this difference from the gradient structure of each scorer, and training dynamics reveal distinct learning trajectories that follow from that difference.

### [43] [What Are LLMs Doing to Scientific Communication? Measuring Changes in Writing Practices and Reading Experience](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19936)
*Filip Miletić,Neele Falk*

Main category: cs.CL

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 构建了包含3.7万篇自然语言处理领域论文（2020-2024年）的语料库，并创建了一个包含3000个人类撰写片段及其LLM改进版本的数据集。2. 运用历时性词汇分析技术，研究词频与语境演变。3. 建模复杂风格特征（包括句法结构、词汇复杂度、词汇多样性等）。4. 开展了一项包含20位领域专家的试点注释研究，通过主观评价评估读者的阅读体验。

Result: 研究发现：1. 词汇的使用频率与上下文发生了显著变化，呈现出语义专门化与泛化并存的趋势。2. 经LLM修改的文本表现出特定的句法结构偏好、词汇更长且更复杂、词汇多样性降低。3. 领域专家普遍认为LLM改进后的文本更易懂且更有吸引力，但同时专家们对LLM的广泛使用持负面的定性态度。

Conclusion: 随着大语言模型（LLM）的普及，科学写作风格正在发生可观测的演变。尽管LLM提升了文本的可读性和吸引力，但也引入了特定的句法倾向和词汇特征。这种技术带来的改变在客观文本指标与主观专家评价之间存在一定张力，反映出学术界对AI辅助写作复杂而矛盾的态度。

Abstract: Has the style of scientific communication changed due to the growing use of large language models in the writing process? We address this question in the domain of Natural Language Processing by leveraging two data resources we create: a naturalistic corpus of over 37,000 papers from the ACL Anthology (2020-2024); and a synthetic dataset of 3,000 human-written passages and their LLM-generated improvements. We first implement a series of diachronic lexical analyses, showing that both word frequency and usage contexts have changed significantly over time, indicating semantic specialization in some cases and generalization in others. Broadening our perspective, we then model a range of more complex stylistic features and find that LLM-modified texts more frequently contain certain syntactic constructions, more complex and longer words and a lower lexical diversity. Finally, we connect these changes in writing practices to subjective reading experience through a pilot annotation study with 20 domain experts. They overall rate LLM-improved texts as more understandable and exciting, but also express negative qualitative attitudes towards LLMs, highlighting the strongly subjective effect of AI-assisted writing on reading experience.

### [44] [FlexDraft: Flexible Speculative Decoding via Attention Tuning and Bonus-Guided Calibration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20022)
*Yaojie Zhang,Jianuo Huang,Junlong Ke,Yuhang Han,Yongji Long,Tianchen Zhao,Biqing Qi,Linfeng Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对现有并行推测解码在大批量下性能崩塌及质量损失的问题，FlexDraft 提出了一种无损的推测解码框架，通过注意力微调、逻辑校准和动态模式切换，实现了高效且灵活的 LLM 推理加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的推测解码存在 drafting 和验证阶段的相互等待以及内存开销问题。现有的并行推测解码方案在大批量下存在验证不匹配导致的吞吐量下降问题，且往往需要昂贵的预训练或牺牲生成质量。因此，需要一种能适应不同批大小且保持无损（lossless）的推测解码框架。

Method: 1. 注意力微调（Attention Tuning）：仅微调最后几层的注意力投影器以生成高质量草稿，保持自回归路径冻结以确保模型质量。2. 奖励引导校准（Bonus-guided Calibration）：利用轻量级 MLP 根据已解析的奖励标记校准草稿逻辑值，缓解验证不匹配问题。3. 灵活解码（Flex Decoding）：根据批处理大小动态切换并行与串行模式，并依据置信度动态调整验证长度。

Result: FlexDraft 能够有效适应不同批大小，显著降低了推测验证不匹配带来的计算开销，提升了 LLM 在多种推理场景下的整体推理吞吐量，同时保持了与原模型完全一致的生成质量。

Conclusion: FlexDraft 通过结合“注意力微调”、“基于奖励的校准”以及“自适应解码策略”，在保证模型输出质量的前提下，有效解决了并行推测解码在大批量场景下吞吐量下降及验证不匹配的问题，实现了推测解码在不同批大小下的性能优化。

Abstract: Speculative decoding accelerates memory-bound LLM inference without quality degradation by using a fast drafter to propose multiple candidate tokens and the target model to verify them in parallel. However, conventional sequential speculative decoding suffers from mutual waiting between drafting and verification, and repeated exchange of intermediate states further increases memory access overhead. Parallel speculative decoding addresses this limitation by performing drafting and verification within a single target forward pass, allowing future drafts to be prepared while current candidates are being verified. Although effective at small batch sizes, existing parallel speculative decoding methods either require costly continual pretraining with quality degradation or suffer from low acceptance rates. More importantly, this paradigm inherently suffers from uncertainty in both the bonus token and the accepted length, leading to draft verification mismatch and causing throughput gains to collapse at large batch sizes. To address these limitations, we introduce FlexDraft, a lossless speculative decoding framework that flexibly adapts to varying batch sizes through three key designs. (1) Attention Tuning enables block diffusion drafting by tuning only the attention projectors of the final few layers on mask tokens, while keeping the autoregressive path frozen to preserve the target distribution and produce high quality drafts with minimal trainable parameters. (2) Bonus-guided Calibration uses a lightweight MLP conditioned on the resolved bonus token to calibrate draft logits, mitigating draft verification mismatch caused by bonus token uncertainty. (3) Flex Decoding dynamically switches between parallel draft and verify at small batch sizes and sequential draft then verify at large batch sizes, and adjusts verification length based on draft confidence to eliminate redundant computation.

</details>


### [45] [Language Mutations Sustain the Persistences of Conspiracy Theories on Social Media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20050)
*Calvin Yixiang Cheng,Dorian Quelle,Scott A. Hale*

TL;DR: 该研究发现阴谋论通过不断的语言与结构变异来延长其在社交媒体上的生命周期；审核策略应从关注单一文本转向针对阴谋论的核心演变逻辑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探讨语言的动态变异如何影响阴谋论在社交媒体上的持续传播，以理解阴谋论为何能够长期存在并不断演化，从而为在线内容审核提供理论依据。

Method: 研究采用了计算语言学分析与生存模型（Survival Modelling）相结合的方法，利用为期三年的社交媒体（X平台）阴谋论帖子数据集进行量化分析，并辅以定性分析以识别具体的变异模式。

Result: 研究发现，具有更高语义变异性的阴谋论往往具有更长的生命周期。具体的心理语言学属性（如代词、社交参考词、认知过程术语等）及核心要素（行动者、行动、目标）的变异均与阴谋论寿命的延长显著相关。主要变异模式表现为简化与同化。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了语言变异是阴谋论在社交媒体上长期存在的关键因素。内容审核策略不应仅关注单一形态的内容，而应识别并干预阴谋论的核心要素，以应对其持续演变带来的传播挑战。

Abstract: This study investigates how language mutations affect the persistent diffusion of conspiracy theories on social media. Drawing on a three-year dataset of conspiracy-related posts from X, and applying computational linguistic analysis alongside survival modelling, we find that conspiracy claims with greater semantic mutations have substantially longer lifespans. Mutations in psycholinguistic properties, including pronouns, social reference words, cognitive process terms, risk- and health- related vocabularies, are associated with extended lifespans. Mutations in actor, action and target (AAT) categories are associated with longer lifespans as well. Qualitative analysis identifies two predominant mutation patterns: simplification and assimilation, at both linguistic and AAT structural levels. Taken together, the results advance our understanding of how language mutations contribute to conspiracy persistence online and shed lights on longitudinal content moderation strategies. We argue that content moderation should consider the mutability of conspiracy claims and focus on the core claims that can address their potential variations.

### [46] [PromptRad: Knowledge-Enhanced Multi-Label Prompt-Tuning for Low-Resource Radiology Report Labeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20052)
*Ying-Jia Lin,Tzu-Chin Lo,Ping-Chien Li,Chi-Tung Cheng,Chien-Hung Liao,Hung-Yu Kao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: PromptRad 是一种基于提示学习的放射学报告自动标注框架，通过整合医学知识库并采用小样本提示调优策略，在极低标注数据条件下实现了优异的分类性能，有效解决了临床报告标注的数据瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的放射学报告标注方法存在局限性：基于规则的方法难以处理临床描述的多样性，而传统的 PLM 微调方法在临床环境下往往缺乏足够的标注数据。

Method: 提出 PromptRad 方法，将多标签分类任务重新表述为掩码语言建模（MLM）任务；利用 UMLS 医学术语集中的同义词构建多词动词化器（multi-word verbalizer）以增强类别表示；在无需额外分类层的情况下对预训练语言模型（PLM）进行提示调优（prompt-tuning）。

Result: 在肝脏 CT 报告数据集上的实验表明，仅使用 32 个标注样本，PromptRad 的表现即优于字典法和传统微调基线，并能达到与 GPT-4 相当的性能；同时，该模型在处理复杂的否定模式方面表现更优。

Conclusion: PromptRad 是一种针对放射学报告标注的高效、低资源解决方案，特别适用于数据稀缺的临床环境，且能够通过知识增强和提示调优达到与大型模型相媲美的效果。

Abstract: Automatic report labeling facilitates the identification of clinical findings from unstructured text and enables large-scale annotation for medical imaging research. Existing rule-based labelers struggle with the diverse descriptions in clinical reports, while fine-tuning pre-trained language models (PLMs) requires large amounts of labeled data that are often unavailable in clinical settings. In this paper, we propose PromptRad, a knowledge-enhanced multi-label \textbf{prompt}-tuning approach for \textbf{rad}iology report labeling under low-resource settings. PromptRad reformulates multi-label classification as masked language modeling and incorporates synonyms from the UMLS Metathesaurus into a multi-word verbalizer to enrich category representations. By fine-tuning the PLM without additional classification layers, PromptRad requires substantially less labeled data than conventional fine-tuning. Experiments on liver CT reports show that PromptRad outperforms dictionary-based and fine-tuning baselines with only 32 labeled training examples, and achieves competitive performance with GPT-4 despite using a much smaller model. Further analysis demonstrates that PromptRad captures complex negation patterns more effectively than existing methods, making it a promising solution for report labeling in data-scarce clinical scenarios. Our code is available at https://github.com/ila-lab/PromptRad.

</details>


### [47] [Rewarding Beliefs, Not Actions: Consistency-Guided Credit Assignment for Long-Horizon Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20061)
*Wenjie Tang,Minne Li,Sijie Huang,Liquan Xiao,Yuan Zhou*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ReBel算法通过显式建模信念状态并引入信念一致性自监督机制，有效解决了长期任务中因部分可观测性导致的决策偏差和信用分配难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在部分可观测的长期交互任务中，模型存在信念漂移问题，且延迟奖励导致难以进行准确的时序信用分配，限制了大语言模型智能体的性能。

Method: 提出了一种名为ReBel的流程级强化学习算法，核心包括：1. 显式结构化信念状态建模，用于总结交互历史；2. 信念一致性监督（belief-consistency supervision），将预测信念与反馈差异转化为密集自监督信号；3. 信念感知分组（belief-aware grouping），通过比较相似信念状态下的轨迹来优化优势估计。

Result: 在ALFWorld和WebShop等基准测试中，ReBel的任务成功率较基准算法（GRPO）提升了最高20.4个百分点，且采样效率提高了2.1倍。

Conclusion: 研究表明，在部分可观测的长期任务中，引入信念感知（belief-aware）的自我监督机制能够有效克服信用分配难题，是提升大模型智能体决策可靠性和采样效率的有效路径。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards (RLVR) is a promising paradigm for improving large language model (LLM) agents on long-horizon interactive tasks. However, in partially observable environments, incomplete observations cause agent beliefs to drift over time, while delayed rewards obscure the causal impact of intermediate decisions, exacerbating temporal credit assignment challenges. To address this, we propose ReBel (Reward Belief), a process-level reinforcement learning algorithm that explicitly models structured belief states to summarize interaction history and guide subsequent policy learning. ReBel introduces belief-consistency supervision, converting discrepancies between predicted beliefs and observed feedback into dense self-supervised signals without requiring external step-wise annotations or verifiers. It also employs belief-aware grouping to compare trajectories under similar belief states, yielding more robust and lower-variance advantage estimates. We evaluate ReBel on challenging long-horizon benchmarks, including ALFWorld and WebShop. ReBel improves task success by up to $20.4$ percentage points over the episode-level baseline GRPO and increases sample efficiency by $2.1\times$. These results suggest that belief-aware self-supervision is a promising direction for reliable long-horizon decision-making under partial observability. Code is available at: https://github.com/Fateyetian/Rebel.git.

</details>


### [48] [Text-to-SPARQL Generation with Reinforcement Learning: A GRPO-based Approach on DBLP](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20066)
*Jann Pfeifer,Debayan Banerjee,Ricardo Usbeck*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究证明了利用GRPO强化学习训练小型语言模型进行知识图谱问答是有效的。即使没有金标准查询标注，仅通过执行反馈奖励也能显著提升模型性能，为低资源环境下的Text-to-SPARQL任务提供了一条可行路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的知识图谱问答（KGQA）方法通常依赖庞大的模型或需要昂贵的金标准查询标注。本研究旨在探索是否可以通过基于结果奖励的强化学习，利用小型指令微调模型（1.7B参数）实现学术领域的零样本Text-to-SPARQL生成，以降低对数据标注的依赖。

Method: 研究采用了基于群体相对策略优化（GRPO）的强化学习方法，在Qwen3-1.7B模型上进行训练。方法核心在于利用执行反馈、结构约束和答案级奖励来引导模型生成SPARQL查询，并额外探讨了结合金标准查询形状（Shaping）的变体。模型输入结合了自然语言问题与关于实体和关系的符号提示。

Result: GRPO训练显著提升了零样本基准的性能，并在处理未见过的模板时表现出良好的泛化能力。对比实验显示，监督式DoRA微调在相同模型规模下达到了更高的整体准确率，但消融实验证明，执行反馈奖励贡献了主要的性能提升，而引入基于金标准查询的形状奖励带来的额外收益有限。

Conclusion: 研究表明，基于结果的强化学习（如GRPO）是训练小型语言模型进行知识图谱问答的一种可行策略，特别是在缺乏金标准查询（Gold Query）进行监督的情况下。虽然监督微调在整体准确率上仍占优势，但强化学习模型在零样本场景下展现出了极具竞争力的泛化能力。

Abstract: Knowledge graph question answering seeks to translate natural language questions into executable queries over knowledge graphs, but existing approaches often rely on large models or full supervision in the form of gold query annotations. This study examines whether reinforcement learning with outcome-based rewards can train a small instruction-tuned language model to perform zero-shot Text-to-SPARQL generation in the scholarly domain. Group-Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) is applied to the Qwen3-1.7B model on DBLP-QuAD, using prompts that combine natural language questions with symbolic hints about entities and relations. Training relies on execution feedback, structural constraints, and answer-level rewards, with an additional variant that incorporates gold-query-based shaping. The resulting models are compared to the unmodified zero-shot baseline and to a supervised DoRA-finetuned baseline across answer-level accuracy, execution accuracy, category-wise scores, and generalization to held-out templates. GRPO substantially improves over the zero-shot baseline and exhibits competitive generalization, while supervised DoRA finetuning achieves higher overall accuracy on the same model scale. Ablation analyses indicate that execution-based rewards account for most gains, with additional shaping yielding limited additional benefit, suggesting that outcome-based reinforcement learning is a viable training strategy when gold queries are unavailable for token-level supervision.

### [49] [CopT: Contrastive On-Policy Thinking with Continuous Spaces for General and Agentic Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20075)
*Dachuan Shi,Hanlin Zhu,Xiangchi Yuan,Wanjia Zhao,Kejing Xia,Wen Xiao,Wenke Lee*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: CopT 是一种新型推理框架，通过“先回答后反思”的机制及基于 Embedding 对比的可靠性评估，在无需额外训练的情况下，显著降低了推理成本并提升了模型处理复杂任务的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统思维链（CoT）范式强制要求在回答前进行漫长的思考，导致即便模型已知答案也会产生不必要的 Token 消耗（即“执行性推理”），且在简单问题上也存在不必要的延迟。为此，需要一种更高效的、能根据回答可靠性自适应调整思维过程的推理框架。

Method: 1. 提出“CopT”推理流水线：改变传统思维链（先思考后回答）的范式，转为先生成草稿回答，再进行有条件的“反思与修正”；
2. 构建基于对比验证的置信度估计：通过对比离散 Token 输入与连续 Embedding 输入下模型对生成 Token 的支持度，计算序列级反向 KL 散度估计器，用于量化回答的可靠性；
3. 动态推理控制：当置信度不足时触发后续思维，利用第二个 KL 估计器动态控制草稿回答的可视性，以平衡信息利用与偏见规避。

Result: 在数学、编程及智能体推理任务中，CopT 相比传统方法最高提升了 23% 的准确率，同时在保持或提升准确率的前提下，最高降低了 57% 的 Token 使用量。

Conclusion: CopT 通过将“回答优先”与“置信度验证”相结合，证明了无需额外训练即可通过反向思维链流程显著优化大模型的推理效率与准确性，为解决大模型推理中的“过度思考”问题提供了有效范式。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) is a standard approach for eliciting reasoning capabilities from large language models (LLMs). However, the common CoT paradigm treats thinking as a prerequisite for answering, which can delay access to plausible answers and incur unnecessary token costs even when the model is able to identify an answer before extended thinking, a behavior known as performative reasoning. In this paper, we introduce CopT, a reformulated reasoning pipeline that reverses the usual order of thinking and answering. Instead of thinking before answering, CopT first elicits a draft answer and then invokes subsequent on-policy thinking conditioned on its own draft answer for reflection and correction. To assess whether the draft answer should be trusted, CopT recasts continuous embeddings as inference-time contrastive verifiers. Specifically, it contrasts the model's support for the same generated tokens under discrete-token inputs and continuous-embedding inputs, yielding a sequence-level reverse KL estimator for answer reliability. Our analysis shows that under certain assumptions, the expected estimate equals the mutual information between the unresolved latent state and the emitted answer token, explaining why it captures answer-relevant uncertainty rather than arbitrary uncertainty in the latent state. When the answer is deemed insufficiently reliable, CopT performs further on-policy thinking, where a second KL estimator dynamically controls draft-answer visibility, preserving useful partial information while reducing the risk of being misled by unreliable content. Across mathematics, coding, and agentic reasoning tasks, CopT improves peak accuracy by up to 23% and reduces token usage by up to 57% at comparable or higher accuracy, without any additional training. The code is available at https://github.com/sdc17/CopT.

</details>


### [50] [BalanceRAG: Joint Risk Calibration for Cascaded Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20084)
*Zijun Jia,Yuanchang Ye,Sen Jia,Yiyao Qian,Haoning Wang,Baojie Chen,Diyin Tang,Jinsong Yu,Zhiyuan Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: BalanceRAG 是一种级联检索增强生成（RAG）的校准框架，通过二维风险自适应阈值选择，在保证系统输出可信度的前提下，有效降低了冗余的检索调用并提升了系统整体效能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然 RAG 可以提升 LLM 的事实准确性，但对所有查询进行检索既不必要也不经济。现有的级联 RAG 方法通常在各阶段独立进行不确定性校准，导致系统决策过于保守。因此，需要一种能够平衡 LLM 原生输出与检索增强输出、并能实现全局风险可控的校准机制。

Method: BalanceRAG 框架将 LLM-only 和 RAG 分支的不确定性评分视为二维格点上的操作点，利用序列图形化检验（sequential graphical testing）技术来识别满足目标风险水平的安全操作点，从而实现对系统级错误率的精确控制。此外，该方法还支持多风险校准，能够同时对检索调用频率和输出准确性进行联合约束。

Result: 在三个开放域问答数据集上的实验表明，BalanceRAG 不仅严格达到了预设的风险阈值，而且在保持更高覆盖率和更多正确示例的同时，显著减少了不必要的检索调用次数，优于传统的“始终开启”式 RAG 系统。

Conclusion: BalanceRAG 通过引入风险自适应阈值校准，有效解决了传统级联 RAG 在不同阶段独立校准导致的保守性问题。该方法能够在保证系统级错误率的前提下，最大化覆盖率并减少不必要的检索开销，是实现高效、可信检索增强生成的有力工具。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can enhance factuality via retrieval-augmented generation (RAG), but applying RAG to every query is unnecessary when the model-only answer is reliable. This motivates cascaded RAG: each query is first handled by an LLM-only branch, escalated to a RAG fallback only if the primary branch is uncertain, and abstained from when neither branch is sufficiently trustworthy. However, calibrating such cascades stage by stage may be conservative, since the final utility depends on joint uncertainty thresholding of LLM-only and RAG. In this work, we develop BalanceRAG to certify threshold pairs at a target risk level. Given uncertainty scores from the two branches, BalanceRAG frames each threshold pair as an operating point on a two-dimensional lattice and identifies safe operating points using sequential graphical testing. This enables risk-adaptive threshold calibration, controlling the system-level error rate among accepted points, while retaining more examples. Furthermore, BalanceRAG extends to multi-risk calibration, allowing retrieval usage to be bounded together with the selection-conditioned risk. Experiments on three open-domain question answering (QA) benchmarks across multiple LLM backbones demonstrate that BalanceRAG meets prescribed risk levels, preserves higher coverage and more accepted correct examples, and reduces unnecessary retrieval calls compared with always-on RAG.

</details>


### [51] [ThoughtTrace: Understanding User Thoughts in Real-World LLM Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20087)
*Chuanyang Jin,Binze Li,Haopeng Xie,Cathy Mengying Fang,Tianjian Li,Shayne Longpre,Hongxiang Gu,Maximillian Chen,Tianmin Shu*

TL;DR: 本文推出了首个包含用户对话意图与反应思维的大规模数据集 ThoughtTrace，证明了将这些“隐性思维”显式化不仅能提升模型对用户行为的预测精度，还能通过细粒度的对齐信号推动个性化智能助手的研发。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的对话式 AI 数据集仅记录了用户的显性输入（即“说什么”），而忽视了用户发送指令背后的潜在动机、意图及对回复的心理评价（即“想什么”）。为了填补这一认知空缺，作者提出了 ThoughtTrace。

Method: 研究人员收集了包含 1,058 名用户、2,155 次多轮对话及 10,174 条自我报告思维标注的 ThoughtTrace 数据集。通过分析思维与对话内容的语义差异、评估当前 LLM 推理思维的能力，并验证了思维在改进用户行为预测及通过“思维引导重写”进行个性化对齐任务中的应用价值。

Result: 研究发现，用户思维与对话信息在语义上具有显著差异，现有的前沿大模型难以仅通过上下文准确推断出这些思维。实验表明，将思维作为推理阶段的上下文可提升模型对用户行为的预测能力，且利用思维进行回复重写能为个性化助手训练提供更细粒度的对齐信号。

Conclusion: ThoughtTrace 建立了一个全新的数据集模态——“用户思维”，它能够揭示人机交互背后的认知动态，为构建能深入理解并适应用户潜在目标、偏好和需求的下一代智能助手奠定了基础。

Abstract: Conversational AI has now reached billions of users, yet existing datasets capture only what people say, not what they think. We introduce ThoughtTrace, the first large-scale dataset that pairs real-world multi-turn human--AI conversations with users' self-reported thoughts: their reasons for sending prompts and reactions to assistant responses. ThoughtTrace comprises 1,058 users, 2,155 conversations, 17,058 turns, and 10,174 thought annotations collected across 20 language models. Our analysis shows that ThoughtTrace captures long-horizon, topically diverse interactions, and that thoughts are semantically distinct from messages, difficult for frontier LLMs to infer from context, diverse in content, and tied to conversation stages. We further demonstrate the utility of thoughts for downstream modeling. First, thoughts improve user-behavior prediction as inference-time context. Second, thought-guided rewrites provide fine-grained alignment signals for training personalized assistants. Together, ThoughtTrace establishes user thoughts as a new data modality for studying the cognitive dynamics behind human--AI interaction and provides a foundation for building assistants that better understand and adapt to users' latent goals, preferences, and needs.

### [52] [MixRea: Benchmarking Explicit-Implicit Reasoning in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20128)
*Yuanqing Cai,Ziyi Huang,Minhao Liu,Lixin Duan,Wen Li,Yanru Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 研究揭示了大型语言模型普遍存在类似于人类的“非注意盲视”缺陷，即在明确任务指令下容易忽略细微的语境信息，并提出了一种通过恢复隐含关系来提升模型推理能力的有效提示方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受到人类认知心理学中“非注意盲视”（Inattentional Blindness）理论的启发，研究者质疑在人类偏好语料上训练的大型语言模型是否会表现出类似的缺陷，即在执行明确任务指令时，无法察觉到细微但至关重要的语境信息。

Method: 1. 构建了包含2,246道多选题的“显隐推理”评估基准（MixRea），涵盖9种推理类型；2. 评估了21种先进LLM的表现；3. 提出了“潜在关系补全提示（PRCP）”方法，通过显式恢复被忽略的因果关系来提升推理性能。

Result: 实验结果显示，即使是表现最好的模型（Gemini 2.5 Pro）在一致性测试中也仅达到42.8%，证明了“非注意盲视”在LLM中普遍存在；PRCP方法能有效改善模型对这些被忽略的因果关系的补全，进而提升推理能力。

Conclusion: 大型语言模型在处理隐含信息时存在普遍的“非注意盲视”现象。这一局限性表明，目前的模型在处理复杂推理任务时，往往过度依赖显式指令而忽略了关键的隐性语境。未来研究需要关注如何提升模型在认知层面的对齐能力，使其能像人类一样捕捉并整合细微的语境线索。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly integrated into high-stakes decision-making. Inspired by the theory of \emph{inattentional blindness} in human cognition, we investigate whether LLMs, trained on human-preferred corpora that embed attentional biases, exhibit a similar limitation: \emph{failing to attend to subtle yet important contextual cues under explicit task instructions}. To evaluate this, we introduce the task of \textbf{explicit-implicit reasoning} and present \textbf{MixRea}, a benchmark of 2,246 multiple-choice questions across 9 reasoning types with varying distributions of explicit and implicit information. Evaluation of 21 advanced LLMs shows that even the best-performing reasoning model (Gemini 2.5 Pro) achieves only 42.8\% consistency, revealing widespread inattentional blindness. To mitigate this, we propose \textbf{Potential Relation Completion Prompting (PRCP)}, a prompting method that improves reasoning by recovering overlooked causal relations. Further analysis shows that this limitation persists across diverse multi-source reasoning tasks, highlighting the need for more cognitively aligned models.

### [53] [Less Back-and-Forth: A Comparative Study of Structured Prompting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20149)
*Saurav Ghosh,Gabriella Polach,Abdou Sow*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究表明，为大模型任务提供“核对清单（Checklist）”式的结构化提示，比直接提问或让模型进行澄清提问能更有效地提升回答质量，同时减少交互中的资源消耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于大语言模型在面对不明确的提示词时往往会产生低质量的回答，导致用户需要进行多次额外的交互，研究旨在探讨通过结构化的提示词设计是否能有效提升回答质量并降低用户的使用成本。

Method: 研究对比了三种提示策略（原始提示、核对清单优化提示、澄清性提问提示）在四类任务（摘要、规划、解释、编程）中的表现。通过在 ChatGPT、Claude 和 Grok 三个模型上进行测试，并使用包含任务完成度、准确性、合规性和清晰度的统一评分标准进行量化评估。

Result: 核对清单优化提示在评估中表现最优，平均得分为 7.50（满分 8 分），优于原始提示（5.67 分）和澄清性提问提示（6.67 分）。此外，核对清单提示在质量与努力的权衡中表现最佳，其生成的平均 Token 数量最少。

Conclusion: 简单的提示词核对清单（Checklist）是一种高效的结构化提示策略，能够在提升大模型输出质量的同时，显著减少用户与模型的交互负担，是优化开放式任务提示词的有效方法。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are widely used for open-ended tasks, but underspecified prompts can lead to low-quality answers and additional interaction. This paper studies whether structured prompt design improves response quality while reducing user effort. We compare three prompt conditions: a raw prompt, a checklist-improved prompt, and a clarifying-question prompt. We evaluate these conditions across four task types--summarization, planning, explanation, and coding--using three LLM systems: ChatGPT, Claude, and Grok. Each output is scored with a unified rubric covering task completion, correctness, compliance, and clarity. Checklist-improved prompts achieved the highest mean rubric score, 7.50 out of 8, compared with 5.67 for raw prompts and 6.67 for clarifying-question prompts. Checklist prompts also produced the best quality-effort tradeoff, using fewer average tokens than both raw and clarifying prompts. These results suggest that a simple prompt checklist can improve LLM responses while reducing unnecessary interaction.

### [54] [From Seeing to Thinking: Decoupling Perception and Reasoning Improves Post-Training of Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20177)
*Juncheng Wu,Hardy Chen,Haoqin Tu,Xianfeng Tang,Freda Shi,Hui Liu,Hanqing Lu,Cihang Xie,Yuyin Zhou*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对视觉语言模型（VLM）瓶颈的研究发现，感知不足比推理不足更限制性能。本文提出一种将感知与推理能力解耦的阶段性训练方法，通过强化学习强化视觉感知，在显著提升模型推理准确性的同时缩短了推理路径，实现了更高效的视觉智能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前视觉语言模型（VLM）虽强调长链式思维（CoT）推理，但研究发现其性能的主要限制并非推理本身，而是视觉感知能力的匮乏。研究旨在探讨如何通过训练策略的改进，有效提升模型的感知能力，并分析其与推理能力之间的相互作用。

Method: 1. 能力解耦：将模型的训练划分为视觉感知、视觉推理和文本推理三个独立阶段。
2. 阶段性训练：先进行专项视觉感知训练，再进行视觉推理优化。
3. 强化学习应用：在视觉感知阶段采用强化学习进行定向优化，而非传统的指令微调（SFT）。
4. 课程学习策略：引入基于能力的训练维度，并与传统的难度维度相结合，构建多维度课程学习方案。

Result: 1. 性能提升：在多个视觉数学与感知任务中，通过阶段性训练的 VLM 表现显著优于基线模型（如 WeMath 提升 5.2%，RealWorldQA 提升 3.7%）。
2. 推理效率：推理准确率提升 1.5% 的同时，推理序列长度缩短了 20.8%，证明了更强的感知能力能减少对冗余推理的需求。
3. 方法论证：证实了基于能力的阶段性训练显著优于传统的混合训练（merged training）。

Conclusion: 视觉感知能力是视觉语言模型（VLM）的核心瓶颈。通过将感知与推理能力进行解耦，并采用基于能力的阶段性训练策略（先夯实感知，再优化推理），可以显著提升模型在视觉推理任务中的表现。此外，通过强化学习（RL）优化感知比单纯的监督微调（SFT）更有效。这种基于能力的课程学习范式与传统的难度课程学习具有正交性，二者结合可产生协同增效作用。

Abstract: Recent advances in vision-language models (VLMs) emphasize long chain-of-thought reasoning; yet, we find that their performance on visual tasks is primarily limited by a lack of visual perception as opposed to reasoning itself. In this work, we systematically study the interplay between perception and reasoning in VLM post-training by decomposing their capabilities into three separate training stages: visual perception, visual reasoning, and textual reasoning, incorporating specialized training data. We demonstrate that visual perception (a) requires targeted optimization with specialized data; (b) serves as a fundamental scaffold that should be solidified through staged training before refining visual reasoning; and (c) is more effectively learned via RL than caption-based SFT. Our experiments across multiple VLMs demonstrate that staged training consistently improves both visual perception and reasoning performance over merged training. Notably, models trained with our approach achieve 1.5% higher reasoning accuracy with 20.8% shorter reasoning traces, suggesting that superior perception reduces the need for excessive reasoning. Furthermore, we show that this capability-based staging represents a new curriculum dimension orthogonal to traditional difficulty-based curricula, and combining both yields further additive gains. Our staged-training models achieve superior performance among open-weight VLMs, establishing advanced results on several visual math and perception (e.g., +5.2% on WeMath and +3.7% on RealWorldQA) tasks compared with the base counterpart.

</details>


### [55] [TIDE: Efficient and Lossless MoE Diffusion LLM Inference with I/O-aware Expert Offload](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20179)
*Zhiben Chen,Youpeng Zhao,Yang Sui,Jun Wang,Yuzhang Shang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: TIDE 是一个针对混合专家架构扩散大模型（dLLM）的无损推理优化系统，通过利用专家激活的时间稳定性，以数学规划求解最优专家刷新间隔，在无需模型训练的情况下实现了显著的吞吐量提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管扩散大模型（dLLM）在并行解码方面优于自回归模型，但当其规模扩大并采用混合专家（MoE）架构时，在资源受限设备上的部署面临严重的 I/O 开销和计算瓶颈。现有的自回归压缩方法难以直接适用，因此需要一种针对 dLLM 特性的高效推理方案。

Method: 提出了一种名为 TIDE 的推理系统，核心是利用扩散过程中块内专家激活的时间稳定性。具体包含：1. 引入基于区间的专家刷新策略（interval-based expert refresh strategy），以 I/O 感知的方式更新专家布局；2. 将推理调度建模为数学规划问题，通过求解最优刷新间隔以最小化 I/O 流量和 CPU 计算开销。该方法是无损的且无需重新训练模型。

Result: 在单 GPU-CPU 系统上，TIDE 在 LLaDA2.0-mini 和 LLaDA2.0-flash 模型上分别实现了高达 1.4 倍和 1.5 倍的吞吐量提升。

Conclusion: TIDE 证明了利用专家激活在扩散过程中的时间稳定性，能够有效地为基于 MoE 架构的扩散大模型（dLLM）提供一种无需训练的“免费”加速方案，显著降低了资源受限设备上的推理开销。

Abstract: Diffusion Large Language Models (dLLMs) have emerged as a competitive alternative to autoregressive (AR) models, offering better hardware utilization and bidirectional context through parallel block-level decoding. However, as dLLMs continue to scale up with mixture-of-experts (MoE) architectures, their deployment on resource-constrained devices remains an open challenge. Existing AR-based methods often incur either prohibitive I/O overhead or significant compute bottlenecks. In this work, we propose TIDE, a novel resource-efficient inference system that leverages the temporal stability of expert activations during the diffusion process within the block. Specifically, we leverage the temporal stability of expert activations during the diffusion process within the block and introduce an interval-based expert refresh strategy that updates the expert placement in an I/O-aware fashion. To ensure optimal performance, we formulate the inference scheduling as a mathematical programming problem, solving for the optimal interval that minimizes I/O traffic and CPU computation. Most importantly, TIDE is a lossless optimization that requires no model training, providing a "free lunch" acceleration for dLLM inference. In a single GPU-CPU system, we demonstrate that TIDE achieves up to 1.4$\times$ and 1.5$\times$ throughput improvements over prior baselines on LLaDA2.0-mini and LLaDA2.0-flash models, respectively.

</details>

### [56] [Dimensional Balance Improves Large Scale Spatiotemporal Prediction Performance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18793)
*Jing Chen,Shixiang Pan,Yujie Fan,Haocheng Ye,Haitao Xu,Wenqiang Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对时空预测中复杂度不匹配导致的性能瓶颈，本文提出一种基于熵诊断的自适应框架（ST-Balance），通过低秩空间嵌入与长时序建模，有效提高了预测精度与跨领域通用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在处理复杂时空模式分析时存在性能瓶颈，且跨领域迁移能力有限。研究者发现，这是由于模型在处理时空特征时的复杂度不匹配导致的，且在有限模型容量下，这种不匹配会显著增加预测不确定性。

Method: 提出了一种可扩展的自适应框架，主要包含两个关键模块：一是利用低秩矩阵嵌入技术进行空间维度压缩，以保留核心结构信息；二是扩展时间视野以捕获长距离依赖，并缓解时间异质性引发的累积误差。此外，引入时空熵作为诊断指标，评估并调节时空表示的匹配度。

Result: 通过在城市交通、气象和流行病数据集上的广泛实验，结果表明该框架在预测准确性方面实现了显著提升，且在不同领域间展现出良好的泛化性能。

Conclusion: 本文提出的ST-Balance框架通过解决时空复杂度不匹配问题，有效提升了复杂时空数据预测的精度与泛化能力。实验证明，该方法在城市交通、气象及流行病监测等多个领域均表现出卓越的通用性和性能优势。

Abstract: Accurate spatiotemporal pattern analysis is critical in fields such as urban traffic, meteorology, and public health monitoring. However, existing methods face performance bottlenecks, typically yielding only incremental gains and often exhibiting limited cross-domain transferability. We analyze this bottleneck through spatial and temporal entropy measures, which are used as diagnostic indicators of spatiotemporal complexity mismatch rather than as guarantees that entropy alignment alone yields better forecasting. Empirically, larger mismatch is often accompanied by higher prediction uncertainty, especially under a fixed model-capacity budget. Guided by this diagnostic, we propose a scalable, adaptive framework that harmonizes spatial and temporal feature representations. Spatial dimensionality is compressed via low-rank matrix embedding to preserve essential structure, while an extended temporal horizon captures long-range dependencies and mitigates cumulative errors arising from temporal heterogeneity. Extensive experiments on urban traffic, meteorological, and epidemic datasets demonstrate substantial accuracy gains and broad applicability across the evaluated domains, suggesting that the framework is promising for a wide range of spatiotemporal tasks beyond the current study. The code is available on GitHub at https://github.com/ST-Balance/ST-Balance.

</details>


### [57] [Simply Stabilizing the Loop via Fully Looped Transformer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18797)
*Rao Fu,Zixuan Yang,Jiankun Zhang,Jing Ma,Hechang Chen,Yu Li,Yi Chang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对循环 Transformer 训练不稳定的问题，提出了一种名为 Fully Looped Transformer 的改进方案，通过全循环架构和注意力注入技术，在不增加参数量的基础上显著提升了模型的训练稳定性与下游任务性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的模型扩展依赖增加参数量，而循环 Transformer（Looped Transformer）通过重复使用模块在不增加参数的情况下提升性能，但其在增加迭代次数时存在严重的训练不稳定性（梯度振荡和残差爆炸）。研究旨在解决这一不稳定性并提升模型性能。

Method: 提出了 Fully Looped Transformer，引入了两项无需额外参数的改进：1. 全循环架构（Fully Looped Architecture），将循环间的信号分散到所有层以缓解残差爆炸；2. 注意力注入（Attention Injection），通过复用现有的注意力模块来抑制梯度振荡。

Result: Fully Looped Transformer 实现了多达 12 次迭代的稳定训练（基准模型在此规模下会崩溃），并在较温和的设置下将下游任务平均性能提升了 13.2%。此外，模型在推理阶段通过调整循环次数展现了良好的计算适应性。

Conclusion: Fully Looped Transformer 成功解决了循环 Transformer 架构在增加迭代次数时的训练不稳定性问题，通过无需额外参数的架构改进，实现了更优的性能与训练稳定性，并为按需分配推理算力提供了灵活的解决方案。

Abstract: Scaling model performance typically requires increasing model size. Looped Transformer offers a compelling alternative by iteratively reusing the same Transformer blocks, trading additional computation for improved performance without increasing parameter count or context length. Because the number of loop iterations can be adjusted at inference, it also provides a natural mechanism for balancing performance and test-time compute. However, Looped Transformer still suffers from training instability when the number of loop iterations increases. Our analysis reveals that this instability stems from two sources: gradient oscillation and residual explosion. To address these two problems, we propose the Fully Looped Transformer, which introduces two parameter-free modifications: (1) Fully Looped Architecture, which distributes inter-loop signals across all layers to mitigate residual explosion; (2) Attention Injection, which reuses the existing attention block to suppress gradient oscillation. These modifications stabilize training dynamics, enabling the Fully Looped Transformer to be trained stably up to 12 loop iterations, whereas other baseline looped models collapse in this regime. In milder settings where Looped Transformer does not collapse, Fully Looped Transformer still improves average downstream-task performance by up to 13.2\%. Overall, our experiments demonstrate that Fully Looped Transformer improves training stability, enhances downstream performance, and provides preliminary adaptability under different test-time compute budgets by varying loop iterations at inference.

</details>


### [58] [Accurate Evaluation of Quickest Changepoint Detectors via Non-parametric Survival Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18798)
*Taiki Miyagawa,Akinori F. Ebihara*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于生存分析思想的非参数估计方法，解决了快速变点检测中因数据序列有限或不规则而导致ARL和ADD指标难以应用的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的快速变点检测（QCD）指标（ARL和ADD）在理论研究中表现良好，但由于现实世界数据通常具有序列长度有限且分布不规则的特点，导致这些指标难以直接应用。

Method: 借鉴生存分析（Survival Analysis）中的Kaplan-Meier估计思想，针对序列截断问题建模检测概率，并推导出估计偏差界，证明了在无需外推情况下的渐近无偏性。

Result: 实验表明，KM-ARL和KM-ADD在处理有限和不规则序列长度时表现出更强的稳健性，提升了模型评估的可解释性，并为实证模型选择提供了有效的指导。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的KM-ARL和KM-ADD估计量成功弥合了理论QCD指标与现实中有限、不规则数据集之间的鸿沟，为快速变点检测提供了更稳健、可解释的实证评估工具。

Abstract: We propose non-parametric estimators for the average run length (ARL) and average detection delay (ADD) in quickest changepoint detection (QCD) under finite and irregular sequence lengths. Although ARL and ADD are widely used as optimality criteria in theoretical and simulation studies, their application to real-world datasets is hindered by limited and irregular sequence lengths. To address this issue, we propose non-parametric estimators for the ARL and ADD, termed KM-ARL and KM-ADD, by drawing an analogy between QCD and survival analysis to model detection probabilities under sequence truncation. We derive estimation bias bounds and prove that they are asymptotically unbiased unless extrapolation is required. Experiments on simulated and real-world datasets demonstrate their practical utility, enhancing robustness against limited and irregular sequence lengths, improving interpretability, and facilitating empirical, intuitive model selection. Our Python code is provided at https://github.com/TaikiMiyagawa/Kaplan-Meier-Average-Run-Length, offering ready-to-use implementations for practitioners.

</details>


### [59] [ReCrit: Transition-Aware Reinforcement Learning for Scientific Critic Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18799)
*Wanghan Xu,Yuhao Zhou,Hengyuan Zhao,Shuo Li,Dianzhi Yu,Zhenfei Yin,Yaowen Hu,Fengli Xu,Wanli Ouyang,Wenlong Zhang,Lei Bai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大模型在科学推理中因盲目听从用户误导批评而导致回答变错的问题，本文提出了ReCrit框架。该方法通过将交互过程拆解为四类行为并施加差异化奖励，成功引导模型在保持纠错能力的同时抵御谄媚，显著提升了模型在多轮交互中的科学推理准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在面对用户批评时，常出现“过度服从”问题，即使最初的答案是正确的，也会受用户误导而改为错误答案，这在科学推理任务中具有极高风险。现有方法多关注最终答案准确性，忽略了多轮交互中的逻辑转换过程。

Method: 1. 将交互过程建模为“初始到批评行为”的四个象限：纠错（Correction）、谄媚（Sycophancy）、稳健（Robustness）和边界（Boundary）。
2. 提出ReCrit框架，通过强化学习针对性地奖励纠错与稳健行为，惩罚谄媚行为。
3. 引入动态异步部署（Dynamic Asynchronous Rollout）与尾部自适应补全技术，以降低交互训练的计算延迟和等待时间。

Result: 在ChemBench、TRQA和EarthSE三个科学推理基准测试中，ReCrit显著提升了模型在批评交互后的准确率：Qwen3.5-4B从38.15提升至51.49，Qwen3.5-9B从45.40提升至55.59。消融实验证实，基于转换意识的奖励信号比传统的最终答案奖励更能显著改善模型的批评交互质量。

Conclusion: 本文的研究表明，将批评互动建模为“转折状态转换问题”而非单纯的最终答案准确性问题，是提升大模型科学推理能力的关键。通过ReCrit框架明确区分纠错与谄媚行为，能有效增强模型的稳健性。实验证明，基于转换意识的强化学习奖励机制比传统的最终答案奖励更具指导意义，为大模型在多轮交互中的科学推理训练提供了有效方案。

Abstract: Large language models can fail in critic interaction not only by answering incorrectly, but also by abandoning an initially correct scientific solution after user criticism. This is especially risky in scientific reasoning, where user criticism can turn a valid answer into an incorrect one. We frame critic interaction as an inter-turn correctness-transition problem rather than a final-answer accuracy problem, and identify three challenges: transition awareness, decoupling useful correction from harmful sycophancy, and scalable rollout. We propose ReCrit, a transition-aware reinforcement learning framework that decomposes Initial-to-Critic behavior into four quadrants: Correction, Sycophancy, Robustness, and Boundary. ReCrit rewards correction and robustness, penalizes sycophancy, and treats persistent errors as weak boundary signals. To make interaction training practical, ReCrit further uses dynamic asynchronous rollout with tail-adaptive completion to reduce rollout waiting. On three scientific reasoning benchmarks, ChemBench, TRQA, and EarthSE, ReCrit improves average Critic accuracy from 38.15 to 51.49 on Qwen3.5-4B and from 45.40 to 55.59 on Qwen3.5-9B. Ablations show that final-answer rewards provide little interaction-level gain, while transition-aware rewards and quadrant weighting produce more distinguishable training signals and larger net Critic-stage improvement. The code is available at https://github.com/black-yt/ReCrit .

</details>


### [60] [Theory-optimal Quantization Based on Flatness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18800)
*Xiusheng Huang,Zhe Li,Xuanwu Yin,Lu Wang,Yequan Wang,Dong Li,Emad Barsoum,Kang Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大模型量化中激活异常值导致的精度损失，本文提出了双向对角量化（BDQ）方法，通过优化对角矩阵变换分散异常值，显著提升了极低比特量化下的模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的量化方法通过线性变换处理大模型中的激活异常值时，仍存在异常值模式持续存在且幅度分布集中的问题，导致低比特量化（如 W4A4 或更低）时性能大幅下降。

Method: 提出了一种名为“平坦度”（Flatness）的新指标来量化异常值分布，通过数学建模推导出优化平坦度的理论最优解，并据此设计了双向对角量化（BDQ）框架，通过学习到的对角运算将异常值幅度分布到矩阵的不同维度中。

Result: 实验表明，BDQ 设定了新的量化基准。在 LLaMA-3-8B 模型的 W4A4 量化中，精度下降不到 1%；在更具挑战性的 W2A4KV16 设置下，BDQ 在 DeepSeek-R1-Distill-LLaMA-70B 模型上将性能差距缩小了 39.1%。

Conclusion: BDQ 通过优化的对角矩阵变换有效地分散了异常值，解决了大模型在低比特量化中因异常值导致的性能下降问题，为大模型量化提供了一种高效且稳健的新方案。

Abstract: Post-training quantization has emerged as a widely adopted technique for compressing and accelerating the inference of Large Language Models (LLMs). The primary challenges in LLMs quantization stem from activation outliers, which significantly degrade model performance especially at lower bit precision. While recent approaches attempt to mitigate outliers through linear transformations across feature dimensions, our analysis reveals that the transformed weights and activations still exhibit persistent outlier patterns with concentrated magnitude distributions. In this paper, we first model the mathematical relationship between quantization error and outliers, and then introduce a new metric Flatness to quantify the distribution of outliers. Based on this, we derive the theoretical optimal solution with respect to Flatness. Building on these insights, we propose Bidirectional Diagonal Quantization (BDQ), a novel post-training quantization framework that effectively disperses outlier patterns through optimized matrix transformations. BDQ strategically distributes outlier magnitudes across matrix dimensions via learned diagonal operations. Extensive experiments demonstrate that BDQ establishes a new quantization benchmark. It achieves less than 1\% accuracy drop in W4A4 quantization on the LLaMA-3-8B model. In the more challenging W2A4KV16 experiment, compared to state-of-the-art approaches, BDQ reduces the performance gap by 39.1\% on the DeepSeek-R1-Distill-LLaMA-70B model.

</details>


### [61] [PROWL: Prioritized Regret-Driven Optimization for World Model Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18803)
*Ahmet H. Güzel,Jenny Seidenschwarz,Benjamin Graham,Jonathan Sadeghi,Jeffrey Hawke,Jack Parker-Holder,Ilija Bogunovic*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了PROWL框架，通过对抗性训练和优先轨迹缓存策略，主动发现并修复视频世界模型在关键交互场景下的预测失败，从而显著提升了模型在分布外场景下的鲁棒性和可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代视频世界模型在处理稀有的、对交互至关重要的场景时表现不可靠。由于被动演示数据中这些高影响场景样本不足，通过被动学习难以提升模型的鲁棒性，因此需要一种能够主动诱发模型失败并进行针对性训练的方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为PROWL的框架，包含两个核心组件：1. KL约束的对抗性课程：训练一个策略来暴露世界模型的高误差轨迹，同时保持在分布范围内；2. 优先对抗轨迹（PAT）缓存：根据预测误差、动作保真度和学习进度对轨迹进行重新排序，确保模型专注于尚未解决的故障模式。

Result: 在MineRL框架下的实验表明，PROWL在处理未见过的分布外轨迹时表现出更强的鲁棒性；该方法能够有效揭示弱行为约束下的奖励作弊行为，并证明了其在生成高质量训练数据方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，通过主动、有针对性地生成信息量大的训练数据，而非仅依赖被动数据集，可以显著提升动作条件视频世界模型的鲁棒性。研究强调了在对抗性失败探索与行为正则化之间取得平衡，对于训练高性能世界模型至关重要。

Abstract: Modern action-conditioned video world models achieve strong short-horizon visual realism, yet remain unreliable on rare, interaction-critical transitions that dominate downstream planning and policy performance. Because passive demonstration data systematically under-samples these high-impact regimes, improving robustness requires actively eliciting model failures rather than relying on their natural occurrence. We introduce a KL-constrained adversarial curriculum in which a policy is trained to expose high-error trajectories of a diffusion-based world model while remaining close to the behavior distribution. The world model is continuously fine-tuned on these adversarially discovered trajectories, yielding an adversarial training loop that converts rare failures into a stable, near-distribution training signal without drifting into out-of-distribution exploitation. To maintain pressure on unresolved weaknesses as the model improves, we propose a Prioritized Adversarial Trajectory (PAT) buffer that re-ranks trajectories based on prediction error, action fidelity, and learning progress, focusing training on unresolved failure modes rather than repeatedly revisiting solved cases. We implement our approach in the MineRL framework and evaluate it on held-out out-of-distribution trajectories; PROWL improves robustness over models trained on passive data alone, reveals reward-hacking behaviors under weak behavioral constraints, and demonstrates that effective adversarial world-model training critically depends on balancing exploratory failure discovery with explicit behavioral regularization. Our results suggest that scalable world models benefit not only from larger datasets, but also from selectively generating informative training data.

</details>


### [62] [Block-Based Double Decoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18807)
*Asher Labovich,Benjamin Bradley,Vanessa Alexander,Chaitanya Harsha*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新型的“块状双解码器”架构，通过特殊的注意力掩码机制，使模型既能像纯解码器模型一样高效训练，又能像编码器-解码器模型一样实现低成本推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的编码器-解码器模型虽具有推理优势，但因预训练目标稀疏且序列长度动态，难以在大规模场景下实施；而纯解码器模型训练效率高但推理成本大，本文旨在结合两者的优势。

Method: 提出了一种基于“块状双解码器”（Block-based Double Decoders）的Transformer架构，引入了“双重因果块状注意力掩码”（doubly-causal block-based attention masks），以支持全损失监督训练和静态序列填充。

Result: 实验表明，在缩放定律（scaling law）测试中，该架构的表现优于传统编码器-解码器模型，并紧追纯解码器模型；在推理阶段，该模型在不牺牲现有缓存优化的情况下，将KV缓存内存和单位令牌计算量降低了至少三分之二。

Conclusion: 本文提出的“块状双解码器”架构有效弥合了编码器-解码器模型（推理高效）与纯解码器模型（训练高效）之间的鸿沟，为大规模预训练提供了一种兼具两者优势的实用替代方案。

Abstract: Encoder-decoder models offer substantial inference-time savings over decoder-only models, but their pretraining objectives suffer from sparse supervision and dynamic sequence lengths, keeping them out of practice at scale. We propose block-based double decoders, a novel transformer architecture that utilizes doubly-causal block-based attention masks to train with full loss supervision and static sequence packing, combining decoder-only training efficiency with encoder-decoder inference efficiency. In scaling law experiments, block-based double decoders strongly outperform encoder-decoders and closely track decoder-only models across scales. At inference time, they cut KV-cache memory and per-token compute by at least 2/3 without sacrificing prefill caching or other existing inference optimizations available to decoder-only models.

### [63] [Compositional Literary Primitives in Instruction-Tuned LLMs: Cross-Architectural SAE Features for Self, Style, and Affect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18808)
*Joao Paulo Cavalcante Presa,Savio Salvarino Teles de Oliveira*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过稀疏自编码器解析了Llama 3.1和Gemma 2内部的文学表达原语，证明了模型可以通过组合特定的情感、风格和视角特征来精确控制叙事，揭示了模型在“直接命名”与“间接唤起”情感模式上的架构差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探索大语言模型（LLM）内部表征的结构化特征，特别是模型如何通过组合不同的“文学原语”来生成特定情感、风格和叙事视角，从而实现对模型内部“黑盒”中生成文学作品能力的机制性理解与精准控制。

Method: 采用了三阶段验证流程：1. 利用稀疏自编码器（SAE）提取模型中间层残差流中的特征；2. 通过Logit-lens技术分析特征作用；3. 建立“5-LLM评委团”机制，在27类情感分类（Cowen-Keltner）下对生成文本进行严格的强制选择评估，以验证特征的可解释性与组合能力。

Result: 研究在Llama 3.1 8B和Gemma 2 9B模型中识别出四类核心特征：命名门控、第一人称自我指涉簇、风格调节器及组合情感特征。实验显示Llama实现了27/27的情感全覆盖，Gemma实现23/27；同时发现模型内部存在身份标记与情感表达的双重特征，且Llama倾向于直接命名情感，而Gemma更倾向于通过场景描写唤起情感。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了LLM内部存在一套关于文学表达的组合式语义原语，这些原语不仅能精确调控模型的情感输出，还揭示了模型风格（如“展示而非陈述”）与身份角色（Helper-AI）之间的深层关联。研究证明了通过稀疏自编码器解析模型内部表征的可行性与有效性，并为理解大模型如何构建复杂文学叙事提供了机制解释。

Abstract: We characterize a compositional architecture of literary primitives in two instruction-tuned large language models (Llama 3.1 8B-Instruct and Gemma 2 9B-IT) via sparse autoencoders on mid-depth residual streams. Four feature classes emerge: naming-gates that promote lexical tokens of a target affect, an eleven-self cluster of first-person register features, stylistic register modulators (show-don't-tell and defamiliarization), and compositional emotions that arise only from multi-feature steering. Under a forced-choice 5-LLM judge panel applied to a 27-category emotion taxonomy (Cowen-Keltner), Llama reaches full 27/27 coverage by combining naming-gates, multi-feature recipes, and single self-feature steering; Gemma reaches 23/27 with adoration as the single residual strict-fail. Under random judging, the per-cell pass probability is on the order of $10^{-3}$ and the expected number of two-seed false-positive cells across the catalog is negligible, so the observed coverage is not consistent with chance. A cross-architectural asymmetry sits in the strict-versus-soft judge contrast: on the same generations, judges agree more often on Llama outputs than on Gemma outputs because Llama outputs name the target affect more directly while Gemma outputs evoke it through scene and imagery. Both architectures contain self-features that serve simultaneously as register markers and as emotion emitters, including a single most-RLHF-loaded self-feature per architecture that intensifies the institutional Helper-AI persona at one operating regime and produces affect-categorizable output at the same calibrated coefficient. Methodologically, the paper presents a three-stage validation pipeline (logit-lens, LLM-rate, 5-LLM judge) with documented anti-patterns; the total compute is single-GPU and about 15 minutes per emotion-feature discovery cycle.

### [64] [PASC: Pipeline-Aware Conformal Prediction with Joint Coverage Guarantees for Multi-Stage NLP and LLM Pipelines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18812)
*Varun Kotte*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 PASC，这是一种用于多阶段 AI 流水线的不确定性量化新方法。它通过将联合覆盖问题简化为单标量共形预测，在保证严格的统计覆盖前提下，显著优于传统方法，并能有效应对多阶段流水线中的错误累积与分布偏移问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代 NLP 和 LLM 系统通常采用多阶段流水线（如 NER -> NED -> 实体类型化），错误会在各阶段间累积。现有的不确定性量化方法要么无法保证流水线整体的联合覆盖（独立校准），要么过于保守（使用 Bonferroni 界导致性能下降）。作者旨在寻找一种既能保证多阶段联合覆盖，又不会过度牺牲预测精度的通用解决方案。

Method: 本文提出了 PASC（Pipeline-Aware Split Conformal）方法。其核心思想是将多阶段流水线的联合覆盖要求转化为针对“联合最大非一致性得分”（joint maximum nonconformity score）的单一标量共形预测问题。这种方法无需对每个阶段进行独立校准，也不依赖保守的 Bonferroni 联合界，从而在实现有限样本、无分布假设的覆盖保证的同时，保持了预测集的紧致性。

Result: 在三阶段实体识别流水线实验中，PASC 实现了 96.4% 的端到端覆盖率，远超 Bonferroni（93.4%）和独立 CP（86.5%），且预测集大小几乎一致。在分布偏移测试中，PASC 依然能保持目标覆盖率，而独立 CP 表现大幅下降。此外，PASC 计算速度比 Bonferroni 快 1.7 倍，且能良好扩展至更长（K=6）的流水线任务。

Conclusion: PASC 是一种高效且具备统计保证的框架，能够解决多阶段 NLP 及 LLM 流水线中的联合不确定性量化问题。它通过将复杂的联合覆盖问题简化为单一标量的共形预测问题，在保持极高计算效率的同时，显著提升了端到端的覆盖鲁棒性，是构建可靠 AI 流水线的关键技术。

Abstract: Modern NLP and LLM systems are pipelines: named entity recognition (NER) -> entity disambiguation (NED) -> entity typing, retrieval-augmented generation (retriever -> reader), and agentic chains of planner -> tool -> critic. Errors compound across stages, but existing uncertainty quantification methods either calibrate each stage independently (no joint coverage) or apply a Bonferroni union bound (joint coverage, but conservative). We present PASC (Pipeline-Aware Split Conformal), which reduces multi-stage joint coverage to a single scalar conformal prediction problem on the joint maximum nonconformity score. PASC provides a finite-sample distribution-free guarantee that all K stages are simultaneously covered with probability at least 1 - alpha, and is nearly tight up to a 1/(n+1) factor. On a three-stage NER -> NED -> entity-typing pipeline over CoNLL-2003, PASC achieves 96.4% end-to-end coverage versus 93.4% for Bonferroni and 86.5% for independent CP, at identical average prediction set size (1.083). Under distribution shift to WNUT-17 Twitter and WikiNEuRal Wikipedia data, PASC empirically maintains the target coverage in the tested shift settings while independent CP collapses to 59%. PASC requires a single quantile computation, runs 1.7x faster than Bonferroni, and scales to K = 6 stages where independent CP drops to 0.53 end-to-end coverage. The same joint-maximum-score reduction applies directly to compound LLM systems and agent pipelines.

</details>


### [65] [Composition of Memory Experts for Diffusion World Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18813)
*Sebastian Stapf,Pablo Acuaviva Huertos,Aram Davtyan,Paolo Favaro*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 为了解决世界模型中记忆容量与计算效率的权衡问题，本文提出了一种基于扩散模型的专家组合框架，通过整合短期、长期及空间记忆专家，实现了在长序列预测中既保留高保真细节又能保持高效计算的目标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的世界模型架构在记忆上存在本质权衡：Transformer在保持局部细节方面表现优秀但计算成本高（二次方复杂度），而循环模型或状态空间模型虽扩展性好但会损失历史信息保真度。论文旨在解决如何在保证长序列上下文的同时，维持高保真的未来预测。

Method: 提出了一种基于扩散模型的框架，通过对比式“专家组合”（Contrastive Product-of-Experts）将异构记忆模型整合。具体包括三个互补专家：1. 短期记忆专家（捕捉局部动态细节）；2. 长期记忆专家（通过轻量级测试时微调，将情景历史存储在扩散权重中）；3. 空间长期记忆专家（强制保持几何与空间连贯性）。

Result: 在模拟和真实世界基准测试中，该方法显著提升了时间一致性、对过去观测结果的召回能力以及导航任务的性能，且避免了模式坍塌，实现了在不产生二次方计算成本的前提下扩展至长上下文。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种基于专家组合（Product-of-Experts）的记忆增强扩散世界模型，通过解耦不同时间尺度的记忆需求，成功克服了传统架构在保持长短期记忆细节与计算效率之间的权衡，为构建高效、鲁棒的世界模型提供了新的范式。

Abstract: World models aim to predict plausible futures consistent with past observations, a capability central to planning and decision-making in reinforcement learning. Yet, existing architectures face a fundamental memory trade-off: transformers preserve local detail but are bottlenecked by quadratic attention, while recurrent and state-space models scale more efficiently but compress history at the cost of fidelity. To overcome this trade-off, we suggest decoupling future-past consistency from any single architecture and instead leveraging a set of specialized experts. We introduce a diffusion-based framework that integrates heterogeneous memory models through a contrastive product-of-experts formulation. Our approach instantiates three complementary roles: a short-term memory expert that captures fine local dynamics, a long-term memory expert that stores episodic history in external diffusion weights via lightweight test-time finetuning, and a spatial long-term memory expert that enforces geometric and spatial coherence. This compositional design avoids mode collapse and scales to long contexts without incurring a quadratic cost. Across simulated and real-world benchmarks, our method improves temporal consistency, recall of past observations, and navigation performance, establishing a novel paradigm for building and operating memory-augmented diffusion world models.

</details>


### [66] [DynaTrain: Fast Online Parallelism Switching for Elastic LLM Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18815)
*Yuanqing Wang,Yuchen Zhang,Hao Lin,Junhao Hu,Chunyang Zhu,Quanlu Zhang,Boxun Li,Guohao Dai,Zhi Yang,Daning Cheng,Yunquan Zhang,Yu Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DynaTrain是一个分布式大模型训练系统，通过引入虚拟参数空间抽象和高效的拓扑切换机制，实现了亚秒级的动态并行配置重构，解决了现有框架难以应对训练资源波动的痛点，且性能优于现有系统三个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代大模型训练环境高度动态（如资源波动、RLHF阶段切换、集群弹性需求），而现有的训练框架多基于静态执行模型，无法灵活应对这些变化，导致重构效率低下。

Method: 1. 提出虚拟参数空间（VPS）抽象：将所有分布式训练状态统一在单一逻辑坐标系下，简化了并行配置间的映射与转换。
2. 状态路由与转换层：实现内存感知且无死锁的秩（rank）级别数据传输。
3. 弹性设备管理器：将新配置拓扑的构建与当前的训练过程重叠（Overlap），以掩盖拓扑变更带来的开销。

Result: 在高达235B参数的密集模型和MoE模型上，DynaTrain实现了极快的重构速度（70B模型小于2秒，235B MoE模型约4.36秒），其性能比现有的基于检查点（checkpoint）的弹性系统快了三个数量级。

Conclusion: DynaTrain 通过引入虚拟参数空间（VPS）成功解决了大规模语言模型训练中动态资源调整的难题，证明了在不牺牲训练正确性的前提下，实现亚秒级、多维度并行配置的在线重构是切实可行的，为动态异构环境下的高效模型训练提供了关键技术路径。

Abstract: Modern large language model (LLM) training is inherently dynamic: resource fluctuations, RLHF phase shifts, and cluster elasticity continually reshape the optimal parallelism layout, posing a significant challenge to existing training frameworks built around a static execution model. We present DynaTrain, a distributed training system for sub-second, online reconfiguration across arbitrary multi-dimensional parallelism. At its core, we propose a Virtual Parameter Space (VPS) abstraction that unifies all distributed training states under one logical coordinate space, turning any parallelism configuration into a deterministic mapping and collapsing complex transition into manageable geometric intersections. On top of VPS, a state routing-and-transition layer executes rank-local transfers under a memory-aware, deadlock-free schedule, and an Elastic Device Manager overlaps new-world construction with ongoing training to mask topology-change cost. On dense and MoE models up to 235B parameters, DynaTrain reconfigures a 70B dense model in under 2s and a 235B MoE model in 4.36s, outperforming state-of-the-art checkpoint-based and elastic systems by up to three orders of magnitude while preserving correctness.

### [67] [Emergence of Frontier Superposition: Möbius attractor and Cascade Supervision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18820)
*Hongyu Gu,Jingwen Fu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了Transformer实现“叠加推理”的内在机制，即通过Möbius吸引子架构与级联监督策略的配合，解决了梯度下降在复杂推理任务中无法收敛到最优状态的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探究Transformer模型能否通过梯度下降自动学习到复杂的“叠加推理”能力（即在固定深度内并行处理推理任务），而非仅仅依赖序列思维链，并解决此前该能力是否能被梯度下降找到的理论空白。

Method: 1. 理论分析：利用动力系统理论，将Transformer在图可达性问题上的层间动态简化为一维Möbius映射，识别出全局最优解流形。
2. 梯度分析：通过数学推导证明端到端监督在深层会导致梯度衰减，并提出“级联监督”策略来解决梯度持久化与选择性引导问题。
3. 实验验证：在Erdős-Rényi图上通过数值实验对比端到端监督与级联监督的效果，验证理论预测的余弦相似度。

Result: 研究发现端到端监督会导致深层梯度衰减，无法到达最优解流形。而采用级联监督后，模型能够克服这一限制，实验测得的推理状态余弦相似度与理论预测值（D=3时，0.69 vs 0.71）吻合，证明了该方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 通过结合Möbius吸引子（架构特性）与级联监督（训练策略），研究揭示了Transformer实现叠加推理的必要条件，并证明了级联监督对于克服梯度消失、实现有效学习的关键作用。实验数据与理论预测高度一致，验证了该机制的有效性。

Abstract: Superposition allows Transformers to reason in depth, carrying an entire reasoning frontier in parallel through a bounded-depth forward pass instead of unrolling serial chain-of-thought tokens. While Zhu et al. (2025) hand-crafted an equal-weight breadth-first frontier in a single residual stream for graph reachability, it remained open whether gradient descent could ever find this target amidst permutation-symmetric saddles.
  We close this gap on Reachability-by-Superposition over Erdős-Rényi graphs by isolating architectural and supervisional contributions. Architecturally, we identify a Möbius attractor: under $S_n$-symmetry in the tree regime, layerwise dynamics reduce to a 1D Möbius map whose zero set is a codimension-one manifold of global optima containing the equal-weight superposition state.
  On the supervision side, we identify Cascade Supervision: a loss class whose backward pass simultaneously delivers (A) selectivity bootstrap, (B) gradient persistence across depth, and (C) per-step discrimination (e.g., \mathcal{L}_{sup} and \mathcal{L}_{node}). End-to-end supervision fails condition (B) and is provably insufficient: internal gradients at layer c decay as (np)^{-(D-c-2)/2} in the graph fan-out and stall before the manifold is reached.
  Our thesis: Möbius attractor + Cascade Supervision = emergence of superposition reasoning. The parameter-free decay law predicts a final-step cosine of 0.35 vs. 0.71 (end-to-end vs. cascade) at depth D=3; experiments confirm 0.37 vs. 0.69, matching within 0.02 at every step.

</details>

### [69] [Hybrid-LoRA: Bridging Full Fine-Tuning and Low-Rank Adaptation for Post-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18822)
*Chengqian Zhang,Wei Zhu,Kyumin Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 Hybrid-LoRA 框架，通过利用新颖的评分机制识别模块敏感度，将全参数微调与 LoRA 相结合，在大幅降低计算成本的同时，有效解决了 PEFT 在复杂推理任务中性能不足的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大语言模型后训练阶段，尽管基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）在推理能力提升上表现卓越，但全参数微调（FFT）成本高昂，而现有的参数高效微调（PEFT）方法如 LoRA 在处理复杂推理任务时往往存在明显的性能损失。本研究旨在寻找一种既能降低计算成本又能保持 FFT 性能的折中方案。

Method: 提出了一种名为“Hybrid-LoRA”的混合后训练框架。该方法引入了“Hybrid-LoRA Score”指标，用于评估模型不同模块对低秩适应的敏感度，进而将全参数微调（FFT）优先应用于最不适合低秩适应的关键模块，其余模块则采用 LoRA 进行微调，从而在有限的预算下最大化模型性能。

Result: 实验结果显示，在仅使用 10% 全参数微调预算的情况下，Hybrid-LoRA 能够紧密匹配 FFT 的性能表现，并稳定优于四种主流的 PEFT 后训练基线，性能平均提升 4.36%，最高可提升 5.65%。

Conclusion: Hybrid-LoRA 框架通过模块敏感度分析，在极低参数预算下实现了逼近全参数微调（FFT）的性能，证明了混合参数高效微调在复杂推理任务后训练中的巨大潜力和实用价值。

Abstract: Post-training has become essential for adapting large language models (LLMs) to complex downstream behaviors, including instruction following, preference alignment, and multi-step reasoning. Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has recently emerged as a particularly effective post-training paradigm for improving reasoning capabilities, with critic-free algorithms such as GRPO and GSPO enabling scalable optimization. However, RLVR post-training with full fine-tuning (FFT) requires substantial GPU memory and incurs high training costs. Although parameter-efficient fine-tuning (PEFT) methods, such as Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA), effectively reduce computational costs, they often suffer from a noticeable performance gap compared to full fine-tuning in post-training for complex reasoning tasks. In this paper, we propose Hybrid-LoRA, an efficient hybrid post-training framework that selectively applies full fine-tuning to a small subset of modules less suited to low-rank adaptation, while adapting the remaining components with LoRA. We introduce a novel Hybrid-LoRA Score to rank candidate modules according to their sensitivity to low-rank adaptation under a fixed parameter budget. Experiments show that Hybrid-LoRA closely matches full fine-tuning performance under a 10% full fine-tuning module budget, with the remaining candidate modules adapted by LoRA, consistently outperforming four state-of-the-art PEFT post-training baselines, achieving improvements of up to 5.65% and on average 4.36% over the best baseline.

</details>


### [70] [Not All Tokens Are Worth Caching: Learning Semantic-Aware Eviction for LLM Prefix Caches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18825)
*Shaoke Fang,Ziang Li,Wenfei Wu,Jiatong Ji,Qingsong Liu,Ruizhi Pu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SAECache通过一种语义感知的自适应缓存驱逐策略，根据Token类型和任务特征动态调整KV块的留存优先级，极大提高了大模型服务的缓存效率与性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM前缀缓存驱逐策略（如LRU）未能区分不同类型Token的复用差异（复用率差异高达756倍），导致昂贵的GPU显存资源利用率低下，限制了服务性能。

Method: 1. 多队列架构：将KV块路由至针对不同任务（如多轮对话、模板化请求）的特定队列，应用差异化的优先级策略；2. 语义感知加权机制：通过驱逐反馈在线学习不同Token类型的复用价值；3. 全自适应在线学习框架：自动更新参数（包括时间参数、位置衰减、队列权重等），消除了人工调优的需求。

Result: 在多种异构负载下，SAECache相比生产环境基准，首字延迟（TTFT）提升了1.4倍至2.7倍；同时，该方法具备极强的自适应能力，避免了固定参数策略在负载失配时可能导致的性能大幅下降（高达2.7倍）。

Conclusion: SAECache通过语义感知和在线学习机制，有效地解决了大模型服务中前缀缓存资源竞争的问题，显著提升了系统在异构负载下的性能与鲁棒性，证明了利用Token类型差异优化缓存策略的必要性。

Abstract: Prefix caching is a key optimization in Large Language Model (LLM) serving, reusing attention Key-Value (KV) states across requests with shared prompt prefixes to reduce expensive prefill computation. However, its benefit depends critically on the eviction policy as GPU memory is scarce, and existing policies such as LRU largely treat cached blocks uniformly. This view ignores a fundamental property of LLM prompts: not all tokens are equally worth caching. We show that different token types within a prompt, including system prompts, user queries, tool outputs, model responses, and chain-of-thought reasoning, exhibit up to 756x variation in reuse rates, yet no existing eviction policy exploits this signal. In this paper, we present SAECache (Semantic-Adaptive Eviction for prefix caches), a semantic-adaptive prefix cache eviction policy that addresses this gap through three innovations: (1) a multi-queue architecture that routes KV blocks to task-specific queues with tailored priority metrics, capturing both session reuse in multi-turn requests and structural reuse in templated single-turn requests; (2) a semantic-aware token weighting mechanism that learns the reuse value of different token types online through eviction feedback; and (3) a fully adaptive online learning schema for all parameter updates, including log-normal timing parameters, position decay power, queue weights, and meta-parameters, which eliminates manual tuning and enables automatic adaptation to deployment-specific workload characteristics. Through extensive evaluation across heterogeneous workloads, we demonstrate that SAECache achieves 1.4x-2.7x TTFT improvement over production-style baselines, while fixed-parameter alternatives can degrade by up to 2.7x under workload mismatch -- a failure mode our adaptive approach avoids entirely.

</details>


### [71] [The Routing and Filtering Structure of Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18826)
*Shafayeth Jamil,Rehan Kapadia*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出将注意力机制拆解为“路由”与“过滤”两个分量，发现路由具有低秩且呈现“谱级联”的特性，并据此设计了 S-D 注意力机制，在保持模型性能的同时大幅降低了计算与参数复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的注意力机制将信息重分配（路由）和相关性缩放（过滤）混合在 QK^T 矩阵中，难以直接优化。作者旨在将两者解耦，以理解注意力头的工作机制，并探索如何利用这种内在结构来简化模型设计、降低参数量。

Method: 1. 提出 S-D 注意力（S-D attention），通过构造将注意力交互矩阵拆解为对称（过滤）和斜对称（路由）分量。2. 利用该参数化方法实现无归一化（unnormalized）的稳定训练。3. 通过对模型层级结构的研究，发现并验证了路由的谱级联特性。4. 实验测试了将部分层替换为线性注意力（ELU+1）的效果。

Result: 1. 路由过程具有低秩特征，远低于现有分配的容量。2. 引入的 S-D 注意力在无需层归一化的情况下保持训练稳定。3. 路由呈现出从底层到高层扩展的“谱级联”现象。4. 基于级联理论，可将前几层注意力线性化，在极小困惑度损失下显著减少参数量（47%-65% 的注意力参数节省）。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了注意力机制中路由（routing）和过滤（filtering）功能的解耦机制，并提出了“谱级联”（spectral cascade）结构。通过这种设计，不仅提升了模型的可解释性，还为在大规模语言模型中通过线性化和参数缩减进行压缩提供了理论依据与实践路径。

Abstract: The attention interaction matrix $QK^{\top}$ contains two entangled computations: a skew-symmetric component that redistributes information between positions (routing) and a symmetric component that scales mutual relevance (filtering). We decompose 1776 heads across five pretrained transformers and find routing operating at low rank, well below the routing capacity allocated by the weight kernel. We introduce $S$-$D$ attention as a diagnostic parameterization that disentangles routing from filtering by construction with guaranteed stability ($\mathrm{Re}(λ) \le 0$) and trains stably without layer normalization. When disentangled and unnormalized, routing self-organizes into a spectral cascade, effective rank $2$ at the first layer, expanding with depth across six scales from 7M to 355M parameters. The cascade predicts where attention can be simplified: linearizing the first seven layers of 125M $S$-$D$ attention costs ${<}5\%$ perplexity, whereas standard attention collapses under the same intervention. The linearizable region widens with depth. Replacing the first four layers with ELU+1 linear attention reaches within $1.4\%$ of baseline at full head dimension. Cascade-allocated architectures trade attention parameters for perplexity ($47\%-65\%$ fewer attention parameters at $+3.9\%$ to $+8.4\%$ PPL). The routing-filtering decomposition makes the spectral budget legible; the cascade makes it actionable.

### [72] [Lossless Anti-Distillation Sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18829)
*Zibo Diao,Jingchu Gai,Xinyue Ai,Zhang Zhang,Zhenyu He,Di He*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出 LADS 防御方案，通过将模型输出与语义内容和请求历史挂钩，使正常用户的体验保持无损，同时强制蒸馏攻击者获取的训练数据产生相关性，从而有效破坏蒸馏模型的效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前的生成模型防蒸馏方案存在缺陷：要么通过修改输出降低模型性能（影响用户体验），要么依靠易被多账号绕过的行为检测。该研究旨在提出一种既能防御多账号蒸馏攻击，又能保持正常用户体验（无损）的新型防护机制。

Method: 提出“无损反蒸馏采样（LADS）”方法。该方法根据查询的语义内容和用户历史请求次数生成私有种子，以此决定模型输出的随机性。对于正常用户，每次查询依然是独立的；而对于通过多账号进行蒸馏的攻击者，语义相近的查询会被强制关联相同的潜在随机性，导致蒸馏数据出现相关性，从而降低其训练数据的多样性和泛化能力。

Result: 实验在图像生成、数学推理和代码生成任务中证明，LADS 能够显著降低蒸馏学生模型的性能；同时，理论分析（利用一致收敛理论）确认 LADS 会降低蒸馏模型在无条件和有条件生成设置下的泛化收敛速率。

Conclusion: LADS 是一种创新的防蒸馏采样方案，它在保障正常用户体验不受影响的前提下，通过引入语义相关的随机性约束，有效破坏了蒸馏模型训练数据的独立同分布（i.i.d.）特性，从而在理论和实验层面显著抑制了模型蒸馏攻击的效果。

Abstract: Frontier commercial generative models face a growing threat from distillation, whereby a distiller harvests generated responses and trains a competing model of its own at drastically lower cost. Existing defenses either rely on modifying the models outputs, thereby sacrificing response quality for benign users, or on behavioral detection methods, which can be readily circumvented by distributing queries across multiple accounts. In this work, we propose Lossless Anti-Distillation Sampling (LADS), a novel sampling scheme specifically designed to counter multi-account distillation while maintaining a lossless experience for benign users. Concretely, LADS derives the randomness underlying each generation from a private seed determined by the semantic content of the query and the number of times the user has queried the model. By construction, every benign user receives a response independently sampled from the original model at each visit, and thus experiences no distortion. In contrast, for a distiller, different accounts share latent randomness whenever their queries fall in the same semantic bucket. As a result, the harvested data becomes correlated, potentially reducing sample diversity and degrading generalization. Using uniform convergence theory, we show that LADS provably degrades the convergence rate of the distillers generalization gap relative to standard i.i.d. sampling in both unconditional and conditional generation settings. Experiments on image generation, mathematical reasoning, and code generation confirm that LADS substantially degrades the performance of distilled students while preserving exact statistical fidelity for individual users.

We surpass conventional practices by integrating diverse representations within the knowledge graph, drawing insights from contextual information from a thorough literature investigation. This integration allows us to develop a comprehensive and context-specific data quality assessment plan tailored to each context. Leveraging the knowledge graph improves our understanding of the input dataset's context, overcoming the limitations of traditional methods that rely solely on strict matching and overlook contextual characteristics. By injecting numerical edge attributes, we assign corresponding weights to each predicted quality measurement, providing a comprehensive data quality assessment plan for the input dataset.

We present SAGE, a novel counterfactual-aware negative harvesting approach that combines SimHash-based stratified sampling with a modular gating ensemble for confident negative identification from unlabeled data. ### [75] [Spectral Gradient Surgery for Domain-Generalizable Dataset Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18836)
*Minyoung Oh,Najeong Chae,Jae-Young Sim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对数据集蒸馏在分布外（OOD）场景下性能下降的问题，本文提出了DGDD框架及“谱梯度手术（SGS）”技术，通过在梯度层面解耦类别特征与域特征，有效提升了合成数据集的泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的数据集蒸馏方法假设训练集与测试集同分布，但在实际应用中该假设常失效。直接结合现有的域泛化（DG）方法因缺乏真实数据集的多样性且计算开销巨大而效果不佳，因此需要专门针对OOD泛化能力进行优化的数据集蒸馏方案。

Method: 提出了面向领域泛化的数据集蒸馏（DGDD）新问题设置，并针对分布匹配（DM）基线方法开发了“谱梯度手术（SGS）”技术。该方法通过在谱域分析跨域梯度的一致性，识别并保留共享的类别判别梯度，抑制领域特定信息，同时引入了促进合成集多样性的增强梯度更新策略。

Result: 实验结果表明，SGS方法显著提升了蒸馏数据集在OOD场景下的泛化性能，且作为一种即插即用的方案，能够无缝兼容现有的分布匹配算法，在保持数据集高效性的同时增强了模型的稳健性。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的SGS方法成功通过谱梯度手术实现了类别判别信息与领域特定信息的解耦，证明了在数据集蒸馏中显式考虑OOD泛化能力是可行且必要的，为构建具有鲁棒性的紧凑数据集提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Dataset Distillation (DD) synthesizes a compact synthetic dataset that preserves the training utility of a full dataset. However, its standard formulation assumes that test data follow the same distribution as training data, an assumption that rarely holds in practice. A straightforward extension-applying post-hoc Domain Generalization (DG) techniques to distilled data-is ill-suited because existing DG methods rely on the natural diversity of real datasets, which compact synthetic sets inherently lack, while also incurring substantial augmentation overhead that conflicts with the efficiency objective of dataset distillation. To address this limitation, we introduce Domain Generalizable Dataset Distillation (DGDD), a new problem setting that explicitly targets out-of-distribution (OOD) generalization of distilled datasets. We study this problem through a widely adopted DD baseline of Distribution Matching (DM). We attribute the OOD vulnerability of DM to the entanglement of class-discriminative and domain-specific information within the compressed synthetic set, and propose Spectral Gradient Surgery (SGS) to disentangle the two. The key insight of SGS is that cross-domain agreement among domain-wise gradients in the spectral domain reveals which gradient components are shared across source domains-and are therefore class-discriminative-and which are domain-specific. Based on this observation, SGS augments the standard DM update with two complementary gradients: one that reinforces cross-domain shared components and another that explicitly promotes diversity within the distilled dataset. Extensive experiments on diverse-scale benchmarks demonstrate that SGS substantially improves OOD generalization while remaining plug-and-play compatible with existing DM methods.

### [76] [Lying Is Just a Phase: The Hidden Alignment Transition in Language Model Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18838)
*Adil Amin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究发现语言模型的推理与真实性能力之间存在一种随规模变化的相变现象：在较小规模下两种能力相互竞争，而在超过临界规模后则相互合作；通过优化数据和架构可以突破这一限制，实现在更小规模下获得更好的协同性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的缩放定律（Scaling Laws）主要关注计算量与损失函数之间的关系，但无法解释模型不同能力（如推理能力与真实性）之间是如何相互影响和交互的。研究旨在探究这些核心能力在不同模型规模和训练条件下如何演化。

Method: 研究人员通过分析来自16个模型家族的63个基础模型，测量了推理与真实性能力之间的耦合关系。利用稀疏回归常微分方程（ODE）模型进行交叉验证和预测，并通过分析注意头行为、宽度归一化以及模型家族的公开基准测试得分，探讨了架构、数据质量和训练配方对能力耦合的影响。

Result: 研究发现能力耦合存在一个临界规模 $N_c$（约为35亿参数）：在 $N_c$ 以下，推理与真实性呈负相关；在 $N_c$ 以上，两者呈正相关。模型结构、数据质量和训练方法能显著改变 $N_c$ 的位置。此外，通过宽度归一化可消除负相关，且该发现对于前沿模型同样适用（相关系数达+0.72）。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了语言模型中推理与真实性能力之间存在一种“相变”现象。这种机制在损失函数曲线中不可见，但在特定的临界规模（$N_c$）附近表现出从竞争到合作的转变。通过数据清洗、架构优化和蒸馏技术，可以有效降低 $N_c$，从而在较小规模下实现更高的性能协同。该发现为理解大模型的缩放定律及其内部机制提供了新的视角。

Abstract: Scaling laws predict loss from compute but not how capabilities interact. We measure the coupling between reasoning and truthfulness across 63 base models from 16 families and find a regime change invisible to loss curves: below a family-dependent critical scale $N_c$, capabilities anticorrelate; above it, they cooperate. $N_c \approx 3.5$B parameters [2.9B, 13.4B] (bootstrap 95% CI), but model size is not the only variable that determines phase. Architecture, data curation, and training recipe each shift $N_c$ independently: curated training eliminated the coupling dip between Qwen generations ($0.025 \to 0.830$ at matched scale), Gemma-4 at 4B achieves coupling 0.871, characteristic of 13B+ standard-trained models, through distillation and architectural innovation, and Phi at 1B matches web-trained coupling at 10B through data curation alone. Width normalization eliminates the anticorrelation across all tested families, supporting an output-projection bottleneck. Internally, 38 of 40 models show zero competing attention heads. A sparse-regression ODE cross-predicts held-out Llama-2 at 5.6% error. The diagnostic requires no model internals -- only public benchmark scores across a model family. The cooperative regime extends to the frontier ($r = +0.72$, 34 models, 10 labs). Code, data, and an open-source activation-steering tool for any open-weight model are released alongside an interactive dashboard that diagnoses any model's coupling phase, suggests concrete interventions (data curation, width, benchmark rotation), and provides ODE scaling predictions, frontier diagnostics, and eigenstructure analysis: https://zehenlabs.com/cape/.

</details>

Abstract: Overcrowding in emergency departments (ED) remains a persistent operational challenge worldwide, causing delays in care delivery and downstream congestion. ### [78] [The Growing Pains of Frontier Models: When Leaderboards Stop Separating and What to Measure Next](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18840)
*Adil Amin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个评估前沿AI模型能力协同演进的框架，通过将编程和推理能力分解为耦合趋势与偏差指标，揭示了不同实验室的研发策略差异，并为未来的基准测试演变提供了可验证的预测模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Leaderboards rank frontier models on independent axes but do not reveal whether capabilities reinforce or trade off across releases -- and at the frontier, this interaction is the more informative signal. ### [79] [From Cumulative Constraints to Adaptive Runtime Safety Control for Nonstationary Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18841)
*Timofey Tomashevskiy*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对非平稳强化学习环境，本文提出了CPSS机制，将全局累积安全预算自适应地转化为实时状态级动作约束，有效提升了复杂动态环境下的系统安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在强化学习中，传统的累积代价约束无法直接规避非平稳环境下的个体危险决策。固定的状态级阈值难以平衡保守性与灵活性，导致系统在面对环境变化时无法有效维护安全性。

Method: 提出约束投影安全防御（CPSS）机制：1. 实时跟踪剩余安全预算；2. 将预算投影为随时间变化的动态风险阈值；3. 利用上下文信号在线调整阈值（高需求场景下更严格，预算充足时更宽松）；4. 通过过滤器剔除预测安全代价超过阈值的策略动作。

Result: 理论分析表明CPSS能保证执行动作满足每状态阈值，且具有有限时域累积代价边界和受控的性能损耗；在非平稳高速公路合并场景实验中，该方法显著减少了安全违规行为，增加了安全距离，且在干预频率与策略执行之间取得了良好的平衡。

Conclusion: CPSS提供了一种将全局累积安全预算转化为局部动态约束的有效框架，证明了在非平稳强化学习环境下，通过上下文自适应的实时防御机制可以显著提升安全性，同时保证了有限的性能损耗，是构建可靠连续学习系统的实用方案。

Abstract: Safety in reinforcement learning is often specified through cumulative cost constraints, but these trajectory-level guarantees do not directly prevent unsafe individual decisions, especially under nonstationarity. In continual and nonstationary settings, the difficulty is amplified because the risk associated with the same action can vary across contexts, while a fixed state-level threshold may be either too conservative or too weak. We propose Constraint Projection Safety Shield (CPSS), a runtime mechanism that converts a cumulative safety budget into adaptive state-level control constraints during execution. CPSS tracks the remaining safety budget, projects it into a time-varying admissible risk threshold, and filters policy actions whose predicted safety cost exceeds the active threshold. The threshold is adjusted online using contextual signals so that enforcement becomes stricter in more demanding or rapidly changing regimes and less restrictive when the available safety budget is sufficient. We analyze the resulting shielded policy and show that the mechanism guarantees per-state threshold satisfaction for executed actions, induces finite-horizon cumulative cost bounds, and yields a performance degradation bound in terms of intervention frequency and per-step reward distortion. We evaluate CPSS in nonstationary highway merging scenarios using highway-env. Across multiple seeds, CPSS substantially reduces proximity-based safety violations and increases separation margins while intervening selectively rather than dominating the learned policy. These results support adaptive budget-to-threshold projection as a practical way to transform cumulative safety specifications into effective local safety control for continual reinforcement learning systems.
