### [121] [LoRA vs. Full Fine-Tuning: A Theoretical Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19018)
*Ali Zindari,Rotem Mulayoff,Sebastian U. Stich*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文从理论层面解释了LoRA优于全量微调的原因：当任务间差异具备低秩特性时，LoRA能够通过隐式的低秩约束获得更优的泛化能力，并揭示了LoRA秩选择对性能的影响机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管LoRA作为一种高效微调技术被广泛应用，但其背后的理论机制（尤其是为什么它能达到甚至超越全量微调的效果）尚不明确。研究者旨在通过数学建模来解析LoRA的理论行为及其泛化性能。

Method: 本文在简化线性回归模型框架下，对比了LoRA与全量微调的超额风险（excess risk），分析了在超定和欠定情形下的性能表现，并探讨了LoRA秩的选择对模型泛化能力的影响。同时，通过在实际任务上的实验对理论发现进行了验证。

Result: 研究发现，当预训练任务与下游任务的差异具有低秩结构时，LoRA的超额风险低于全量微调。此外，研究解释了为何较小的秩能够通过限制模型表达能力从而在特定场景下提升泛化精度，且该结论在非线性实际任务中同样适用。

Conclusion: 本文从理论上阐明了LoRA在特定条件下优于全量微调的原因，证明了当预训练任务与下游任务之间的差异具有低秩特性时，LoRA能够获得更好的泛化表现，并揭示了低秩约束在缓解过拟合方面的正则化作用。

Abstract: Fine-tuning adapts a pre-trained model to downstream tasks using a small amount of labeled data. Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) is an efficient fine-tuning method that reduces memory and computation costs while often achieving performance close to full fine-tuning. Despite its widespread use, the theoretical behavior of LoRA is not yet well understood. In this paper, we study LoRA in a simple linear regression setting and compare its excess risk with that of full fine-tuning. Our analysis identifies regimes in which LoRA achieves lower excess risk than full fine-tuning in both overdetermined and underdetermined settings. Specifically, our theory predicts that LoRA can outperform full fine-tuning when the difference between the pretraining and the downstream tasks is effectively low-rank. We further show how the choice of LoRA rank affects generalization performance, explaining why using a very small rank can improve test accuracy in certain settings, even though it limits model expressivity. Finally, we support our theoretical results with experiments on practical tasks, suggesting that the identified tradeoffs and insights extend beyond linear regression.

</details>


### [122] [GRASP: Deterministic argument ranking in interaction graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19141)
*Diganta Misra,Antonio Orvieto,Rediet Abebe,Volkan Cevher*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大模型作为辩论裁判时评估不一致且不透明的问题，本文提出GRASP框架，通过将复杂辩论拆解为局部交互并利用传播算法生成结构化排名，显著提升了评估的可重复性与透明度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大模型作为裁判进行“整体式评估（holistic judging）”时存在严重的不稳定性（模型间不一致），且将复杂的交互结构压缩为单一评分导致缺乏透明度，难以区分论证结构与修辞偏好。

Method: 提出了一种名为GRASP（Gradual Ranking with Attacks and Support Propagation）的框架。该方法将辩论分解为局部的交互判断，利用收敛的攻防传播算子将这些稳定的局部交互判断聚合为全局排名，而非直接生成单一的整体评分。

Result: 实验表明，局部交互判断比整体排名具有更好的可重复性；GRASP能产生更一致的全局排名；且GRASP评分与人类的主观“说服力”标签不相关，成功区分了论证的结构稳健性与修辞效果。

Conclusion: GRASP提供了一种透明且可审计的替代方案，通过衡量论证的“结构充分性”而非单一的整体评分，解决了大模型作为裁判时存在的不稳定性和不透明性问题，能够有效提升评估的可重复性。

Abstract: Large language models are increasingly deployed as automated judges to evaluate the strength of arguments. As this role expands, their legitimacy depends on consistency, transparency, and the ability to separate argumentative structure from rhetorical appeal. However, we show that holistic judging - a common LLM-as-a-Judge practice where a model provides a global verdict on a debate - suffers from substantial inter-model disagreement. We argue that this instability arises from collapsing a debate's complex interaction structure into a single opaque score. To address this, we propose GRASP (Gradual Ranking with Attacks and Support Propagation), a deterministic framework that aggregates stable local interaction judgments into a global ranking via a convergent attack--defense propagation operator. We show that local interaction judgments are more reproducible than holistic rankings in LLM-as-a-Judge evaluations, allowing GRASP to produce more consistent global rankings. We further show that GRASP scores do not correlate with human "convincingness" labels, highlighting a vital sociotechnical distinction: GRASP does not measure persuasion, factuality, or rhetorical appeal, but structural sufficiency - a defense-aware notion of argument robustness over the explicit interaction graph. Overall, GRASP offers a transparent and auditable alternative to holistic LLM judging.

### [123] [CEPO: RLVR Self-Distillation using Contrastive Evidence Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19436)
*Ahmed Heakl,Abdelrahman M. Shaker,Youssef Mohamed,Rania Elbadry,Omar Fetouh,Fahad Shahbaz Khan,Salman Khan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大模型推理任务中信用分配不准的问题，提出 CEPO 方法，通过利用错误样本进行对比学习，在不增加成本的前提下精确识别关键推理步骤，提升了模型的推理准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）方法在处理奖励分配时过于粗糙，无法区分模型生成的关键推理步骤与无关的语法填补，导致训练效率低下。而现有的自蒸馏方法又容易因答案泄露导致梯度污染，CEPO 旨在解决这些信用分配不公与梯度泄露的问题。

Method: 提出对比证据策略优化（Contrastive Evidence Policy Optimization, CEPO）。该方法不仅考虑“正确答案是否支持该 token”，还要求“错误答案是否反对该 token”。它利用训练批次中现有的错误输出作为“负面教师”，在每个 token 上进行对比评估，从而精确识别并强化关键的推理步骤，过滤掉无关的填补内容。

Result: 在五个多模态数学推理基准测试中，CEPO 在 2B 和 4B 参数规模下分别取得了 43.43% 和 60.56% 的平均准确率，显著优于基准方法 GRPO（分别为 41.17% 和 57.43%），且验证了传统自蒸馏方法会因信息泄露导致性能下降的理论预测。

Conclusion: CEPO 是一种高效且鲁棒的强化学习微调方法，通过引入负面反馈（错误回答的教师信号）来更精准地进行信用分配。它克服了传统 RLVR 方法无法区分关键推理步骤与冗余填补内容的缺陷，且在不增加采样成本的情况下提升了模型在多模态数学推理任务中的性能。

Abstract: When a model produces a correct solution under reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), every token receives the same reward signal regardless of whether it was a decisive reasoning step or a grammatical filler. A natural fix is to condition the model on the correct answer as a teacher, identifying tokens it would have generated differently had it known the answer. Prior work shows this either corrupts training by leaking the answer into the gradient, or produces a weak signal that cannot distinguish decisive steps from filler, since both look equally surprising relative to the model's baseline. We propose Contrastive Evidence Policy Optimization (CEPO), which asks a sharper question at every token: not just "does the correct answer favor this token?" but "does the correct answer favor it while the wrong answer disfavors it?" A token satisfying both is a genuine reasoning step; one satisfying neither is filler. The wrong-answer teacher is constructed from rejected rollouts already in the training batch, incurring no additional sampling cost. We prove CEPO inherits all structural safety guarantees of the prior state of the art while strictly sharpening credit at decisive tokens, with the improvement vanishing exactly at filler positions. Empirically, CEPO achieves 43.43% and 60.56% average accuracy across five multimodal mathematical reasoning benchmarks at 2B and 4B scale, respectively, versus 41.17% and 57.43% for GRPO under identical training budgets. Distribution-matching self-distillation methods (OPSD, SDPO) fall below the untrained baseline, empirically confirming the information leakage our theory predicts. Our code is available at https://github.com/ahmedheakl/CEPO.

</details>


### [124] [Learning When to Adapt](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19028)
*Ali Zindari,Xiaowen Jiang,Rotem Mulayoff,Sebastian U. Stich*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DISeL 是一种增强型 LoRA 方法，通过为低秩组件添加轻量级输入敏感门控，实现了按需更新，从而在提升微调效果的同时有效减少了对预训练知识的遗忘。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 LoRA 方法采用“输入无关”的静态更新，导致在微调分布与预训练分布之间存在权衡，极易引发灾难性遗忘。作者旨在开发一种能够感知输入内容的动态适应方法，以解决上述平衡问题。

Method: 提出 DISeL（动态输入敏感 LoRA），在 LoRA 的每个秩-1 组件上引入轻量级的输入相关门控机制（Gating Mechanism）。该机制默认保持预训练行为，仅在必要时激活特定的组件以降低微调损失。

Result: 在 RoBERTa (GLUE 基准) 以及 Llama 和 Mistral (数学推理与代码生成任务) 上的实验表明，DISeL 在保持竞争性微调精度的同时，显著降低了灾难性遗忘。此外，门控激活情况提供了关于模型内部任务适配机制的可解释性分析。

Conclusion: DISeL 提供了一种高效且可解释的微调方案，通过动态门控机制缓解了传统 LoRA 静态更新带来的灾难性遗忘问题，在保持参数高效性的同时显著提升了模型在跨分布任务上的鲁棒性。

Abstract: Low-rank adaptation (LoRA) is a widely used parameter-efficient fine-tuning method, yet its learned correction is static: the same low-rank update is applied to every input. This input-agnostic approach creates an inevitable compromise between adapting to the fine-tuning distribution and preserving pre-trained behavior on inputs outside that distribution, contributing to catastrophic forgetting. We introduce DISeL (Dynamic Input-Sensitive LoRA), which augments LoRA modules with lightweight input-dependent gates over individual rank-one components. The gating mechanism is designed to preserve the pre-trained model's behavior by default, while training learns to activate selected components that reduce the fine-tuning loss. DISeL adds only a small number of parameters and preserves the low-rank structure. Across RoBERTa on GLUE, and Llama and Mistral models fine-tuned for mathematical reasoning and code generation, DISeL reduces forgetting relative to LoRA and related variants while maintaining competitive fine-tuning accuracy. In addition, the learned gate activations provide an interpretable diagnostic view of which layers and rank components are most activated during fine-tuning, giving insight into where task-specific adaptation is concentrated. Code available at https://github.com/alizindari/DISeL .

### [125] [KVBuffer: IO-aware Serving for Linear Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19049)
*Longwei Zou,Lin Zhong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 KVBuffer，一种针对线性注意力机制的 IO 感知缓冲服务方案，通过优化内存访问与计算方式，显著降低了长上下文推理的解码延迟并提升了系统并发吞吐量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管线性注意力机制通过常数级解码成本在长上下文任务中表现出色，但现有系统将其实现为在每步解码时循环计算并更新庞大的线性注意力状态。由于该状态体积远大于单 token 的键值，导致高昂的内存访问开销，严重限制了推理服务的效率。

Method: 提出了一种名为 KVBuffer 的 IO 感知服务机制，其核心思想是缓存最近的键（Key）和值（Value）。在此基础上，实现了三种优化策略：1. 分块计算（Chunkwise computation），通过延迟状态更新以减少内存访问；2. 针对投机采样（Speculative decoding）的并行验证，避免存储临时状态；3. 针对短上下文，直接从缓存的键值计算注意力输出，无需创建或维护线性注意力状态。

Result: 在 SGLang 框架下针对 Qwen3-Next 模型进行实现与评估，结果显示 KVBuffer 可将线性注意力解码延迟降低 45.17%；在投机采样场景下，验证 4 个草稿 token 时，最大并发请求处理能力提升了 5 倍。

Conclusion: KVBuffer 通过一种 IO 感知的缓冲机制，有效解决了线性注意力机制在推理服务中因循环计算巨大状态而导致的内存访问瓶颈。该方案在保持模型性能的同时，显著提升了线性注意力模型的推理效率与吞吐量，为长上下文推理服务提供了优化的系统级解决方案。

Abstract: Linear attention has recently gained significant attention for long-context inference due to its constant decoding cost with respect to context length. However, existing serving systems typically serve linear attention by recurrently computing and updating a large linear attention state in every decoding step. Since the state is much larger than the per-token key and value, recurrent decoding incurs substantial memory access and becomes inefficient for serving linear attention. In this paper, we propose KVBuffer, an IO-aware serving mechanism for linear attention. By buffering recent keys and values, KVBuffer enables serving systems to compute linear attention outputs in more flexible and memory-efficient ways. For decoding, KVBuffer enables chunkwise computation, which reduces average memory access and decoding latency by deferring state updates and applying them in batch. For speculative decoding, KVBuffer verifies draft tokens in parallel and avoids storing temporary states. For short contexts, KVBuffer computes attention outputs directly from buffered keys and values, without creating or updating the linear attention state. We implement KVBuffer in SGLang for Qwen3-Next. Our evaluations show that KVBuffer can reduce linear attention decoding latency by up to 45.17% and increase the maximum number of serving requests by 5x for speculative decoding when verifying four draft tokens.

</details>


### [126] [Generative Pseudo-Force Fields for Molecular Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19050)
*Stefaan Simon Pierre Hessmann,Khaled Kahouli,Stefan Gugler,Michael Plainer,Frank Noé,Klaus-Robert Müller,Niklas Wolf Andreas Gebauer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出生成伪力场（GPFF），通过将物理力场学习与扩散模型结合，实现了无需高昂计算开销、无需时间步调参的高效分子构象生成，在生成速度和有效性上均优于现有基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 提出生成伪力场（GPFF），在参考平衡结构上构建二次伪势能面进行MLFF训练；2. 利用高斯噪声对平衡结构进行扰动，实现非平衡训练数据的实时生成；3. 将GPFF与时间步无关的方差爆炸扩散模型结合，使力场预测直接等同于分数（Score）；4. 引入基于MLFF启发的直接去噪方案及支持几何约束的采样算法。

Result: 在QM9数据集上，GPFF在256次神经函数评估（NFE）下达到了100%的有效性，在仅需6次NFE时有效性超过50%，表现优于主流扩散模型基准。此外，该方法支持自定义先验和几何约束，并能实现在药物设计场景下的分子实时生成。

Conclusion: 生成伪力场（GPFF）有效地将扩散模型的高效采样与分子力场的物理规律结合起来。它不仅避免了昂贵的从头计算（ab-initio）数据需求，还实现了无需时间步长调节的稳定生成，为分子设计提供了高效、实时的工具。

Abstract: Generating stable molecular conformations typically forces a tradeoff between the physical realism of energy-based relaxation and the sampling efficiency of data-driven generative models. While machine learning force fields (MLFFs) can sample stable conformations by relaxing molecular geometries according to physical forces, they require costly ab-initio training data. Conversely, diffusion models (DMs) learn from equilibrium data alone but are dependent on noise schedules and time-step conditioning. In this work, we propose generative pseudo-force fields (GPFFs) to bridge these paradigms by training an MLFF on a quadratic pseudo-potential energy surface relative to reference equilibrium structures. Because no ab-initio calculations are required for the perturbed geometries, non-equilibrium training data can be generated on the fly by perturbing the equilibria with Gaussian noise. We show that GPFFs constitute a time-step-agnostic variant of variance exploding DMs: the score comes from the predicted pseudo-forces but because force magnitudes implicitly encode the noise level, no time-step conditioning is needed. Our GPFF can hence be used as a drop-in replacement in standard diffusion sampling (ancestral, Heun) but also facilitates more efficient, adaptive variants and an MLFF inspired direct denoising scheme. Our proposed sampling algorithms support arbitrary structural priors and geometric constraints. On QM9, GPFF has 100 % validity at 256 neural function evaluations (NFE) and over 50 % at just 6 NFE, outperforming diffusion baselines across all samplers. Combined with custom priors, we showcase the fast and accurate generation process of our method in a molecular editor for a drug design setting, where a molecule is generated in real time.

### [127] [OScaR: The Occam's Razor for Extreme KV Cache Quantization in LLMs and Beyond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19660)
*Zunhai Su,Rui Yang,Chao Zhang,Yaxiu Liu,Yifan Zhang,Wei Wu,Jing Xiong,Dayou Du,Xialie Zhuang,Yulei Qian,Yuchen Xie,Yik-Chung Wu,Hongxia Yang,Ngai Wong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 为了解决大模型推理中 KV Cache 的内存瓶颈，本文揭示了词元范数不平衡（TNI）导致的量化误差问题，并提出了一种轻量且强大的量化框架 OScaR。该方法通过通道旋转和词元缩放技术，在 INT2 极低比特下实现了性能与效率的平衡，显著提升了推理速度与吞吐量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大模型上下文长度和多模态能力的增长，KV Cache 的内存占用成为推理瓶颈。传统的通道级量化在极高压缩比下性能退化严重，这是因为忽略了“词元范数不平衡”（Token Norm Imbalance, TNI）现象，该现象在量化过程中会放大误差。因此，作者旨在寻找一种能够克服 TNI 影响、实现极低位宽下高精度压缩的方法。

Method: 论文提出了 OScaR (Omni-Scaled Canalized Rotation) 框架，包含两个核心组件：1. Canalized Rotation（通道化旋转）：通过旋转操作平滑通道间的异常值；2. Omni-Token Scaling（全词元缩放）：针对性地解决 Token Norm Imbalance (TNI) 问题，减小词元间范数差异。此外，该工作还开发了优化的 CUDA 内核以支持高效部署。

Result: OScaR 在各种 X-LLM（纯文本、多模态、全模态模型）上均表现优异，在 INT2 量化下实现近乎无损的性能。与 BF16 FlashDecoding-v2 相比，该方法实现了最高 3.0 倍的解码加速，内存占用减少 5.3 倍，吞吐量提升 4.1 倍。

Conclusion: OScaR 提出了一种高效、通用的 KV Cache 量化框架，能够有效解决长上下文和多模态大模型中的内存瓶颈问题。该方法在极低比特（INT2）下实现了近乎无损的性能，并显著提升了推理速度与吞吐量，为大规模语言模型的部署提供了一个高性能的新基准。

Abstract: The rapid advancement toward long-context reasoning and multi-modal intelligence has made the memory footprint of the Key-Value (KV) cache a dominant memory bottleneck for efficient deployment. While the established per-channel quantization effectively accommodates intrinsic channel-wise outliers in Key tensors, its efficacy diminishes under extreme compression. In this work, we revisit the inherent limitations of the per-channel quantization paradigm from both empirical and theoretical perspectives. Our analysis identifies Token Norm Imbalance (TNI) as the primary bottleneck to quantization fidelity. We demonstrate that TNI systematically amplifies errors when shared quantization parameters are required to span token groups exhibiting substantial norm disparities. Instead of relying on intricate quantization pipelines (e.g., TurboQuant), we propose OScaR (Omni-Scaled Canalized Rotation), an accurate and lightweight KV cache compression framework for X-LLMs (i.e., text-only, multi-modal, and omni-modal LLMs). Advancing the per-channel paradigm, OScaR employs Canalized Rotation followed by Omni-Token Scaling to mitigate TNI-induced sequence-dimensional variance both effectively and efficiently, further supported by our optimized system design and CUDA kernels. Extensive evaluations across X-LLMs show that OScaR consistently outperforms existing methods and achieves near-lossless performance under INT2 quantization, establishing it as a robust, low-complexity, and universal framework that defines a new Pareto front. Compared with the BF16 FlashDecoding-v2 baseline, our OScaR implementation achieves a notable up to 3.0x speedup in decoding, reduces memory footprint by 5.3x, and increases throughput by 4.1x. The code for OScaR is publicly available at https://github.com/ZunhaiSu/OScaR-KV-Quant.

### [128] [Mapping Uncharted Symmetries: Machine Discovery in Combinatorics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19063)

Method: 提出了“简单刚性比例下的学习”（SLURP）框架，并开发了两种方法：MapSeek-Functional（通过伪标签和监督学习交替建模）和MapSeek-Symbolic（直接生成符号公式）。

Abstract: Inspired by long-standing open problems in algebraic combinatorics, we show that modern machine learning can meaningfully contribute to verifiable mathematical discoveries. In particular, we focus on the construction of simple mathematical functions under exact distributional constraints, a setting we formalize as Simple Learning Under Rigid Proportions (SLURP). To streamline verification and reproducibility, we release all code, including a formalization of all the mathematical discoveries of this paper in Lean 4.

### [129] [MANGO: Meta-Adaptive Network Gradient Optimization for Online Continual Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19080)
*Ankita Awasthi,Marco Apolinario,Kaushik Roy*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对在线持续学习中的灾难性遗忘问题，本文提出了 MANGO 框架，利用梯度门控和元学习正则化机制，显著提升了模型在不断流式数据下的稳定性和学习效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在线持续学习（OCL）面临严峻的灾难性遗忘挑战，而现有的重演（rehearsal）、蒸馏、正则化或元学习方法在偏差控制、参数调制灵活性及反馈机制方面存在局限性。

Method: 提出了一种名为 MANGO 的框架，通过“梯度门控”（gradient-gating）根据参数敏感度调节更新，并使用“元学习正则化”（meta-learned regularization）动态调整稳定性系数，将经验回放（replay）同时作为训练信号和遗忘评估器。

Result: 在 CLEAR-10、CIFAR-100 和 Tiny-ImageNet 等基准测试中，MANGO 均优于现有基线方法，达到了最先进（SOTA）的水平，在各种回放容量下表现稳定，并能在部分任务中实现正向的向后迁移。

Conclusion: MANGO 框架通过结合梯度门控和元学习正则化，有效解决了在线持续学习中稳定性与可塑性之间的权衡问题，在多个标准数据集上取得了领先的性能，并实现了正向的向后迁移。

Abstract: In Online Continual Learning (OCL), a neural network sequentially learns from a non-stationary data stream in a single-pass with access only to a limited memory replay buffer. This contrasts sharply with off-line continual learning where training is multiple epoch dependent on large datasets. The main challenge faced by OCL is to overcome catastrophic forgetting of past tasks (stability) while learning new ones efficiently (plasticity). Existing methods counter forgetting via replay-based rehearsal, output level distillation, fixed regularization, or meta-learning on the current data. However, these methods have limitations: rehearsal introduces a stored sample bias; distillation operates on output-distributions without modulating parameter updates; fixed-regularization penalizes parameters irrespective of sensitivity; stream-only meta-learning lacks a feedback controlled parameter update. We propose Meta-Adaptive Network Gradient Optimization (MANGO), an OCL framework that balances stability-plasticity via gradient-gating and meta-learned regularization. Gradient-gating scales parameter updates based on sensitivity, preventing destructive updates. Meta-learned regularization adapts stability coefficients, evaluating the effect of parameter update on replay. In MANGO, replay acts as both a training signal and a forgetting evaluator. We evaluated our method on three standard OCL benchmark datasets. MANGO outperforms strong baselines, achieving state-of-the-art results with consistent performance across replay sizes. In domain incremental learning on CLEAR-10 and class incremental learning on CIFAR-100 and Tiny-ImageNet, it achieves highest accuracy among all baselines and achieves positive Backward Transfer, overcoming forgetting on CLEAR-10.

</details>


### [130] [A Measure-Theoretic Analysis of Reasoning: Structural Generalization and Approximation Limits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19944)
*Yuyang Zhang,Yifu Zhang,Xuehai Zhou,Xiaoyin Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过最优传输理论揭示了LLM推理泛化的机制，指出必须采用平移不变的注意力机制，并增加模型深度（而非单纯增加宽度）才能有效解决分布外任务中的推理崩塌问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型（LLM）的推理缩放律已有大量实证记录，但其分布外（OOD）泛化的理论机制尚不明确，特别是在位置编码选择和模型架构深度对泛化能力的影响方面缺乏理论支撑。

Method: 1. 将推理过程形式化为最优传输（Optimal Transport），利用Wasserstein-1距离量化领域偏移；2. 运用Kantorovich对偶理论，通过架构的Lipschitz连续性和函数逼近极限来界定OOD泛化误差；3. 将序列回溯映射为Dyck-k语言，推导TC0 Transformer的电路深度下界；4. 在54种Transformer配置上进行组合搜索任务的实证验证。

Result: 1. 证明了绝对位置编码因无法保持平移不变性，会导致OOD风险无法收敛；而旋转位置编码（RoPE）通过保持等变性有效界定了误差；2. 揭示了深度对于解决复杂逻辑任务（如回溯推理）的必要性，证明仅靠增加模型宽度无法克服Barron空间中的不可约逼近误差；3. 实证结果显示泛化风险随Wasserstein领域偏移呈现单调退化。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，LLM的分布外（OOD）泛化能力受限于架构的Lipschitz连续性和函数逼近极限。为了实现稳健的推理，模型必须采用平移不变的注意力机制（如RoPE），且必须通过增加深度（而非宽度）来突破电路复杂度的下界，以避免表示崩塌。

Abstract: While empirical scaling laws for LLM reasoning are well-documented, the theoretical mechanisms governing out-of-distribution (OOD) generalization remain elusive. We formalize reasoning via optimal transport, projecting discrete trajectories into a continuous metric space to quantify domain shifts using the Wasserstein-1 distance. Invoking Kantorovich duality, we bound OOD generalization via architectural Lipschitz continuity and functional approximation limits. This exposes two primary constraints. First, position-dependent attention (e.g., Absolute Positional Encoding) fails to preserve shift invariance, yielding an $Ω(1)$ Lipschitz constant and expected risk, whereas shift-invariant mechanisms (e.g., Rotary Embeddings) preserve equivariance and bound the error. Second, by mapping sequential backtracking to a Dyck-$k$ language, we establish a strict circuit depth lower bound for $\text{TC}^0$ Transformers. Scaling physical layer depth is necessary to avert representation collapse -- a constraint that scaling representation width cannot bypass due to irreducible approximation bounds in Barron spaces. Evaluations across 54 Transformer configurations on combinatorial search corroborate these bounds, demonstrating that generalization risk degrades monotonically with the Wasserstein domain shift.

### [131] [Chessformer: A Unified Architecture for Chess Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19091)
*Daniel Monroe,George Eilender,Philip Chalmers,Zhenwei Tang,Ashton Anderson*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 Chessformer，这是一种统一的 Transformer 架构，通过结合创新的几何注意力偏差（GAB）和方格标记化设计，在国际象棋的胜率提升、人类行为预测以及模型可解释性三个方面均达到了行业领先水平。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统人工智能在国际象棋领域的建模任务（强化实力、预测人类行为、模型可解释性）通常采用不同的架构且往往与领域几何特性不匹配。研究旨在探究是否存在一种统一的架构，能够同时支持这三个核心目标。

Method: 提出了一种名为 Chessformer 的编码器型 Transformer 架构。该模型将棋盘方格视为标记，引入了名为“几何注意力偏差（GAB）”的新型动态位置编码以适应棋盘几何特性，并使用基于注意力的源-目标策略头进行行动预测。

Result: 1. 在人类落子预测任务（Maia3）上，以不到四分之一的参数量实现了 57.1% 的预测准确率，刷新了业界水平；2. 集成至 Leela Chess Zero 后，提升了超过 100 Elo 的竞技实力，并在多项顶尖计算机国际象棋赛事中击败了 Stockfish；3. 实现了直接基于棋盘方格的细粒度可解释性分析。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了通过将模型的标记化、位置编码和输出设计与特定领域的底层几何结构对齐，可以同时实现性能提升、人类行为兼容性和模型可解释性。Chessformer 为复杂博弈任务提供了一种统一且高效的建模范式。

Abstract: Chess has long served as a canonical testbed for artificial intelligence, but modeling approaches for its central tasks have diverged. Maximizing playing strength, predicting human play, and enabling interpretability are typically solved with disparate architectures, and these designs are often misaligned with the geometry of the domain. This raises the natural question of whether these objectives require separate modeling paradigms, or if there exists a single architecture that supports them simultaneously. We introduce Chessformer, a unified architecture that advances the state of the art on all three central goals in chess modeling. Chessformer is an encoder-only transformer that represents board squares as tokens, augments self-attention with a novel dynamic positional encoding called Geometric Attention Bias (GAB) that adapts to domain-specific geometry, and predicts actions with an attention-based source-destination policy head. We evaluate Chessformer on each front. First, we develop \maiathree, a family of models for human move prediction that reaches 57.1\% move-matching accuracy, significantly surpassing the previous state of the art with fewer than a quarter of the parameters. Second, we integrate Chessformer into Leela Chess Zero, a leading open-source engine, adding over 100 Elo of playing strength and resulting in tournament victories over Stockfish in major computer chess competitions. Third, we show that Chessformer's square-token design makes attention patterns and activations directly attributable to board squares, enabling granular interpretability analyses that prior architectures do not naturally support. More broadly, our results demonstrate that aligning a model's tokenization, positional encoding, and output design with the underlying structure of a domain can yield simultaneous gains in performance, human compatibility, and interpretability.

Abstract: Schedule-Free Learning has shown promise as a practical anytime training method for machine learning, showing success across dozens of standard benchmark problems. However, strong performance for LLM training has only been demonstrated at small scales. We identify a number of fixes necessary to scale up Schedule-Free Learning to larger batch sizes and model sizes, and present a learning-rate-free and schedule-free method (ScheduleFree+) for training large language models which greatly outperforms Warmup-Stable-Decay (WSD) schedules. We also demonstrate that Schedule-Free Learning is most effective for long duration training, and at 1000 tokens per parameter, it outperforms SOTA schedules by 31%. Schedule-Free Learning provides a theoretical foundation for the use of model averaging and checkpoint merging during pretraining.

In lab settings, performance degradation can be characterized through electrochemical testing protocols by periodic pauses of normal operation. Such interruption is not practical for full-scale stack deployments, limiting system operators' ability to make real-time assessments of state-of-health (SoH). We present a machine learning (ML) framework that performs virtual electrochemical characterization during normal operation. The method uses an encoder-decoder transformer, conditioned on operational data, to reconstruct characterization outputs, focusing here on polarization curves. Abstract: Causal representation learning (CRL) seeks to uncover meaningful latent variables and their corresponding causal structure from high-dimensional observational data. Although its significance, CRL identifiability remains a crucial property, as it ensures the recovery of the mechanisms behind the data generation process, and hence the interpretability and robustness of the representation. Proving identifiability in CRL is intrinsically difficult, and we address in this work an even more challenging setting: multimodality. We consider multimodal observed data with a latent partially shared structure. Each modality is generated, through non linear mixing functions, from a specific subset of causal latent variables. Under flexible assumptions and without imposing any parametric distribution on the latent variables, we establish component-wise identifiability guarantees for the causal latent representation. Our identifiability results, furthermore, apply to the undercomplete scenario where we have, for each modality, more observed than latent variables. To instantiate our theoretical analysis, we introduce a Wasserstein-based module to recover the partially shared latent structure. ### [136] [PMF-CL: Pareto-Minimal-Forgetting Continual Learner for Conflicting Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19145)
*Srijith Nair,Atilla Eryilmaz,Jia,Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文从多任务学习的角度出发，提出了一种基于帕累托最优的持续学习算法框架（PMF-CL），解决了传统方法中关于遗忘理论定义模糊的问题，并实现了对冲突任务的高效内存管理与性能平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的持续学习算法虽然通过内存机制缓解灾难性遗忘，但缺乏对“保留何种信息以最小化遗忘”这一核心问题的理论支撑。由于实际任务间往往不存在公共全局最优解，传统的假设在应用中受限，因此需要一种能处理冲突任务并提供系统性理论框架的方法。

Method: 本文采用多任务学习（MTL）视角，将持续学习问题转化为寻找帕累托最优解的过程。针对线性回归、基函数回归以及具有二次上界的损失函数（如逻辑回归），推导出了帕累托最小遗忘（PMF-CL）算法。该算法利用内存高效的迭代更新机制，在处理具有 d 个参数的模型时，仅需 O(d^2) 的静态内存开销。

Result: 研究表明，通过采用帕累托最优性准则，可以有效量化并最小化任务间的冲突与遗忘。对于二次优化问题，PMF-CL 算法实现了内存占用与计算效率的平衡，提供了一种在给定内存预算下实现近似最优性能的系统性方法。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种基于帕累托最优性的持续学习（CL）新范式，证明了在任务冲突且无公共全局最优解的现实场景下，追求帕累托最优解是最小化遗忘的理论基础。该方法为在计算资源受限的情况下平衡多个任务的性能提供了严谨的数学框架。

Abstract: In the literature, many continual learning (CL) algorithms have been proposed to address the issue of catastrophic forgetting in ML models (i.e., learning new tasks leads to the loss of performance on previously learned tasks). Although all CL approaches use some form of memory to retain information about past tasks, a grounded understanding of what information needs to be stored to minimize catastrophic forgetting remains elusive. Recently, it has been recognized that under the strong assumption of the existence of a common global minimizer over all tasks, catastrophic forgetting can be completely avoided. However, in practice, tasks rarely have a common global minimizer, and a certain amount of forgetting is inevitable. In this paper, we propose a foundational framework for principled and systematic CL of conflicting tasks using a multi-task learning (MTL) perspective. The approach is based on finding Pareto-optimal solutions, i.e., the solutions which, by definition, minimally forget the previous tasks in the Pareto sense. We derive Pareto-minimal-forgetting CL algorithms for linear and basis-function regression, and general loss functions which have a quadratic upper bound, e.g., logistic regression. For quadratic problems, PMF-CL uses memory-efficient iterative updates with a static memory footage of $\mathcal{O}(d^2)$ for models with $d$ parameters.

</details>


### [137] [Planner-Admissible Graph-PDE Value Extensions for Sparse Goal-Conditioned Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19185)
*Shiheng Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文将图价值函数扩展视作PDE Dirichlet问题，提出了一种基于局部动作间隙的证书，证明了AMLE（绝对最小Lipschitz扩展）相比传统的调和扩展，能更好地引导稀疏标签环境下的贪婪规划，并在AntMaze实验中取得了显著的性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在仅有少量成本标签的稀疏目标条件下，如何准确地扩展价值函数以引导贪婪路径成功到达目标是一个挑战。传统的调和扩展方法虽然常见，但在处理最短路径贪婪排序方面存在局限性，作者旨在探究哪种图价值扩展方法在基于argmin-Q的规划器下是“规划可采纳的”（planner-admissible）。

Method: 本文将目标条件规划建模为图上的PDE Dirichlet扩展问题。作者推导了一个局部动作间隙证书，证明当替代价值误差小于真实动作间隙的一半时，贪婪路径即可到达目标。研究对比了AMLE、调和扩展以及不同p值的图p-Laplacian扩展在AntMaze布局图上的性能，并通过机制审计分析了不同方法在局部几何决策中的表现差异。

Result: 在120个AntMaze配置的实验中，AMLE达到了97.0%的成功率，显著高于调和扩展（58.4%）。随着p值增加，有限p-Laplacian方法的效果也趋近于AMLE（p=8时成功率为97.3%，p=16时为98.2%）。分析表明，AMLE能有效纠正调和扩展在局部决策中产生的错误排序，更符合贪婪路径的最优决策需求。

Conclusion: AMLE（绝对最小Lipschitz扩展）在基于稀疏标签的规划任务中表现优异，优于传统的调和扩展（Harmonic extension）。AMLE通过确保局部动作间隙（action-gap）满足证书要求，能有效保证贪婪路径的成功率。对于图规划中的价值函数传播，p-Laplacian族方法（尤其是高p值或AMLE）能比调和扩展提供更稳健的决策依据。

Abstract: Sparse goal-conditioned planning with few cost-to-go labels can be viewed as a graph-PDE Dirichlet extension problem: extend sparse labels on a goal-dependent boundary to unlabelled graph vertices so that greedy rollouts reach the goal. We study which graph value extensions are planner-admissible under the operational argmin-Q planner. Our main result is a local action-gap certificate: if the surrogate value error along the rollout stays below half the true action gap, then the greedy rollout reaches the goal. Absolutely Minimal Lipschitz Extension (AMLE), the p=infinity endpoint of the graph p-Laplacian family, instantiates this certificate through a comparison-principle fill-distance bound. Harmonic extension, by contrast, can mis-rank local actions because its values reflect boundary hitting probabilities rather than shortest-path greedy order.
  On 120 AntMaze layout-derived graph configurations, harmonic extension achieves 0.584 aggregate rollout success, while AMLE reaches 0.970. Finite high-p methods also enter a high-success regime, with success 0.903 for p=4, 0.973 for p=8, and 0.982 for a fixed-budget p=16 solver, though the p=16 row is not used as a converged endpoint ranking due to incomplete solver certification. Mechanism audits show that many rollout decisions occur in AMLE-compatible but harmonic-incompatible local geometry, and that AMLE corrects most harmonic inversions on the rollout-weighted decision scope.

</details>


### [138] [Worst-Group Equalized Odds Regularization for Multi-Attribute Fair Medical Image Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19214)
*Nikhil Cherian Kurian,Victor Caquilpan Parra,Abin Shoby,Luke Whitbread,Lauren Oakden-Rayner,Robert Vandersluis,Jessica Schrouff,Lyle J. Palmer,Mark Jenkinson*

TL;DR: 针对医疗AI在不同人口统计学群体间诊断不公平的问题，提出了一种正则化方法，通过惩罚偏差最严重的子群体，在不显著降低准确率的情况下，实现了跨多种族、性别等维度下的临床诊断公平性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 医疗人工智能在不同人群中的诊断表现存在系统性差异。传统的AUC指标无法反映临床决策中可能出现的“过度诊断”（部分人群真/假阳性率偏高）与“诊断不足”（部分人群真/假阳性率偏低）问题，这些差异会导致临床医疗不公，因此需要一种能针对推理操作点进行公平性校准的方法。

Method: 提出了一种“最差群体均衡赔率边缘正则化器”（Worst-group equalized-odds margin regularizer）。该方法在训练过程中动态识别在真阳性率和假阳性率边缘上偏差最大的子群体，并对其应用统一惩罚，从而在无需显式交叉约束的情况下，同时跨多个维度（如年龄、性别、种族）优化公平性。

Result: 在两个医学影像多标签数据集上的实验结果表明，该方法在保持模型总体诊断性能（AUC）的同时，有效地降低了不同群体间的“均衡赔率”和“均衡机会”差距，减少了诊断偏差。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的最差群体均衡赔率边缘正则化方法，能够有效解决医疗人工智能在不同人群中诊断行为不一致的问题，在几乎不损失模型整体诊断准确率的前提下，显著提升了医疗决策的公平性。

Abstract: Diagnostic performance in medical AI varies systematically across demographic groups, yet subgroup AUC can mask clinically important disparities. At a fixed inference-time operating point, some groups may exhibit over-diagnostic behaviour, characterized by elevated true and false positive rates, while others show under-diagnostic patterns with reduced true and false positive rates. These opposing tendencies can cancel in aggregate AUCs while producing meaningful inequities in clinical decision-making. Motivated by the need to assess and mitigate such disparities at the operating point and across multiple demographic attributes simultaneously, we propose a worst-group equalized-odds margin regularizer. The proposed regularizer explicitly targets subgroup-level deviations on both the true positive and false positive sides at inference. At each update, the method identifies subgroups defined by explicit demographic attributes (e.g., age, sex, and race) that exhibit the most extreme margin deviations and applies a unified penalty, enabling fairness optimization across multiple demographic axes without requiring explicit intersectional constraints. Across two medical imaging datasets in realistic multi-label settings, our method consistently reduces disparities in Equalized Odds and Equalized Opportunity with minimal impact on AUC, preserving diagnostic performance while improving fairness.

### [139] [DeRegiME: Deep Regime Mixtures for Probabilistic Forecasting under Distribution Shift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19231)
*Kieran Wood,Stefan Zohren,Stephen J. Roberts*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DeRegiME是一种新型深度概率预测模型，通过结合稀疏变分高斯过程与机制混合技术，实现了时间序列均值、残差与噪声的有效分解，在应对复杂的非平稳分布偏移时，显著提升了预测准确度与不确定性量化的质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经预测模型往往忽视残差中的异方差性，且通常的概率预测头无法有效揭示时间序列中隐式的机制结构。在面临突变、渐变或与时段相关的分布偏移时，模型性能受限。作者旨在构建一个能够明确分离潜在不确定性机制、提供可解释的均值-残差-噪声分解，并有效建模非平稳残差结构的概率预测器。

Method: DeRegiME（深度机制混合专家模型）提出了一种直接多时段概率预测方法。它利用稀疏变分高斯过程（GP）作为门控机制，将预测位置软分配给学习到的循环机制；通过具有非平稳机制混合核和Student-t似然的结构，将各机制的子核和噪声过程结合，形成单一的稀疏GP后验，而非传统的专家混合模型。该模型通过Stick-breaking机制实现机制数量的修剪，并结合直接求和特征空间表示，实现均值-残差-噪声的分解。

Result: 在十个数据集及三种编码器配置的基准测试中，DeRegiME表现卓越，其负对数预测密度（NLPD）较最强的基准模型（DeepAR/GluonTS风格的动态Student-t头）提升了20.3%，同时在连续排序概率分数（CRPS）和均方误差（MSE）上分别提升了3.0%和4.7%。实验证明该模型在处理突发、渐进及季节性变化时具有极强的通用性和稳健性。

Conclusion: DeRegiME通过将时间序列分解为可解释的均值、残差和噪声分量，成功捕获了复杂的异方差性和分布偏移。该模型不仅在数学上证明了其核有效性和预测密度的适宜性，还在多个基准测试中展现了优于现有深度概率预测模型的性能，为处理多时段、非平稳时间序列预测提供了一种鲁棒且可解释的新框架。

Abstract: We introduce DeRegiME -- Deep Regime Mixture of Experts -- a direct multi-horizon probabilistic forecaster that separates latent uncertainty regimes from the underlying signal and softly assigns each forecast location to learned recurring regimes using a sparse variational Gaussian process (GP) whose nonstationary regime-mixing kernel and Student-t likelihood combine per-regime sub-kernels and noise processes via a shared gate. This yields a single sparse-GP posterior, not a mixture of GP experts. DeRegiME addresses a key limitation of neural forecasters: point forecasts discard residual uncertainty, and probabilistic heads -- whether single marginals, uninterpreted mixtures, quantile sets, or diffusion samples -- rarely expose the regime structure of the residual. Yet distribution shift in noisy heteroskedastic time series may be abrupt, gradual, or horizon-dependent and often appears in residual uncertainty rather than the conditional mean. DeRegiME yields an interpretable mean-residual-noise decomposition with a direct-sum feature-space representation that anchors regimes as clusters of residual similarity whose transitions surface as implicit changepoints. The effective number of regimes is pruned by the stick-breaking gate. We prove kernel validity and predictive-density propriety, and across ten benchmarks and three encoder grids DeRegiME improves negative log predictive density (NLPD) by 20.3% over the strongest encoder-matched baseline, a DeepAR/GluonTS-style dynamic Student-t head, with parallel gains on CRPS (3.0%) and MSE (4.7%). Improvements are consistent across all datasets, which span abrupt, gradual, and seasonal shifts.

### [140] [GAE Falls Short in Imperfect-Information Self-Play Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19235)
*Zhiyuan Fan,Gabriele Farina*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对自博弈强化学习中因随机策略导致的优势估计方差问题，本文提出了VRPO算法。该算法利用Q-boosting技术通过计算多步动作期望来降低噪声，有效提升了在复杂非完美信息博弈中的训练效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非完美信息博弈的自博弈强化学习中，由于智能体策略的随机性，标准的广义优势估计（GAE）会引入额外的采样方差，且这种方差即便在评价器准确的情况下依然存在，严重制约了算法的训练效率和收敛性能。

Method: 作者提出了一种名为Q-boosting的方差缩减优势估计器。该方法通过集中式动作价值评价器，利用多步Expected SARSA(λ)轨迹取代传统的采样多步备份，在每一步计算动作期望以平滑动作采样带来的噪声，同时保留了PPO的裁剪目标函数和同策略更新机制，从而构建了VRPO算法。

Result: 实验结果表明，VRPO算法在包括“斗地主”和“一对一无限注德州扑克”在内的中大规模非完美信息博弈中，均表现出优于基准算法的鲁棒性和性能。

Conclusion: 本文提出的VRPO算法通过Q-boosting技术有效缓解了多智能体强化学习中由于策略随机性带来的方差问题，为在复杂非完美信息博弈中实现更稳定、高效的策略优化提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: Competitive multi-agent reinforcement learning in imperfect-information games requires agents to act under partial observability and against adversarial opponents, necessitating stochastic policies. While self-play reinforcement learning with Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) has achieved strong empirical success, its standard advantage estimator, generalized advantage estimation, suffers from additional variance due to the sampling of stochastic future actions. This variance is amplified in equilibrium self-play because of the stochastic nature of the equilibrium policy and persists even when the critic is exact. We address this bottleneck by introducing $Q$-boosting, a variance-reduced advantage estimator based on a centralized action-value critic, and propose Variance-Reduced Policy Optimization (VRPO), incorporating this new estimator. The algorithm replaces sampled multi-step backups with a multi-step Expected SARSA$(λ)$ trace, computing policy expectations at each step to average out action-sampling noise, while retaining PPO's clipped objective and on-policy actor updates. Empirically, VRPO consistently achieves strong performance from mid-sized to large-scale games including Dou Dizhu and Heads-Up No-Limit Texas Hold'em.

### [141] [Euclidean Embedding of Data Using Local Distances](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19243)
*Dimitris Arabadjis*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在许多实际应用中，数据往往仅以局部成对距离（如邻域图）的形式存在，而缺乏显式的全局坐标或高维向量表示。现有的嵌入方法通常依赖于预先的特征向量，因此作者旨在开发一种仅基于局部距离图、无需预先表示即可直接恢复全局一致性欧几里得嵌入的方法。

Method: 作者提出了一种基于变分法的框架，将局部图距离与嵌入函数的微分诱导的欧几里得度量进行匹配。推导了坐标无关形式的欧拉-拉格朗日方程，并设计了一种通过迭代更新稀疏线性系统来求解该方程的数值算法，该算法完全依赖于局部邻域图的运算，无需初始特征向量。

Result: 实验结果表明，该算法在合成流形和真实数据集上表现出色，不仅能够精准保留数据的局部度量结构和邻域关系，还能有效逼近全局等距嵌入。与现有方法相比，该算法在无参数设置下展现了较好的稳健性和计算效率。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种无需预先获取数据向量表示的全局一致性欧几里得嵌入方法。该方法通过局部距离图的变分处理，有效地保留了局部度量结构，并能在全局尺度上逼近等距嵌入。它证明了复杂的非线性嵌入问题可以通过迭代求解稀疏线性方程组来高效解决，为流形学习和数据降维提供了一种稳健的无参数框架。

Abstract: We study the problem of recovering a globally consistent Euclidean embedding of data, given only a local distance graph and propose a method that optimally represents these distances. The method operates solely on a neighborhood graph weighted by pairwise distances, without requiring any prior vector representation of the data. The embedding is obtained by solving a variational problem that matches local, on-graph distances to the Euclidean metric, induced by the differentials of the embedding functions. The resulting Euler-Lagrange equations are derived in a coordinate-free form, enabling direct evaluation of all operators from the distance graph alone. Though non-linear and missing an explicit expression for their non-linearity, these equations are shown to be resolved as an iteratively updated sparse linear problem. The main contributions of the proposed approach are (a) the derivation of the functional equations governing the optimal Euclidean embedding in the continuum, (b) a representation-free formulation that requires only a neighborhood distance graph and no feature vectors and (c) an estimation procedure based exclusively on local graph operations. We experimentally evaluate the resulting non-parametric algorithm on synthetic manifolds and real datasets, demonstrating consistent preservation of local metric structure and neighboring relations, while approximating the global isometric embedding.

### [143] [Backdooring Masked Diffusion Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19262)
*Daniel Yiming Cao,Chengzhong Wang,Sheng-Yen Chou,Chengyu Huang,Pin-Yu Chen,Shengwei An*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了针对掩码扩散语言模型（MDLMs）的首个系统性训练阶段后门攻击方案——SHADOWMASK，通过修改模型的前向腐蚀过程，在保持正常文本生成性能的同时，实现了高成功率、高顽强性的恶意后门植入。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管掩码扩散语言模型（MDLMs）在文本生成领域表现出色，但其在训练阶段的安全性尚未得到充分研究。现有的针对高斯扩散模型或自回归模型的后门攻击方法无法直接应用于 MDLMs，因为 MDLMs 采用的是离散状态腐蚀和迭代去噪机制，而非连续噪声处理。

Method: 提出了 SHADOWMASK 攻击框架，通过将标准的“全掩码”终止分布替换为“触发器-掩码混合先验”，建立从触发器腐蚀状态到攻击者指定目标的专用去噪路径。作者还通过数学推导定义了后门前向过程、推导了反向时间后验分布，并给出了连续时间下的训练目标。

Result: 在 DiT 和 LLaDA-8B-Instruct 等模型上的实验表明，SHADOWMASK 实现了近乎 100% 的攻击成功率，性能显著优于传统的数据投毒方式，在保持模型原有性能的同时，对全参数微调和参数高效微调（PEFT）均具有顽强性，且能抵抗现有的主流防御措施。

Conclusion: SHADOWMASK 是一种针对掩码扩散语言模型（MDLMs）的有效且隐蔽的后门攻击方法。该研究表明，通过修改前向腐蚀过程可以实现高成功率的攻击，且现有防御手段难以有效抵御此类攻击，凸显了 MDLM 在训练阶段的脆弱性，为未来开发针对性的防御策略提供了研究基础。

Abstract: Masked diffusion language models (MDLMs) are emerging as a compelling new paradigm for text generation, but their training-time security remains largely unexplored. Existing backdoor attacks on Gaussian diffusion models or autoregressive language models do not directly apply to MDLMs because MDLMs rely on discrete state corruption and iterative denoising rather than continuous noising or left-to-right prediction. In this work, we present the first systematic study of training-time backdoor attacks on MDLMs. We propose SHADOWMASK, a backdoor attack that modifies the MDLM forward corruption process by replacing the standard all-mask terminal distribution with a trigger-mask mixture prior. This creates a dedicated denoising pathway from trigger-corrupted states to attacker-specified targets while preserving clean denoising behavior. We further provide a principled mathematical formulation by defining the backdoored forward process, deriving the reverse-time posterior, and obtaining the continuous-time training objective. Evaluations on DiT-based MDLM and LLaDA-8B-Instruct across WikiText-103, OpenWebText, and Alpaca show that SHADOWMASK achieves near-100% attack success, substantially outperforms standard data poisoning, largely preserves clean utility, remains effective under full-model and parameter-efficient fine-tuning, and is robust against representative defenses.

### [144] [CODA: Rewriting Transformer Blocks as GEMM-Epilogue Programs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19269)
*Han Guo,Jack Zhang,Arjun Menon,Driss Guessous,Vijay Thakkar,Yoon Kim,Tri Dao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对Transformer训练中内存密集型算子导致的性能瓶颈，本文提出了CODA内核抽象。通过将这些算子融合进GEMM的输出处理阶段（epilogue），减少了全局内存访问，在保持高生产力的前提下实现了硬件级的高性能计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Transformer训练中，除矩阵乘法外，大量的内存密集型算子（如归一化、激活函数等）会导致频繁的数据移动，成为系统性能的瓶颈，即使矩阵乘法部分已高度优化，整体训练效率仍受限。

Method: 提出CODA内核抽象，将Transformer中的归一化、激活函数、残差更新等算子重参数化为GEMM的后续处理步骤（epilogue）。通过固定GEMM主循环，并提供一组可组合的元语，使算子在GEMM输出分块驻留在片上缓存（on-chip）时直接完成计算，从而避免了中间结果回写全局内存的开销。

Result: 在多个Transformer工作负载的基准测试中，基于人工编写和LLM辅助生成的CODA内核均表现出了高性能，有效缓解了数据移动瓶颈，验证了该方法在硬件效率与开发便捷性之间的平衡。

Conclusion: CODA证明了将Transformer中的内存密集型算子融合到GEMM（通用矩阵乘法）输出阶段（epilogue）是一种高效的策略，能够显著提升训练效率，并为在保持框架生产力的同时实现硬件极致性能提供了一条可行路径。

Abstract: Transformer training systems are built around dense linear algebra, yet a nontrivial fraction of end-to-end time is spent on surrounding memory-bound operators. Normalization, activations, residual updates, reductions, and related computations repeatedly move large intermediate tensors through global memory while performing little arithmetic, making data movement an increasingly important bottleneck in otherwise highly optimized training stacks. We introduce CODA, a GPU kernel abstraction that expresses these computations as GEMM-plus-epilogue programs. CODA is based on the observation that many Transformer operators exposed as separate framework kernels can be algebraically reparameterized to execute while a GEMM output tile remains on chip, before it is written to memory. The abstraction fixes the GEMM mainloop and exposes a small set of composable epilogue primitives for scaling, reductions, pairwise transformations, and accumulation. This constrained interface preserves the performance structure of expert-written GEMMs while remaining expressive enough to cover nearly all non-attention computation in the forward and backward pass of a standard Transformer block. Across representative Transformer workloads, both human- and LLM-authored CODA kernels achieve high performance, suggesting that GEMM-plus-epilogue programming offers a practical path toward combining framework-level productivity with hardware-level efficiency.

</details>


### [145] [EviTrack: Selection over Sampling for Delayed Disambiguation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19283)
*Omer Haq*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 EviTrack 框架，通过在潜在轨迹层级进行基于证据的选择，而非传统的边缘采样，有效地解决了序列预测中因早期信息模糊导致的决策偏差问题，实现了更可靠的推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于边缘推理的序列预测方法在面对“延迟消歧”（早期观测存在歧义，多种解释共存）场景时，往往会过早陷入局部最优或在后续证据出现时无法有效恢复，导致性能下降。

Method: 提出了名为 EviTrack 的测试时推理框架。该框架不直接处理边缘状态，而是维护一组竞争性的潜在轨迹假设，利用证据和似然比作为选择标准，推迟对单一结论的确定，直到获得足够的数据支持。

Result: 在一个设计好的包含已知潜在真实值的合成基准测试中，在相同推理预算下，EviTrack 的表现显著优于基于采样的基准方法，尤其在消歧后的恢复速度方面具有明显优势。

Conclusion: 在延迟消歧场景中，相比于单纯增加采样覆盖率，采用基于轨迹层级的选择策略能更有效地进行可靠的序列推理，该研究确立了“选择优于采样”的核心原则。

Abstract: Sequential prediction is challenging in regimes of delayed disambiguation, where early observations are ambiguous and multiple latent explanations remain plausible until sufficient evidence accumulates. Standard approaches based on marginal inference struggle in this setting, either collapsing uncertainty prematurely or failing to recover once informative evidence arrives.
  We introduce EviTrack, a test-time inference framework that operates over latent trajectories rather than marginal states. EviTrack maintains a set of competing trajectory hypotheses and applies evidence- and likelihood-ratio-based selection to delay commitment until supported by data, drawing inspiration from hypothesis management in multiple hypothesis tracking and track-before-detect.
  To evaluate this setting, we construct a controlled synthetic benchmark with known latent ground truth that explicitly exhibits delayed disambiguation. At matched inference budget, EviTrack substantially outperforms sampling-based baselines, achieving faster post-disambiguation recovery.
  These results show that, in delayed disambiguation regimes, moderate trajectory-level selection is more effective than increasing sampling coverage, highlighting selection over sampling as a key principle for reliable sequential inference.

</details>


### [146] [An Objective Performance Evaluation of the LSTM Networks in Time Series Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19311)
*Sooraj Sunil,Balakumar Balasingam*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究通过对比实验发现，在结构化的时间序列分类任务中，传统的基于模型的方法（如EM算法）表现优于数据驱动的LSTM模型，且数据驱动模型即便在大规模数据下也难以克服其缺乏结构先验的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管深度学习在时间序列分析中应用广泛，但其在遵循物理规律的结构化环境中，与传统基于模型（Model-based）的方法相比，缺乏客观且定量的性能评估。该论文旨在探究数据驱动模型（LSTM）在这些特定场景下的实际表现上限及局限性。

Method: 构建了一个性能评估框架，对比了LSTM分类器与基于期望最大化（EM）算法的模型驱动分类器。实验基于两种标量线性高斯状态空间模型，通过蒙特卡洛模拟，在任务难度（噪声分离度）、序列长度和训练集大小三个维度上进行客观评估，并以基于真实参数的卡尔曼滤波器似然比检验作为最优基准。

Conclusion: 在结构化环境中，利用先验知识的基于模型的分类器（如EM算法）通常优于数据驱动的深度学习模型（如LSTM）。当数据符合模型假设时，模型驱动方法不仅更高效，且在性能极限上表现更优。LSTM在处理此类问题时存在固有局限，即便增加序列长度或训练数据量也难以弥补其缺乏结构化先验带来的劣势。

Abstract: The rapid adoption of deep learning has increasingly led to data-driven models replacing classical model-based algorithms, even in domains governed by well-understood physical laws. While data-driven models, such as long short-term memory (LSTM) networks, have become a popular choice for time-series analysis, their performance relative to model-based approaches in structured environments is rarely evaluated objectively. This paper presents a performance evaluation framework comparing an LSTM classifier against a model-based expectation maximization (EM) classifier for binary time-series classification. The evaluation is conducted on two scalar linear Gaussian state space models differing only in their noise statistics, where the Kalman filter likelihood ratio test with true parameters serves as a reference for the best achievable classification performance.Through Monte Carlo simulations, the classifiers are evaluated across three axes: task difficulty, controlled by the separation in process or measurement noise between the two models; sequence length; and training dataset size. The results show that the EM classifier, which exploits the known model structure, performs strongly when the data conform to the assumed model class. The LSTM classifier requires a larger separation in noise statistics to achieve reliable classification, and its performance saturates below the reference classifier when the models differ only in measurement noise, regardless of sequence length or training dataset size.

### [147] [Inference-Time Scaling in Diffusion Models through Iterative Partial Refinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19317)
*Taegu Kang,Jaesik Yoon,Sungjin Ahn*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 IPR 的扩散模型推理时扩展方法。它通过在推理过程中迭代式地局部重采样与优化，无需外部验证器即可显著提升模型在处理全局约束任务时的性能与一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有扩散模型的推理时扩展通常依赖于外部验证器或奖励模型进行采样评估，这限制了其适用范围。此外，针对序列化、区域混合噪声条件的推理时扩展研究尚不充分。因此，作者旨在探索一种无需额外监督、能提升全局一致性的推理时扩展策略。

Method: 提出了一种迭代局部细化（Iterative Partial Refinement, IPR）方法。该方法在初始样本生成后，通过对部分区域进行加噪并基于剩余区域提供的丰富上下文进行重生成，从而在无外部评价模型的情况下修正早期决策，实现推理时的迭代优化。

Result: 在需要满足全局约束的推理任务（如 MNIST 数独）中，IPR 表现优异，有效解率从 55.8% 提升至 75.0%，验证了该方法在序列化混合噪声设定下的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文证明了在序列化扩散模型中，无需外部验证器，仅通过迭代局部细化（IPR）即可有效实现推理时扩展。该方法通过在推理阶段利用更丰富的上下文重采样部分区域，能显著提高模型在全局约束推理任务中的表现。

Abstract: Inference-time scaling has emerged as a major approach for improving reasoning capabilities, and has been increasingly applied to diffusion models. However, existing inference-time scaling methods for diffusion models typically rely on external verifiers or reward models to rank and select samples, limiting their scalability to settings where such evaluators are available and reliable. Moreover, while recent diffusion models perform sequential inference with region-wise, mixed-noise conditioning, inference-time scaling tailored to this setting remains relatively underexplored. We propose Iterative Partial Refinement (IPR), an inference-time scaling method for sequential diffusion that requires no external verifier. Starting from an already-generated sample, IPR re-noises a subset of regions and regenerates them conditioned on the remaining regions, enabling the model to revise earlier decisions under a richer context than was available during the initial generation. This iterative partial refinement produces more globally consistent samples without external verification. On reasoning tasks requiring global constraint satisfaction, IPR consistently improves performance: on MNIST Sudoku, the valid solution rate increases from 55.8% to 75.0%. These results show that iterative partial refinement alone can serve as an effective inference-time scaling strategy for diffusion models in sequential, mixed-noise settings. Code is available at: https://github.com/ahn-ml/IPR

### [148] [An Exterior Method for Nonnegative Matrix Factorization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19325)
*Qiujing Lu,Tonmoy Monsoor,Ehsan Ebrahimzadeh,Kartik Sharma,Vwani Roychowdhury*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 作者提出了一种创新的外部优化框架（eNMF）来解决非负矩阵分解问题，通过将低秩近似与约束分离，显著提升了算法的收敛速度、精度以及对复杂数据的处理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的非负矩阵分解（NMF）方法通常在优化过程中通过内点法强制执行非负约束，这往往会限制搜索空间，导致收敛缓慢或陷入次优平稳点。作者旨在克服这些因约束驱动而带来的优化障碍。

Method: 提出了一种外部优化框架（eNMF），其核心在于将低秩近似与非负性约束强制分离。方法首先在无约束条件下进行因式分解，随后引入一种旋转过程，将无约束因子映射到最接近非负象限的外部点，并通过简单的迭代更新收敛至满足 KKT 条件的平稳点。

Result: eNMF 在 400 次实验中表现卓越，与 9 种主流算法和 9 种初始化方案对比，在 3 个真实数据集和 2 个合成数据集上均表现更优；在等时条件下重构误差降低高达 30%，在等误差条件下速度提升高达 150%，并在音频处理和推荐系统任务中验证了其实际应用性能。

Conclusion: eNMF 通过将低秩近似与非负约束分离，不仅在理论上为 NMF 提供了一种几何解释，在实践中也显著提升了收敛速度和精度，优于现有的多种主流算法，证明了外部优化框架在处理非凸 NMF 问题上的有效性。

Abstract: Nonnegative matrix factorization (NMF) seeks a low-rank approximation $X \approx UV^T$ with nonnegative factors and is commonly solved using interior methods that enforce feasibility throughout optimization. We show that such constraint-driven approaches can impede progress in the nonconvex landscape, leading to slow convergence or convergence to suboptimal stationary points. We propose an exterior framework for NMF (eNMF) that separates low-rank approximation from nonnegativity enforcement. Our method initializes from the optimal unconstrained factorization and introduces a rotation procedure that maps unconstrained factors to an exterior point closest to the nonnegative orthant. This viewpoint yields an algorithmic framework in which simple iterative updates converge to KKT-satisfying stationary points on the boundary of the positive orthant. The exterior formulation also enables a geometric interpretation of NMF solutions, clarifying equivalence classes of factorizations under permutation and orthogonal transformations. An intriguing numerical result, involving 400 NMF experiments across both real and synthetic datasets, show that in 99% of the cases, different algorithms tend to converge towards equivalent factor matrices. We benchmark eNMF against 9 state-of-the-art NMF algorithms with 9 initialization schemes across 3 real-world and 2 synthetic datasets. eNMF consistently outperforms all 81 competitors, achieving up to 30% lower reconstruction error under equal-time settings and up to 150% speedup under equal-error settings. The downstream experiments further demonstrate substantial performance gains in audio processing and recommendation tasks, corroborating the practical benefits of the proposed exterior optimization framework. Code is available at https://github.com/roychowdhuryresearch/eNMF

### [150] [The Evaluation Game: Beyond Static LLM Benchmarking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19377)
*Paul Wang,Jade Garcia-Bourrée,Anne-Marie Kermarrec,Vincent Corruble*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过博弈论与群论框架揭示了LLM微调防御的局限性：现有的安全微调往往仅实现局部泛化，呈现出“打补丁”式的特征，而非真正提升鲁棒性。评估模型安全性时，必须将动态对抗过程纳入考量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型（LLM）jailbreak攻击手段的不断演进，微调成为了主流防御策略，但目前缺乏对其鲁棒性底层机制的理论研究。现有评估方法往往忽视了训练者与评估者之间的动态对抗过程，难以判断模型防御的真实有效性。

Method: 1. 构建博弈论框架：将评估者（寻找jailbreak）与训练者（微调模型防御）的互动建模为二人博弈。
2. 引入群论：利用群作用（Group Actions）形式化描述数据增强，分析训练者在不同泛化范围下的行为表现。
3. 实证分析：对Llama、Qwen和Mistral模型进行实验，通过分析拒绝率与对抗提示词距离之间的相关性，验证模型微调的“局部泛化”特性。

Result: 1. 理论发现：在低于临界阈值的泛化范围内，评估者能够持续发现漏报，揭示了微调防御的局限性。
2. 实证结论：针对Llama、Qwen和Mistral的测试显示，微调防御表现出显著的“局部依赖性”，即模型对测试样本的拒绝能力与其距离训练对抗提示词的距离高度相关。
3. 框架意义：提出基准测试集应被视为评估者群作用下的“轨道（orbit）”，而非静态集合。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种基于博弈论和群论的框架来理解LLM的安全性防御，揭示了微调防御在本质上往往是局部的、易于被绕过的“打补丁”行为，而非根本性的鲁棒性提升。作者强调，在评估安全性时，必须考虑防御者（训练者）的动态适应性，否则静态基准测试无法区分模型是“学会了安全”还是“记住了规避路径”。

Abstract: As jailbreaks, adversarially crafted inputs that bypass safety constraints, continue to be discovered in Large Language Models, practitioners increasingly rely on fine-tuning as a defensive strategy. Yet the theoretical foundations underlying this robustness fine-tuning remain underexplored. We introduce a game-theoretic framework in which the interaction between an evaluator (auditing the model for jailbreaks) and a trainer is formalized as a two-player game.
  A key feature of our approach is the use of group actions, a mathematical structure that captures symmetries and transformations, to formally represent data augmentation. The simplest non-trivial instance is the circle with cyclic translation groups, where we exhibit various regimes depending on the trainer's generalization range. Below a critical threshold, the evaluator maintains a constant miss ratio for linearly many rounds, whereas other settings can yield very different behaviors. We further provide empirical evidence supporting locality-dependence of the model: for the three model families we tested (Llama, Qwen and Mistral), we have significant evidence that fine-tuning on adversarial prompts induces only local generalization, with refusal rates on test examples highly correlated with the distance to the fine-tuning prompts. Our framework recasts the central object of adversarial evaluation: a benchmark is not a static set of prompts but an orbit under the evaluator's group action, and audit protocols that ignore trainer-side adaptation cannot distinguish a genuine fix from a memorized patch.

*Lihong Lin,Haidong Kang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于常微分方程（ODE）的模型合并方法（ODE-M），通过在参数空间中沿低损失路径演化模型来解决持续学习中的灾难性遗忘问题，实现了比传统静态代数合并方法更优的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的持续模型合并（CMM）方法缺乏对学习容量分配的显式控制，导致在处理异构任务时出现严重的遗忘问题。作者指出根本原因在于现有方法仅进行静态代数运算，未考虑到模型在参数空间中的连通性（Mode Connectivity）。

Method: 提出了 ODE-M（ODE-driven Merging）方法。该方法将模型合并过程建模为在参数空间中沿着低损失路径演化的 ODE（常微分方程），通过积分随时间变化的向量场，并施加屏障约束以防止进入高损失区域，从而在处理序列任务时保持模型性能。

Result: 在主流的 CMM 基准测试中，ODE-M 显著优于现有的模型合并方法，表现出最先进的性能，验证了该方法在减少遗忘和提升持续学习能力方面的有效性。

Conclusion: ODE-M 通过引入基于模态连接性的 ODE 框架，有效地解决了持续模型合并中的灾难性遗忘问题，并为实现更可控、更高效的模型增量学习提供了新的理论与技术范式。

Abstract: Continual Model Merging (CMM) enables rapid customization of foundation models across sequentially arriving tasks, offering a scalable alternative to repeated retraining. However, existing merging rules lack explicit controllability over the allocation of learning capacity between previously learned capabilities and newly merged models. Consequently, as tasks are merged sequentially, this deficiency accumulates into severe forgetting, particularly in scenarios with heterogeneous task importance, where performance allocation becomes highly inconsistent. The key reason can be attributed to the fact that previous methods treat each task model as an isolated parameter point and apply fixed algebraic combinations, rather than explicitly constructing a transition that respects how independently trained models can be connected in parameter space. Motivated by mode connectivity, we assume that desirable merged models lie on low loss connecting paths, and that continual merging should follow such paths without crossing loss barriers that induce forgetting. Grounded in these insights, we propose a novel ODE-driven Merging (ODE-M) tailored for CMM that traces such a path by integrating a time-dependent velocity field and enforcing barrier constraints to prevent loss-increasing steps. Extensive experiments demonstrate that ODE-M achieves state-of-the-art performance compared to its competitors across mainstream CMM benchmarks.

### [153] [When to Stop Reusing: Dynamic Gradient Gating for Sample-Efficient RLVR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19425)
*Yuchun Miao,Sen Zhang,Yuqi Zhang,Yaorui Shi,Qi Gu,Xunliang Cai,Lefei Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对 LLM 强化学习中样本重用导致的性能下降问题，发现了关键预警信号——lm_head 权重梯度异常，并据此提出了“动态梯度门控（DGG）”技术，显著提升了训练的样本效率与速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大型语言模型（LLM）的强化学习验证奖励（RLVR）任务中，获取样本成本极高，但现有的样本重用策略（即多次梯度更新）会引发严重的策略偏移导致性能恶化。研究旨在解决这一样本效率瓶颈，并寻找一种检测和防止此类性能退化的早期预警机制。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为“动态梯度门控（DGG）”的方法。该方法基于作者发现的“权值比例差异（DWD）”现象，即性能退化与 lm_head 权重变化的剧烈波动同步。DGG 在训练过程中实时监控 lm_head 的梯度范数，一旦检测到异常的梯度波动，便拦截该更新，从而防止有害梯度破坏模型参数。

Result: 实验表明，DGG 方法在数学、ALFWorld、WebShop 及搜索增强型问答任务中表现出色，在保持或超越单次使用样本基准的同时，实现了高达 2.93 倍的样本效率提升和 2.14 倍的训练速度加速。此外，理论分析证明了 lm_head 的梯度范数是策略偏离的有效度量指标。

Conclusion: 本文提出的动态梯度门控（DGG）机制通过监控 lm_head 的梯度范数，成功解决了强化学习中多次重用样本导致的策略偏移与性能退化问题，为提高大语言模型推理任务的样本效率提供了一种兼顾稳定性与速度的有效解决方案。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has become the dominant paradigm for advanced reasoning in Large Language Models (LLMs), but rollout samples are expensive to obtain, making sample efficiency a critical bottleneck. A natural remedy is to reuse each rollout batch for multiple gradient updates, a standard practice in classical RL. Yet in RLVR, this amplifies policy shift, leading to severe performance degradation. Detecting the onset of degradation early enough to stop reuse remains an open and challenging problem. We close this gap by identifying the \textit{Disproportionate Weight Divergence (DWD)} phenomenon: performance degradation is synchronized with a sharp surge in the \texttt{lm\_head} weight change, while intermediate layers remain stable. Empirically, we verify that DWD emerges consistently across diverse LLMs and tasks. Theoretically, we prove that (i) harmful gradients concentrate at the \texttt{lm\_head} while intermediate layers are structurally attenuated, and (ii) the \texttt{lm\_head} gradient norm lower-bounds the policy divergence. These results establish the \texttt{lm\_head} gradient norm as a principled, real-time signal of catastrophic policy shift. Guided by this insight, we propose \textit{Dynamic Gradient Gating (DGG)}, a lightweight intervention that monitors the \texttt{lm\_head} gradient norm in real time and intercepts harmful gradients before they corrupt the optimizer. DGG consistently matches or exceeds the standard single-use baseline, achieving up to $2.93\times$ sample efficiency and $2.14\times$ wall-clock speedup across math, ALFWorld, WebShop, and search-augmented QA tasks.

</details>

*Hongxiang Lin,Zhirui Kuai,Erpeng Xue,Lei Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对现有测试时强化学习（TTRL）导致模型丢失正确推理信号的问题，本文提出了 TTRL-Guard 框架，通过引入翻转率感知、保留少数派信号及稀疏更新机制，有效克服了学习过程中的“正确答案灭绝”现象，显著提升了数学推理性能。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者提出了 TTRL-Guard 框架，包含三个核心机制：1. 翻转率感知奖励缩放（FRS）：根据翻转率降低风险更新权重；2. 保留少数样本采样（MPS）：保护少数派正确答案的梯度信号；3. 风险条件稀疏更新（RCSU）：针对两极分化的题目暂停更新，以防止模型陷入错误答案。

Conclusion: 研究表明，现有的测试时强化学习（TTRL）在数学推理任务中的性能提升存在系统性误读，且存在“正确答案灭绝窗口”问题。提出的 TTRL-Guard 框架通过保护极少数正确答案信号和动态调整更新策略，能有效提升模型的数学推理能力，证明了精细化的学习机制优于单纯的伪标签强化。

Abstract: Test-time reinforcement learning (TTRL) reports substantial accuracy gains on mathematical reasoning benchmarks using majority vote as a pseudo-label signal. We argue these gains are systematically misinterpreted: most reflect sharpening of already-solvable problems rather than genuine learning, while problems corrupted from correct to incorrect outnumber truly learned ones, and this damage is irreversible once majority vote locks onto a wrong answer. Per-problem tracking reveals that correct-answer signals in low-ability problems are briefly active before being permanently suppressed, a phenomenon we term the \textit{Correct-Answer Extinction Window}, with Flip Rate (FR) as its leading indicator. We thus propose \textbf{TTRL-Guard}, a lightweight framework with three mechanisms targeting the extinction window: Flip-Rate-Aware Reward Scaling (FRS) down-weights at-risk updates as FR declines, Minority-Preserving Sampling (MPS) retains gradient signal from minority correct answers, and Risk-Conditioned Sparse Updatings (RCSU) suspends updates on polarized problems. Experiments across three models and four benchmarks show that TTRL-Guard achieves the best average pass@1 on Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct and Qwen3-4B, improves relatively over TTRL by +54\% on AIME 2025. \footnote{Our code and implementation details are available at https://github.com/linhxkkkk/TTRL-Guard.

Conclusion: 该研究表明时间序列的表征效用并非普适，而是受到精度-不变性权衡的制约。预训练带来的收益高度依赖于下游任务对信号分辨率的需求。此外，表征质量与数据来源相关性较低，且在适度架构深度下趋于饱和，这为通过大规模合成数据进行扩展提供了新方向。

Abstract: The success of self-supervised learning (SSL) in vision and NLP has motivated its rapid adoption for time series. We establish a controlled framework to evaluate the "pre-training dividend": the value added by SSL across diverse temporal tasks. We systematically compare Generative paradigms against Latent Alignment architectures, introducing adaptations of LeJEPA and DINO for time series. These adaptations utilize Discrete Wavelet Transform (DWT) augmentations to enforce invariance to local fluctuations. Our analysis reveals that the pre-training dividend is highly asymmetric: SSL yields gains of up to 375% for anomaly detection and classification, yet remains marginal for forecasting. We demonstrate that representational utility is non-universal, governed by a precision-invariance trade-off where the specific signal resolution required by the task must align with the objective. Finally, we show that representation quality is largely independent of data origin and saturates at moderate architectural depths, suggesting a path to scaling via massive synthetic generation. ### [156] [Adynamical systems view of training generativemodels and the memorization phenomenon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19483)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 证明了生成模型在恒定步长SGD训练下，由于损失函数对变量依赖的差异导致双时间尺度动力学，进而引发模型崩溃与记忆现象的产生。该研究明确了生成模型训练动态与模型输出稳定性之间的数学关系。

Abstract: Using recent works of one of the authors (VSB) on collapse in generative models and two time scale dynamics in stochastic gradient descent in high dimensions, we give a system theoretic explanation of the memorization phenomenon in generative models. This relies purely on the dynamic aspects of the training phase. Specifically, we use a result of Austin [2016] to motivate a stylized model for the loss function for stochastic gradient descent (SGD) wherein the loss function has a strong dependence on some variables and weak dependence on the rest in a precise sense. This naturally leads to two distinct time scales in the constant step size SGD that is commonly used in machine learning. This fact has been used to explain the double descent phenomenon in SGD in Borkar [2026]. In conjunction with a mathematical model for collapse phenomenon in SGD developed in Borkar [2025a], we analyze the constant step size SGD using the recent results of Azizian et al. [2024] in order to explain the phenomenon of memorization wherein a generative model that is concurrently being tuned yields the same or similar outputs for significant stretches of time. This gives a novel perspective on the aforementioned phenomena reported in machine learning literature and their interrelationships, using a dynamical systems viewpoint.

### [157] [The Silent Hyperparameter: Quantifying the Impact of Inference Backends on LLM Reproducibility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19537)
*David Pape,Jonathan Evertz,Lea Schönherr*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 大模型的基准测试分数不仅取决于模型本身，还受到推理引擎底层技术实现（如算子优化、计算图调度）的显著影响。仅因后端差异即可造成高达16.6%的评分波动，研究建议将推理技术栈纳入评估标准并进行透明化汇报。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大模型基准测试的性能提升往往以百分之一甚至更小的幅度衡量，但现代推理引擎在执行模型时所采用的底层优化（如自定义CUDA内核、低精度运算等）可能引入非确定性，从而导致输出结果的偏差。目前学界普遍忽视了推理技术栈对基准测试结果的潜在影响。

Method: 研究人员首先调查了200个推理引擎和35,000篇机器学习论文，随后开展了系统性实证研究。在保持模型权重、解码参数和硬件环境不变的前提下，对比了vLLM、SGLang、llama.cpp等5种主流推理引擎在多个模型和基准测试上的表现，并追踪了执行流水线以定位导致结果差异的系统级优化手段。

Result: 研究发现，仅更换推理后端就可能导致基准测试分数产生高达16.6个百分点的差异，并引发高比例的输出不一致。导致这种分歧的核心原因在于前缀缓存（prefix caching）、CUDA图（CUDA graphs）、自定义内核以及引擎特有的Logit处理默认设置等系统级优化。

Conclusion: 研究表明，推理后端是LLM评估中一个未被重视但影响巨大的“超参数”。为了提高大模型基准测试的复现性与可解释性，研究者呼吁在学术报告中必须标准化地披露推理技术栈信息。

Abstract: Progress in LLMs is increasingly measured through standardized benchmarks, where state-of-the-art improvements are often separated by fractions of a percentage point. At the same time, the computational cost of evaluating modern LLMs has driven widespread adoption of specialized inference backends, software systems that execute trained models efficiently at inference time. While critical for scalability, system-level optimizations, such as custom CUDA kernels and reduced-precision arithmetic, can alter token probabilities and introduce non-determinism, possibly cascading into divergent generation. In this work, we first survey the inference landscape, identifying 200 distinct engines, and analyze 35,000 ML publications, finding that the specific inference stack is rarely reported despite this widespread diversity. We then present a systematic empirical study of how inference backends affect LLM benchmark results. Holding model weights, decoding parameters, and hardware constant, we evaluate five widely used inference engines, including vLLM, SGLang, and llama.cpp, across multiple open-weight models and established benchmarks. We show that the choice of backend alone can shift benchmark scores by up to 16.6 percentage points and induce high rates of output disagreement. By isolating backend optimizations and tracing the execution pipeline, we find this divergence is driven by system-level optimizations like prefix caching and CUDA graphs, custom kernels, and engine-specific defaults in logit processing. Our findings identify the inference backend as a previously unreported but consequential hyperparameter in the evaluation of LLM and advocate standardized reporting of inference stacks to improve the reproducibility and interpretability of benchmark comparisons.

### [158] [TORQ: Two-Level Orthogonal Rotation for MXFP4 Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19561)
*Zukang Xu,Xing Hu,Dawei Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对MXFP4在大模型激活量化中的精度下降问题，该论文提出了一种无需训练的TORQ框架，通过块间与块内两级正交旋转优化激活分布，显著提升了4-bit低位宽推理的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MXFP4格式虽能平衡硬件效率与动态范围，但在直接用于LLM激活值量化时会导致显著的精度损失。其核心原因在于激活值分布与MXFP4块浮点格式之间的结构性不匹配，具体表现为极端的块间方差失衡和块内码本利用率失衡。

Method: 提出了TORQ（两级正交旋转）方法：1. 宏观层面：利用舒尔-霍恩定理（Schur-Horn theorem）进行块间正交旋转，重新分配激活能量，减小块间方差差异；2. 微观层面：采用最大熵引导的块内正交旋转，以优化码本利用率，防止码本崩溃。该方案无需额外训练，属于后训练量化（PTQ）范畴。

Result: 在LLaMA3和Qwen3等主流大模型上的实验表明，TORQ显著提升了MXFP4激活量化的精度。例如，在Qwen3-32B上，通过TORQ处理后，准确率从直接舍入（RTN）的38.40%大幅提升至73.63%，非常接近BF16全精度（74.82%）。

Conclusion: TORQ框架通过在宏观和微观两个层面进行正交旋转变换，有效解决了MXFP4在量化大模型激活值时的结构失衡问题。该方法作为一种无需训练的PTQ方案，极大地缩小了4-bit浮点量化与全精度推理之间的性能差距，为低位宽推理部署提供了高效可靠的解决方案。

Abstract: As Large Language Models (LLMs) advance toward practical deployment, the Microscaling FP4 (MXFP4) format has emerged as a cornerstone for next-generation low-bit inference, owing to its ability to balance high dynamic range with hardware efficiency. However, directly applying MXFP4 to LLM activation quantization inevitably leads to significant accuracy degradation. In this paper, we theoretically analyze the error structure of MXFP4 activation quantization, revealing that the root cause of this performance drop lies in two structural imbalances between activation distributions and the MXFP4 block floating-point format: (1) extreme inter-block variance imbalance and (2) intra-block codebook utilization imbalance. To address these challenges, we propose TORQ (Two-level Orthogonal Rotation for MXFP4 Quantization), a training-free Post-Training Quantization (PTQ) framework designed to reshape the geometric properties of the activation space through optimal coordinate transformations. At the macroscopic level, TORQ leverages the Schur-Horn theorem to redistribute activation energy via inter-block orthogonal rotation, preventing high-variance blocks from driving up shared scaling factors and thereby preserving the precision of small-magnitude elements. At the microscopic level, TORQ employs maximum-entropy-guided intra-block rotation to alleviate codebook collapse and maximize the MXFP4 codebook's information capacity. Experiments on mainstream LLMs such as LLaMA3 and Qwen3 show that TORQ significantly improves the accuracy of MXFP4 activation quantization compared to existing methods: on Qwen3-32B, the perplexity on WikiText is reduced to 8.43 (vs. 7.61 for BF16), and the average accuracy increases from 38.40% with direct RTN to 73.63% (vs. 74.82% for BF16), substantially narrowing the gap between 4-bit floating-point quantization and full-precision inference.

</details>


### [159] [Online Market Making and the Value of Observing the Order Book](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19584)
*Davide Maran,Marcello Restelli*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在线做市问题，提出了一种利用订单簿“未成交信息”的动作依赖反馈模型。研究证明该模型能显著优化学习效率，并在随机、均值回归和对抗性市场环境下，分别实现了高效的遗憾界保障。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的在线做市学习模型通常假设反馈完全被遮蔽（完全置信度反馈）。然而，在现实的限价订单簿（LOB）中，未成交的订单往往能提供有关市场供需的宝贵信息。本文旨在探究这种“动作依赖反馈”如何改变学习性能，并打破传统多臂老虎机反馈模型的局限。

Method: 1. 引入动作依赖的反馈模型：当交易未发生时提供有关供需的额外信息；
2. 随机环境：提出一种基于消除（elimination-based）的算法，实现高概率的 O(√T) 遗憾界；
3. 均值回归环境：通过新的集中不等式处理局部自回归及全局漂移条件，实现 O(√T) 遗憾界；
4. 对抗环境：设计“探索后扰动”（explore-then-perturb）算法，实现期望 O(T^2/3) 遗憾界。

Result: 1. 在随机设置下，无需对交易者估值分布做平滑性假设，实现了 O(√T) 的遗憾界；
2. 在均值回归模型中，通过新的集中不等式，成功处理了复杂的市场动态，证明了 O(√T) 的遗憾界；
3. 在对抗性市场条件下，实现了 O(T^2/3) 的期望遗憾界；
4. 证明了订单簿反馈能显著改善在线做市的后悔度保障。

Conclusion: 该研究通过引入动作依赖的反馈模型，证明了在订单簿场景下，即使反馈是不完全的，也能显著提升在线做市的性能。该工作不仅为处理不同市场动态（随机、均值回归及对抗性）提供了算法框架，还量化了订单簿反馈对于降低遗憾值的核心价值。

Abstract: We study an online market-making problem in which a learner sequentially posts bid and ask prices for a single asset while interacting with traders holding private valuations. Unlike existing online learning formulations that assume fully censored feedback, we introduce an action-dependent feedback model inspired by real limit order books: when a trade occurs, the trader's valuation remains hidden, whereas when no trade occurs, informative feedback about supply and demand is revealed.
  We show that this additional information fundamentally changes the learnability of the problem. In the stochastic setting with i.i.d. market prices, we propose an elimination-based algorithm that achieves $O(\sqrt T)$ regret with high probability, without requiring any smoothness assumptions on the distribution of trader valuations. We then extend this result to a broad class of mean-reverting price processes by considering both local, autoregressive dynamics and a weaker global drift condition based on cumulative deviations from the mean. Under either assumption, we establish high-probability $O(\sqrt T)$ regret bounds, relying on a new concentration inequality of independent interest. Finally, in the adversarial setting with oblivious prices, we design an explore-then-perturb algorithm that guarantees $O(T^{2/3})$ regret in expectation.
  Our results quantify the value of observing the order book in online market making and demonstrate that even limited, action-dependent feedback can substantially improve regret guarantees compared to standard bandit feedback models.

</details>


### [160] [MiMuon: Mixed Muon Optimizer with Improved Generalization for Large Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19619)
*Feihu Huang,Yuning Luo,Songcan Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对Muon优化器泛化理论缺失的问题，本文推导了其泛化误差界，并提出了改良的MiMuon优化器，在维持原有的高效收敛速度的同时，实现了更优的泛化性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Muon优化器在矩阵结构参数优化中表现出更快的收敛速度，但其泛化性能在理论上尚不明确。研究者旨在通过理论分析量化Muon的泛化误差，并探索提升其泛化能力的方法。

Method: 1. 基于算法稳定性和数学归纳法，推导Muon优化器的泛化误差；2. 提出MiMuon（Mixed Muon）优化器，通过将Muon与基于动量的SGD结合（谨慎使用梯度正交化）来降低泛化误差；3. 对MiMuon进行收敛性分析，并与Muon进行对比。

Result: 1. 证明了Muon的泛化误差为 $O(1/N\kappa^T)$；2. 证明了MiMuon将泛化误差降低至 $O(1/N)$；3. 证明了MiMuon保持了与Muon相同的收敛速率 $O(1/T^{1/4})$；4. 在Qwen3-0.6B和YOLO26m等大规模模型实验中验证了MiMuon的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文通过理论分析确立了Muon优化器的泛化误差界，并提出了MiMuon优化器，在保持收敛速度不变的前提下，通过混合策略显著提升了泛化性能。实验验证了MiMuon在大型模型训练中的有效性。

Abstract: Matrix-structured parameters frequently appear in many artificial intelligence models such as large language models. More recently, an efficient Muon optimizer is designed for matrix parameters of large-scale models, and shows markedly faster convergence than the vector-wise algorithms. Although some works have begun to study convergence properties (i.e., optimization error) of the Muon optimizer, its generalization properties (i.e., generalization error) is still not established. Thus, in this paper, we study generalization error of the Muon optimizer based on algorithmic stability and mathematical induction, and prove that the Muon has a generalization error of $O\big(\frac{1}{Nκ^{T}}\big)$, where $N$ is training sample size, and $T$ denotes iteration number, and $κ>0$ denotes minimum difference between singular values of gradient estimate. To enhance generalization of the Muon, we propose an effective mixed Muon (MiMuon) optimizer by cautiously using orthogonalization of gradient, which is a hybrid of Muon and momentum-based SGD optimizers. Then we prove that our MiMuon optimizer has a lower generalization error of $O\big(\frac{1}{N}\big)$ than $O\big(\frac{1}{Nκ^{T}}\big)$ of Muon optimizer, since $κ$ generally is very small. Meanwhile, we also studied the convergence properties of our MiMuon algorithm, and prove that our MiMuon algorithm has the same convergence rate of $O(\frac{1}{T^{1/4}})$ as the Muon algorithm. Some numerical experimental results on training large models including Qwen3-0.6B and YOLO26m demonstrate efficiency of the MiMuon optimizer.
