### [161] [Optimal Reconstruction from Linear Queries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19625)
*Yuval Filmus,Shay Moran,Elizaveta Nesterova*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了从近似线性查询中重建高维空间中未知点的理论极限，通过推广荣格定理，揭示了查询次数、维度与误差之间的指数级收敛关系，为高维数据恢复提供了核心理论支撑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在定量表征从近似线性查询中重建未知点时的最优误差，解决遥感、信号恢复及隐私数据分析等领域中关于重建精度与查询次数、维度及噪声水平之间相互作用的理论问题。

Method: 利用几何与动力系统方法，将经典的荣格定理（Jung's theorem）推广至鲁棒版本。通过对称性分析和李群作用，推导了最优重建误差的界限，并分析了查询次数、维度与噪声之间的函数关系。

Result: 确定了查询次数趋于无穷大时的最优误差极限为 $\sqrt{2d/(d+1)} δ$；证明了在维度固定时，超额误差呈双指数衰减；确定了在高维情况下，实现消失误差所需的查询数量级为 $\exp(d)$；并探讨了不适当重建（improper reconstruction）的变体。

Conclusion: 该研究通过推广荣格定理（Jung's theorem），建立了线性查询重建问题的理论极限。研究表明，在固定维度下，重建误差以双指数速率收敛；而在高维情形下，查询数量需呈指数级增长才能使超额误差趋于零，为理解高维数据恢复的理论复杂性提供了重要基准。

Abstract: We study the problem of reconstructing an unknown point in $\mathbb{R}^d$ from approximate linear queries. This setting arises naturally in applications ranging from low-dimensional remote sensing and signal recovery to high-dimensional data analysis and privacy-sensitive inference. Our main goal is to characterize the optimal reconstruction error as a function of the number of queries $T$, the ambient dimension $d$, and the noise parameter $δ$.
  We first analyze the limit $T \to \infty$ and show that the optimal reconstruction error converges to the explicit value $\sqrt{2d/(d+1)} δ$, which plays a role analogous to the Bayes optimal error in supervised learning. When the dimension is fixed, we show that the excess error above this limit decays doubly exponentially fast as $T \to \infty$, a rate that is significantly faster than those typically encountered in learning curves. When the dimension grows, we show that a number of queries on the order of $\exp(d)$ is necessary and sufficient to achieve vanishing excess error. Finally, we introduce and analyze an improper variant of the reconstruction problem.
  From a technical perspective, our main contribution is a generalization of Jung's theorem (1901). The classical theorem bounds the maximum possible radius of a set of diameter 1 and characterizes extremal bodies. Our generalization provides a robust variant that characterizes near-extremal bodies and is proved via geometric and dynamical arguments exploiting symmetry and Lie group actions.

Abstract: Accurately identifying metabolites i.e. small molecules from mass spectrometry data remains a core challenge in metabolomics, with broad applications in drug discovery, environmental analysis, and clinical research. We address the Molecule Retrieval task, which consists in recovering the chemical structure of a metabolite from its MS/MS spectrum given a set of candidate molecules. While the recent release of benchmark datasets such as MassSpecGym and Spectraverse has considerably accelerated the development of novel machine learning approaches, the complexity of data preprocessing pipelines and the lack of unified implementations make methods and results difficult to reproduce and compare. We make three contributions. First, we propose a unified framework encompassing recent approaches based on representation alignment and contrastive learning. Second, we introduce MSAlign, inspired by multimodal alignment in vision-language models, which learns a shared representation space by aligning two frozen foundation models (DreaMS for mass spectra and ChemBERTa for molecules) through lightweight MLP projections trained with a candidate-based contrastive objective. MSAlign is simple to implement, fast to train and consistently outperforms existing approaches across all benchmarks. Third, we investigate a long-standing evaluation problem: data splitting strategies in molecule retrieval implicitly trade off data leakage against domain shift. We formalize this tension by introducing a quantitative measure of distribution shift, and use it to evaluate splitting strategies in existing benchmarks. All datasets, splits, candidate sets, and a unified implementation of MSAlign and baselines are publicly released to support reproducible research.

### [163] [AR1-ZO: Topology-Aware Rank-1 Zeroth-Order Queries for High-Rank LoRA Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19767)
*Ziye Chen,Hongbin Lin,Chenyu Zhang,Xiangda Yan,Yongjie Yang,Yao Shu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对零阶优化LoRA微调中的秩悖论，本文引入AR1-ZO算法，通过原子级更新和拓扑感知缩放，实现了在不增加额外计算代价的前提下，对高秩LoRA进行稳定且高效的训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在零阶优化中结合LoRA微调时存在“秩悖论”：增加LoRA的秩会降低有限差分信号的信噪比，导致模型在更新时出现方向性坍塌，限制了高秩LoRA的性能发挥。

Method: 提出AR1-ZO算法，将LoRA参数分解为匹配的秩1原子进行独立查询，并引入拓扑感知缩放（scaling factor γ=αr）来补偿有限差分信噪比的衰减，从而在维持参数秩不变的同时，使有效查询维度与秩解耦。

Result: 理论上证明了原子极小性及方向性坍塌的修复机制；实验结果表明，在OPT和Qwen3模型上，AR1-ZO能够在标准查询预算下有效利用高秩LoRA，显著优于传统的ZO微调方法。

Conclusion: 本文提出了AR1-ZO算法，通过原子级查询和拓扑感知缩放，成功解决了零阶优化（ZO）在LoRA微调中遇到的秩悖论问题。该方法在不依赖外部子空间或额外查询的情况下，实现了高秩LoRA的高效训练，证明了测量拓扑而非子空间维度是限制性能的关键瓶颈。

Abstract: Zeroth-order (ZO) optimization enables large-language-model fine-tuning without storing backpropagation activations, while LoRA supplies compact trainable adapters. Combining them creates a rank paradox: increasing LoRA rank improves adapter capacity, but standard two-point ZO either perturbs a rank-dependent number of coordinates or, under atomwise updates, can make the finite-difference signal unobservable. This paper shows that the bottleneck is a measurement-topology problem rather than a need for an external subspace. LoRA already decomposes into matched rank-$1$ atoms, each a complete factor-coordinate block of dimension $d_\text{out}+d_\text{in}$. Querying one atom per step keeps the stored adapter rank $r$ while removing $r$ from the single-query perturbation dimension. The naive atomwise query is still miscalibrated: if it inherits canonical LoRA scaling $α/r$, the active finite-difference signal shrinks as $1/r$ and the active finite-difference signal-to-noise ratio (FD-SNR) as $1/r^2$, producing directional collapse under a fixed residual evaluation-noise floor. AR1-ZO pairs alternating rank-$1$ atom queries with topology-aware scaling $γ=αr$, restoring rank-invariant active signal without auxiliary bases, activation hooks, curvature estimates, or extra forward queries. Theory proves atom minimality, rank-independent active query dimension, directional collapse and restoration, and the remaining rank dependence as an amortized coverage cost. Experiments on OPT and Qwen3 models validate the signal mechanism and show that AR1-ZO makes high-rank LoRA effective among matched-budget ZO methods under the standard two-forward-pass query budget.

### [164] [Latent Laplace Diffusion for Irregular Multivariate Time Series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19805)
*Zinuo You,Jin Zheng,John Cartlidge*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 LLapDiff 的生成式模型，通过在拉普拉斯域内建模连续时间潜在轨迹，实现了不规则时间序列的高精度长周期预测，并解决了传统方法中的结构失真和误差漂移问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在处理不规则多变量时间序列的长周期预测时存在局限：离散化重采样方法会扭曲时间结构，而连续时间模型在序列求解器中易出现误差漂移。研究旨在消除这些弊端，实现高效且鲁棒的时间序列预测与建模。

Method: 提出了 Latent Laplace Diffusion (LLapDiff) 框架，核心方法包括：1. 将目标建模为低维潜在轨迹，实现跨时段的直接生成；2. 采用基于随机端口哈密顿动力学的模态参数化以确保反向过程的稳定性；3. 在拉普拉斯域中利用可学习的复共轭极点表示平均演化；4. 通过更新平均分析（renewal-averaging analysis）将采样间隔映射为事件域极点，并设计了间隔感知历史汇总器。

Result: 实验证明 LLapDiff 在长周期预测任务中优于现有基准模型，并且由于其连续时间生成特性，该模型能直接应用于历史时间戳的缺失值补全，表现出良好的灵活性。

Conclusion: LLapDiff 通过将连续时间动力学与拉普拉斯域的模态参数化相结合，成功解决了不规则多变量时间序列长周期预测中的结构失真和误差漂移问题，证明了在生成式框架下实现长程预测和缺失值补全的可行性。

Abstract: Irregular multivariate time series impose a trade-off for long-horizon forecasting: discrete methods can distort temporal structure via re-gridding, while continuous-time models often require sequential solvers prone to drift. To bridge this gap, we present Latent Laplace Diffusion (LLapDiff), a generative framework that models the target as a low-dimensional latent trajectory, enabling horizon-wide generation without step-by-step integration over physical time. We guide the reverse process utilizing a stable modal parameterization motivated by stochastic port-Hamiltonian dynamics, and parameterize its mean evolution in the Laplace domain via learnable complex-conjugate poles, enabling direct evaluation over irregular timestamps. We also link continuous dynamics to irregular observations through renewal-averaging analysis, which maps sampling gaps to effective event-domain poles and motivates a gap-aware history summarizer. Extensive experiments show that LLapDiff improves over baselines in long-horizon forecasting, and its continuous-time generative nature supports missing-value imputation by querying the same model at historical timestamps. Code is available at https://github.com/pixelhero98/LLapDiffusion.

### [165] [FLUXtrapolation: A benchmark on extrapolating ecosystem fluxes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19812)
*Anya Fries,Jacob A Nelson,Martin Jung,Markus Reichstein,Jonas Peters*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了名为 FLUXtrapolation 的基准测试，专门用于解决生态系统通量从局部观测塔向全球尺度的推算（upscaling）难题。该研究通过引入更具挑战性的时间、空间和温度分布偏移场景，不仅能更准确地评估模型在极端条件下的鲁棒性，也为提升全球碳、水、能量循环监测的科学准确性提供了标准化的评估工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生态系统通量（碳、水、能量循环的关键指标）通常只能在稀疏的地面观测塔点测量。为了获得全球通量估计，需要利用全球覆盖的协变量进行模型训练并推广至未观测区域（即“上推”/upscaling）。然而，由于气候、生态类型和观测条件的差异，以及存在全局尺度下无法观测到的重要驱动因子，导致模型面临严峻的分布偏移（域泛化）挑战。现有评估体系不足以反映这些复杂偏移带来的现实风险。

Method: 研究团队提出了 FLUXtrapolation 基准测试，该方法基于领域专家知识，定义了基于时间、空间和温度的推算场景。评估指标涵盖了分布偏移下的尾部误差（tail errors）、多时间尺度聚合表现以及对未见域（held-out domains）的预测能力，旨在深入剖析协变量分布偏移（$P_X$）和条件分布偏移（$P_{Y|X}$）的影响。

Result: 初步实验表明，虽然不同模型在常规的 hourly RMSE（中位数指标）下表现相近，但在该基准测试提出的“关注尾部误差”和“多尺度评估”框架下，模型性能出现了明显分化，证明了该基准测试在识别模型鲁棒性缺陷方面的有效性。

Conclusion: FLUXtrapolation 作为一个具有挑战性的基准测试，能够有效评估机器学习模型在生态系统通量推算任务中的分布偏移（distribution shift）表现。它不仅揭示了现有模型在面对极端条件和多尺度预测时的性能差异，还为改进全球通量估算提供了明确的评估框架和研究方向。

Abstract: We introduce FLUXtrapolation, a benchmark for extrapolating ecosystem fluxes under progressively harder distribution shifts. Ecosystem fluxes are central to understanding the carbon, water, and energy cycles, yet they can only be measured directly at sparsely located measurement towers. Producing global flux estimates therefore requires training models on observed sites using globally available covariates and predicting in unobserved regions, that is, upscaling. Flux upscaling is a challenging domain generalization problem that is affected by a shift in covariate distribution across climates, ecosystem types, and environmental conditions, as well as by conditional shift: important drivers remain unobserved at global scale. We provide a quantitative analysis of both these shifts in $P_X$ and $P_{Y\mid X}$. FLUXtrapolation is designed based on domain expertise on flux upscaling: it defines temporal, spatial, and temperature-based extrapolation scenarios and evaluates performance across held-out domains, temporal aggregations, and tail errors. In a pilot study, we find that baselines perform similarly under median hourly RMSE, but separate under the proposed tail-focused and multi-scale evaluation. FLUXtrapolation therefore poses a realistic and thus relevant challenge for machine learning methods under distribution shift; at the same time, progress on this benchmark would directly support the scientific goal of improving flux upscaling.

### [166] [General Lower Bounds for Differentially Private Federated Learning with Arbitrary Public-Transcript Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19813)
*Yicheng Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文推导了在通用差分隐私联邦学习场景下，参数估计精度的理论下界，解决了多轮交互和数据复用情况下的隐私-精度权衡问题。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We prove a general lower bound for differentially private federated learning protocols with arbitrary public-transcript interactions. The protocol may use any number of adaptive rounds, and each client's local samples may be reused across rounds. For parameter estimation under squared \(\ell_2\) loss, we establish a federated van Trees lower bound for every estimator satisfying a total clientwise sample-level zero-concentrated differential privacy (zCDP) constraint. The main technical ingredient is a privacy-information contraction inequality for complete public transcripts. We illustrate the bound through applications to mean estimation, linear regression, and nonparametric regression.

### [167] [Set-Valued Policy Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19830)
*Laura Fuentes-Vicente,Mathieu Even,Gaëlle Dormion,Antoine Chambaz,Uri Shalit,Julie Josse*

Main category: cs.LG

Method: 1. 提出集合值策略学习范式，将单一干预建议扩展为一组合理干预集合，以量化决策不确定性；2. 扩展了“学习推迟（Learning-to-defer）”框架至多处理设置，引入了“最大下界（Greatest Lower Bound）”方法；3. 引入“共形策略学习（Conformal Policy Learning）”，利用噪声标签文献中的随机注入方法，确保了在无需假设黑盒最优规则前提下的边际覆盖率。

Abstract: Conventional treatment policies map patient covariates to a single recommended intervention in order to maximize expected clinical outcomes. Although a rich body of causal inference methods has been developed to estimate such policies, point-valued recommendations can be highly sensitive to estimation uncertainty, model specification, and finite-sample variability, while typically providing little guidance about how confident one should be in the recommended action. In this work, we propose a set-valued policy learning paradigm for the multiple-treatment setting, in which policies output a set of plausible treatments rather than a single recommendation. This formulation enables intrinsic uncertainty quantification, with the size of the predicted set reflecting the degree of decision ambiguity. We extend the learning-to-defer framework to multiple treatments via a novel \textit{greatest Lower Bound} method, and introduce \textit{conformal policy learning}, which bridges the gap between unobserved ground-truth optimal treatments and estimated optimal treatment rules. Drawing on insights from the noisy-label literature, we develop a randomness-injection approach that guarantees marginal coverage without requiring assumptions on underlying black-box optimal treatment rules. ### [169] [Exploiting Non-Negativity in DAG Structure Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19947)
*Samuel Rey,Madeline navarro,Gonzalo Mateos*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对非负边权重DAG的学习算法，通过简化非循环性约束，将DAG学习转化为良性的凸优化问题，解决了传统连续化方法中常见的非凸与驻点陷阱问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的DAG学习方法通常面临复杂的离散组合优化难题。虽然现有的连续化约束方法（如NOTEARS）取得了一定进展，但仍存在非凸优化地形复杂、容易陷入退化的一阶最优性条件等问题。因此，研究旨在利用非负边权重这一特定结构，寻求更简单、更稳健的DAG学习特征表征。

Method: 本文利用非负边权重的结构特性，将有向无环图（DAG）的非循环性约束简化，构建了一个带正则化的非负DAG学习问题，并开发了一种基于乘子法（Method of Multipliers）的优化算法。此外，对该问题的优化地形进行了理论分析，证明了其在总体分布下具有良性的全局最优性。

Result: 理论分析表明，在总体分布下，真实的DAG是所提增强拉格朗日公式的唯一全局最小解，且优化地形中不存在虚假的内部驻点。数值实验证明，该方法在合成数据和真实数据集上的表现均优于现有的连续DAG学习算法。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于非负性约束的DAG学习方法，利用增强拉格朗日乘子法能够有效绕过传统方法中的非凸优化难题，并在理论上证明了在总体分布下真实DAG是唯一的全局最优解，显著提升了因果发现的准确性和稳定性。

Abstract: This work addresses the problem of learning directed acyclic graphs (DAGs) from nodal observations generated by a linear structural equation model. DAG learning is a central task in signal processing, machine learning, and causal inference, but it remains challenging because acyclicity is a global combinatorial property. Continuous acyclicity constraints have led to important algorithmic advances by replacing the discrete DAG constraint with smooth equality constraints. However, existing formulations still involve difficult non-convex optimization landscapes and may suffer from degenerate first-order optimality conditions. Here, we restrict attention to DAGs with non-negative edge weights and exploit this additional structure to obtain a simpler characterization of acyclicity. Building on this characterization, we formulate a regularized non-negative DAG learning problem and develop an algorithm based on the method of multipliers. We further analyze the benign optimization landscape induced by non-negativity. In the population regime, we show that the true DAG is the unique global minimizer of the proposed augmented-Lagrangian formulation; moreover, the landscape contains no spurious interior stationary points, and the true DAG is the only acyclic KKT point. Numerical experiments on synthetic and real-world data show that the proposed method improves over state-of-the-art continuous DAG-learning alternatives.

Using the LLM system prompt to estimate a robust baseline, we standardize user-token entropies and apply a one-sided CUSUM statistic. The resulting detector, CPD Online (CPD), is model-agnostic, training-free, runs online, and localizes the adversarial suffix onset. On a benchmark of 1,012 optimization-based suffix attacks (GCG, AutoDAN, AdvPrompter, BEAST, AutoDAN-HGA) and 1,012 perplexity-controlled benign prompts, CPD improves F1 over the strongest windowed-perplexity baseline on all six open-weight chat models (LLaMA-2-7B/13B, Vicuna-7B/13B, Qwen2.5-7B/14B). ### [171] [Your Neighbors Know: Leveraging Local Neighborhoods for Backdoor Detection in Decentralized Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19969)
*Sayan Biswas,Antoine Boutet,Davide Frey,Romaric Gaudel,Rachid Guerraoui,Maxime Jacovella,Anne-Marie Kermarrec,Dimitri Lerévérend,François Taïani,Martijn de Vos*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Argus 是一种新型的去中心化学习后门防御框架，通过节点间的协作检测与触发器一致性验证，在无中央服务器辅助的情况下，实现了对后门攻击的高效识别与过滤，并在保证模型收敛性的同时显著提升了系统在异构数据环境下的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 去中心化学习（DL）在缺乏中央服务器的情况下容易受到后门攻击，而现有的防御方案往往忽略了去中心化环境下的特殊约束（如缺乏全局信息和数据异构性）。因此，研究者旨在开发一种无需中央协调、无需预知触发器信息的原生去中心化后门检测机制。

Method: Argus 框架采用去中心化协作机制：1) 节点本地分析模型更新以识别潜在后门触发器；2) 节点与邻居共享触发器信息；3) 利用结构相似性度量对比触发器模式，区分真正的恶意攻击与数据异构性导致的“伪警报”（真实触发器具有一致性，伪警报则表现为不一致）；4) 过滤掉未通过测试的恶意模型更新，并逐步驱逐持续恶意行为的节点。

Result: 实验结果表明，Argus 在三个标准数据集上显著优于现有基线方法：攻击成功率最高降低了 90 个百分点，且模型精度（utility）仅比理想无攻击情况下降 5 个百分点以内。特别是在数据异构性较高的情况下，Argus 的防御优势更为明显。此外，文章还首次为去中心化后门检测机制提供了理论收敛性保证。

Conclusion: Argus 是首个专为去中心化学习设计的后门防御框架，通过节点间的协作验证机制，在不依赖中央服务器和先验知识的前提下，有效抵御后门攻击。理论分析证明了其在过滤攻击的同时仍能保持良好的收敛性能，且在大数据异构性场景下表现优异，具有很高的实用价值。

Abstract: Decentralized learning (DL) is an emerging machine learning paradigm where nodes collaboratively train models without a central server. However, the collaborative nature of DL makes it vulnerable to backdoor attacks, where a model is taught to behave normally on standard inputs while executing hidden, malicious actions when encountering data with specific triggers. Backdoor attacks in DL remain understudied and existing defenses often overlook DL constraints. We introduce Argus, a novel backdoor detection framework native to DL that requires neither a central coordinator nor prior knowledge of the trigger. In Argus, honest nodes locally analyze received model updates to identify potential backdoor triggers. Nodes then collectively share their triggers with their neighbors and use a structural similarity metric to separate true backdoors from false alarms induced by data heterogeneity. A key insight is that false positive triggers exhibit inconsistencies across participants while true positive ones show consistent patterns. Model updates that fail this collaborative test are rejected, and persistently malicious senders are eventually evicted. We provide the first theoretical convergence guarantees for a DL-specific backdoor detection mechanism, showing that filtering out suspicious model updates with high probability preserves a convergence rate comparable to standard DL. We implement and evaluate Argus on three standard datasets and against three state-of-the-art baselines. Across settings, Argus reduces attack success rates by up to 90 points compared to no defense, while preserving model utility within 5 percentage points of an omniscient oracle. Furthermore, the effectiveness of Argus compared to baselines improves as data heterogeneity increases.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 理论对比：在统一的框架下对比EDEN、RabitQ和TurboQuant，分析其在均方误差（MSE）和内积失真等不同准则下的表现。2. 算法设计：提出Block-Sphere Quantization（BlockQuant），该算法基于随机旋转向量的球形几何特性，采用分块球面量化而非传统的逐坐标量化。

Result: 理论分析证明BlockQuant在重构MSE和预期内积失真方面均优于现有基准；在真实嵌入数据集和长上下文大语言模型（LLM）推理任务的实验中，BlockQuant展现出了与理论预期一致的性能提升。

Abstract: Vector quantization is a fundamental primitive for scalable machine learning systems, enabling memory-efficient storage, fast retrieval, and compressed inference. Recent rotation-based quantizers such as EDEN, RabitQ, and TurboQuant have introduced strong guarantees and empirical performance, but the surrounding comparisons have been difficult to interpret because they rely on different distortion criteria, probability regimes, and implementation assumptions. As our first contribution, we provide a unified theoretical comparison of these methods and show that their relative advantages are criterion-dependent rather than absolute: EDEN and TurboQuant are favorable for MSE distortion, EDEN is also effective for expected inner-product distortion, and RabitQ provides strong high-probability control. This comparison further clarifies that EDEN provides particularly strong guarantees for expected distortion measures. As our second contribution, we introduce Block-Sphere Quantization (BlockQuant), a new rotation-based block quantization algorithm designed around the spherical geometry of randomly rotated vectors. Unlike coordinate-wise quantizers, BlockQuant quantizes blocks on the sphere, preserving the geometry of rotated embeddings more faithfully. We prove that this block-spherical design theoretically improves over the baselines considered in this paper for both reconstruction MSE and expected inner-product distortion. Our experiments on real embedding datasets and long-context LLM inference tasks show practical gains that are consistent with our theoretical improvements.

Abstract: Benchmark datasets are critical for reproducible, reliable, and discriminative evaluation of LLMs. However, recent studies reveal that many benchmark datasets are included in pretraining corpora, i.e., $\textit{contaminated}$, which diminishes their value as reliable measures of model generalization. In this paper, we argue that benchmark datasets should be $\textit{contamination-resistant}$, i.e., $\textit{unlearnable}$, but support $\textit{inference}$. To accomplish this, we first highlight the wide prevalence of benchmark dataset contamination and outline the properties of contamination-resistant datasets. Second, we highlight how the asymmetry between the inference and training pipelines in the Transformer architecture can be leveraged to support contamination-resistance. Third, we outline mathematical advancements to make these datasets interoperable across various LLM architectures. Based on the above, we call on the community to ensure the reliability of LLM benchmarking by: (i) advancing novel contamination-resistant methodologies, (ii) developing supporting methods and platforms, and (iii) adopting contamination-resistant benchmarks into existing evaluation pipelines.

### [174] [Fine-Tuning Without Forgetting via Loss-Adaptive Learning Rates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20005)
*Parjanya Prajakta Prashant,Jiongli Zhu,Aldan Creo,Babak Salimi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大模型微调中的灾难性遗忘问题，本文提出了 FINCH，这是一种通过动态调整学习率来抑制遗忘的方法，能够在不牺牲新任务学习效果的前提下，显著保持原模型的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在微调新数据时常出现灾难性遗忘。现有的抑制遗忘方法（如抑制高损失 token）往往会损害模型学习新知识的能力（特别是预训练覆盖不足的领域）。因此，作者旨在寻找一种既能控制遗忘，又不强行抑制高损失 token 的微调优化机制。

Method: 提出了一种名为FINCH的损失自适应学习率调度算法。该方法观察到单步遗忘量与学习率及当前损失的平方根乘积相关，因此根据训练损失动态调整学习率：在高损失批次上降低学习率以抑制遗忘，并在模型收敛时提高学习率以优化性能，全程保持微调目标函数不变。

Result: 在知识获取、科学任务及低资源语言适配等基准测试中，FINCH 平均减少了 93% 的遗忘，且任务性能与标准微调持平。在 Qwen3-4B 模型上的测试显示，FINCH 将 TruthfulQA 的性能下降减少了 5 倍，逆转了 HaluEval 的退化，并更好地保持了置信度校准。

Conclusion: 本文证明了学习率调度策略是微调过程中控制模型行为的有效工具，证明了通过调节学习率而非修改损失函数，可以在保持下游任务性能的同时显著抑制灾难性遗忘。

Abstract: Fine-tuning large language models on new data improves task performance but degrades capabilities learned during pretraining, a phenomenon known as catastrophic forgetting. Existing methods mitigate this by modifying the fine-tuning objective to suppress high-loss tokens or sequences, but these tokens are essential for learning new tasks, especially those with poor pretraining coverage. In such settings, hard tokens should still contribute to learning, so forgetting must be controlled without suppressing them. We identify a simple mechanism for doing so: per-step forgetting is bounded by the product of the learning rate and the square root of the current training loss. This suggests that high-loss batches are especially prone to inducing forgetting. Motivated by this observation, we introduce FINCH, a loss-adaptive learning-rate schedule that reduces the learning rate on high-loss batches and increases it as the model converges, while leaving the fine-tuning objective unchanged. Across knowledge acquisition, science, and low-resource language adaptation benchmarks, FINCH reduces forgetting by 93% on average while matching the task performance of standard fine-tuning. On Qwen3-4B knowledge acquisition, FINCH cuts TruthfulQA degradation by 5x and reverses HaluEval degradation, while better preserving confidence calibration. Overall, our results show that learning-rate schedules are an effective tool to shape model behavior during fine-tuning, beyond just target-task optimization.

</details>

Abstract: Bayesian filtering is a well-known problem that aims to estimate plausible states of a dynamical system from observations. Among existing approaches to solve this problem, particle filters are theoretically exact for non-linear dynamics and observations, but suffer from poor scalability in high dimensions. In this work, we show that diffusion-based emulators of dynamical systems can be used to implement, without additional training, an optimal variant of particle filters that has remained largely unexplored due to implementation challenges with classical numerical solvers. Experiments on nonlinear chaotic systems, including atmospheric dynamics, demonstrate that the proposed approach successfully scales particle filtering to high-dimensional settings.

### [176] [Take It or Leave It: Intent-Controlled Partial Optimal Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20030)
*Salil Parth Tripathi,Bertrand Chapron,Fabrice Collard,Nicolas Courty,Ronan Fablet*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出“意图控制部分最优传输”（IC-POT），通过引入逐点拒斥机制取代传统的全局拒斥，实现了对质量不匹配的精细化控制，并在多个跨领域应用中展现了优于传统最优传输方法的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的部分最优传输主要依赖全局拒斥规则，无法根据数据点的可靠性、几何结构或外部先验信息灵活地决定哪些质量可以不匹配，限制了其在复杂实际应用场景中的表现。

Method: 引入“意图控制部分最优传输”（IC-POT），通过在两个测度上引入逐点拒斥成本来替代全局拒斥规则；该方法被重构为增强支持集上的平衡 Kantorovich 最优传输问题，并可通过对偶形式转化为局部接受阈值问题进行求解。

Result: 在正样本-无标签学习（PU Learning）、开放集部分域适应（Open-partial Domain Adaptation）以及多模态卫星海洋测量中，IC-POT 通过整合逐点拒斥规则，显著提升了现有基准模型的性能和结果的物理可解释性。

Conclusion: IC-POT 提供了一种更具灵活性和可控性的部分最优传输框架，能够通过逐点拒斥机制有效地融合领域知识与先验信息，从而在存在噪声或不匹配数据的情况下实现更稳健的分布对比。

Abstract: While optimal transport (OT) enforces a rigid constraint by requiring two measures to be matched exactly, partial optimal transport relaxes this requirement by allowing mass to remain unmatched through a global budget, scalar rebate, or uniform rejection rule. However, many applications call for more structured, pointwise rejection mechanisms, where the decision to leave mass unmatched depends on side-specific reliability, support geometry, or external information about which components should participate in the comparison. We introduce \emph{intent-controlled partial optimal transport} (IC-POT), a targeted generalization of partial transport that replaces the global rejection paradigm with pointwise rejection costs over both measures. We show that the resulting optimization problem admits a dual interpretation in terms of local acceptance thresholds and can be solved by recasting it as a balanced Kantorovich OT problem on an augmented support. Beyond theoretical analysis, we demonstrate the practical relevance of IC-POT in settings where rejection is driven by side information. In positive-unlabeled learning and open-partial domain adaptation, incorporating pointwise rejection rules that encode statistical structure improves fixed baseline pipelines. Finally, we motivate the use of IC-POT with a geophysical practical case: multi-modal satellite ocean measurements, for which physical and sensors priors naturally inform the rejection mechanism and define the retrieved comparable signal information.

However, to evade detection, fraudsters continuously evolve their camouflaging strategies by deliberately mimicking textual responses of benign users, thereby concealing their malicious purposes. This phenomenon, referred to as semantic camouflage, fundamentally undermines commonly relied assumptions on how structural and attribute cues can be exploited to identify fraudsters, and makes it difficult to spot fraudsters with unsupervised TAGFD. To bridge the gaps, we propose a Case-Adaptive Multi-cue Expert fRAmework (CAMERA) for unsupervised TAGFD. CAMERA employs an ego-decoupled mixture-of-experts architecture, where each expert specializes in modeling a distinct type of fraud-indicative cue. A context-informed gating model is introduced to jointly consider the ego node representation and its local neighborhood context for adaptive integration of cues learned by different experts. Furthermore, CAMERA leverages the inherent rarity of fraudsters to support unsupervised one-class learning with expert-level objectives that encourage modeling dominant benign patterns, thereby enabling reliable unsupervised detection of camouflaged fraudsters. Experiments on 4 challenging datasets show that CAMERA consistently outperforms competitors, showing its effectiveness against semantically camouflaged fraudsters. Code available at https://github.com/CampanulaBells/CAMERA

Abstract: Ride-hailing platforms like DiDi Chuxing operate in highly dynamic environments where balancing driver supply and passenger demand is critical. Although driver-side subsidies serve as a primary lever to align these forces and improve key KPIs like completed rides (\texttt{Rides}) and gross merchandise value (\texttt{GMV}), optimizing them in production requires simultaneously meeting three constraints: (i) responsiveness to stochastic shocks, (ii) strict subsidy-rate caps, and (iii) low-latency execution at city scale. These requirements rule out expensive per-order optimization, calling for a forward-looking, constraint-aware city-level controller for online sequential decision making. To meet these requirements, we introduce D$^3$-Subsidy (Dynamic Driver-side Diffusion-based Subsidy), a hierarchical diffusion-based framework for deployable city-wide subsidy control. To bridge the train-inference gap, D$^3$-Subsidy employs a prefix-conditioned diffusion model that samples plausible future trajectories from immutable historical observations, ensuring the training protocol aligns with the fixed-history nature of online deployment. These generated plans are then decoded by a context-conditioned inverse module into low-dimensional city-level control signals. For scalable execution, we bridge the gap between city-level planning and fine-grained dispatch via a Lagrangian-dual-derived mapping, which embeds subsidy-rate caps directly into order-driver incentives without iterative optimization. Additionally, a multi-city pretraining strategy with parameter-efficient fine-tuning enables robust transfer across heterogeneous cities. Extensive offline evaluations demonstrate that D$^3$-Subsidy improves \texttt{Rides} and \texttt{GMV} while enhancing cap compliance, and a real-world A/B test confirms significant uplift while keeping budget-related violation metrics within operational thresholds.

### [179] [Active Context Selection Improves Simple Regret in Contextual Bandits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20040)
*Mohammad Shahverdikondori,Jalal Etesami,Negar Kiyavash*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了上下文空间有限的多臂老虎机问题，提出通过主动选择上下文进行采样，相比被动采样能显著降低后悔（Regret）。作者给出了最优采样策略，并设计了 EETC 算法以解决上下文分布未知的问题，在理论与实验上均证明了其优越性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 理论分析：对比了被动采样（Passive Sampling）与主动采样在上下文相关多臂老虎机问题中的 regret 上界。
2. 采样优化：通过优化分配策略 $q_j \propto p_j^{2/3}$ 来实现最优采样。
3. 算法设计：提出了“探索-探索-提交”（Explore-Explore-Then-Commit, EETC）算法，用于处理上下文分布 $p$ 未知的情况，平衡分布估计与主动分配的时间切换。

Result: 1. 理论上确定了被动采样与主动采样的精确后悔率。

3. 给出了预算受限下的主动采样最优解。
4. EETC 算法在长时程下能匹配已知分布时的最优主动采样性能。
5. 通过合成数据和真实数据实验验证了理论的正确性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过主动采样（Active Sampling）策略，学习者能够根据上下文分布的特性优化样本分配，从而在上下文相关的多臂老虎机问题中显著提升后悔（Regret）表现。对于未知上下文分布的情况，提出的EETC算法能有效平衡探索与利用，渐进地达到最优性能。

Abstract: We study the contextual multi-armed bandit problem with a finite context space (a.k.a. subpopulations), where the learner recommends a best action for each context and is evaluated by context-weighted simple regret. Our guarantees are worst-case over the reward distributions, while remaining instance-dependent with respect to the context distribution vector $p$. Akin to experimental design problems where the population of interest is fixed but the sampled subpopulation can be controlled, we allow the learner to actively choose which context to sample from. For a known $p$, we characterize tight regret rates: passive sampling where contexts are randomly revealed achieves regret of order $\sqrt{n/T \, \lVert p \rVert_{1/2}}$, whereas active sampling with allocation $q_j \propto p_j^{2/3}$ achieves the tight rate $\sqrt{n/T} \, \lVert p \rVert_{2/3}$. The resulting improvement can be as large as $Θ(k^{1/4})$, where $k$ is the number of contexts. We further extend the analysis to budgeted active sampling, characterize the corresponding tight rate, and identify when a limited active budget suffices to recover the fully active rate. When $p$ is unknown, we propose the Explore-Explore-Then-Commit (EETC) algorithm, which optimally balances estimating the context distribution and the time to switch to active allocation, such that for large horizons, it matches the known-$p$ active rate up to constants. Experiments on synthetic and real-world data support our theoretical findings.

### [180] [Smooth Partial Lotteries for Stable Randomized Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20069)
*Alexander Goldberg,Giulia Fanti,Nihar B. Shah*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对竞争选拔中评分微小波动导致录取结果剧烈变化的“不稳定性”问题，本文提出了以平滑性（Lipschitz条件）为核心的“截断线性彩票”机制，通过理论证明和实证数据表明，该机制在实现稳健性的同时，在选拔质量与平滑度之间达到了最佳权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的竞争性选拔（如科研基金评审、录取等）中采用的局部彩票机制存在严重的“不稳定性”问题，即候选人评分的微小变动会导致选拔概率发生巨大跳变，从而削弱了彩票机制旨在减弱决策边界处微小分差影响的初衷。因此，亟需一种设计原则来提升选拔过程的稳健性。

Method: 本文将平滑性形式化为一种Lipschitz条件（即映射评分到选择概率的函数需满足平滑约束），并据此设计了“截断线性彩票”（Clipped Linear Lottery）机制。该机制设定了上下阈值，在阈值范围内选择概率随评分线性增加，低于下限则拒绝，高于上限则接受。研究通过理论证明了该机制的遗憾度（regret）界限，并与个体公平性和差分隐私等稳定性概念进行了对比。

Result: 实验分析了ICLR 2025、NeurIPS 2024及瑞士国家科学基金会的真实评审数据，结果显示现有机制极其不稳定。理论分析与实验验证均表明，截断线性彩票机制不仅在数学上达到了最优平滑度，而且在实际应用中能在保证平滑度的前提下最大化选拔质量，显著优于其他现有的选择机制。

Conclusion: 本文提出的“截断线性彩票”机制通过引入平滑性设计原则，在保障选择过程稳定性的同时，实现了与现有机制相比更优的平滑度与选择质量（regret）之间的权衡。这一机制有效解决了传统彩票机制在决策边界处因评分细微变化而导致选择概率剧烈波动的缺陷。

Abstract: Competitive selection processes, from scientific funding to admissions and hiring, use evaluations to score candidates, and eventually choose a subset of them based on those scores. Recently, many organizations have adopted partial lotteries, which randomize selection based on evaluation scores. However, existing lottery designs are inherently unstable, as a small change to a single candidate's score can cause large shifts in their selection probabilities. This instability undermines a key goal of lotteries: reducing the influence of fine-grained score distinctions near the decision boundary. We propose smoothness as a design principle for partial lotteries, formalizing it as a Lipschitz condition on the mapping from review scores over candidates to selection probabilities. We introduce the Clipped Linear Lottery, a simple mechanism in which selection probabilities scale linearly with estimated quality between an upper threshold, above which we always accept, and a lower threshold, below which we always reject. We prove that the Clipped Linear Lottery's worst-case regret matches a lower bound for any smooth selection rule up to a factor of $(1 - k/n)$, where $k/n$ is the acceptance rate. We compare smooth selection to other stability notions like Individual Fairness and Differential Privacy, showing that the Clipped Linear Lottery achieves a better smoothness-regret tradeoff than alternatives. Experiments on real peer review data from ICLR 2025, NeurIPS 2024, and the Swiss National Science Foundation demonstrate that existing lottery designs are highly unstable in practice even under perturbations to a single score. Our experiments also confirm the tightness of our theoretical analysis and show that our proposed Clipped Linear Lottery achieves a better smoothness-utility tradeoff than alternatives in practice.

### [181] [INSHAPE: Instance-Level Shapelets for Interpretable Time-Series Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20088)
*Seongjun Lee,Seokhyun Lee,Changhee Lee*

Method: 提出了名为INSHAPE的框架，用于发现针对每个时间序列的变长、具有判别力的时间模式。该方法通过将模式识别为非重叠段并建模其时间依赖性，同时采用自底向上策略将实例级形状集聚合成原型（全局级）形状集，从而实现从局部到全局的解释。

Result: 在128个UCR和30个UEA基准数据集上的实验结果表明，INSHAPE在性能上一致优于现有的尖端形状集分类方法，并能提供更直观、深入的可解释性分析。

Conclusion: INSHAPE框架成功解决了传统形状集（Shapelet）方法在个体特征捕捉和模式交互建模上的不足，通过自底向上的设计实现了高精度的分类预测与直观的实例级及全局级可解释性。

Abstract: Discovering shapelets -- i.e., discriminative temporal patterns within time series -- has been widely studied to address the inherent complexity of time-series classification (TSC) and to make model decision-making processes more transparent. However, existing methods primarily focus on population-level shapelets optimized across the entire dataset, which leads to two fundamental limitations: (i) population-level patterns often misalign with instance-specific features, resulting in suboptimal performance and potentially misleading interpretations, and (ii) most methods treat shapelets as independent entities, overlooking important temporal dependencies and interactions among multiple patterns. To address these limitations, we propose INSHAPE, an interpretable TSC framework that discovers variable-length, discriminative temporal patterns specific to each time series. INSHAPE identifies these patterns as non-overlapping segments and models their temporal dependencies, thereby providing clear instance-level interpretations while achieving strong predictive performance. Furthermore, INSHAPE bridges local and global interpretability through a bottom-up approach, aggregating instance-level shapelets into prototypical (population-level) shapelets. Extensive experiments on 128 UCR and 30 UEA benchmark datasets show that INSHAPE consistently outperforms state-of-the-art shapelet-based methods while providing more intuitive and interpretable insights.

</details>


### [182] [Draft Less, Retrieve More: Hybrid Tree Construction for Speculative Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20104)
*Yuhao Shen,Tianyu Liu,Xinyi Hu,Quan Kong,Baolin Zhang,Jun Dai,Jun Zhang,Shuang Ge,Lei Chen,Yue Li,Mingcheng Wan,Cong Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Graft 是一种针对推测解码的无训练补偿框架，它通过在动态剪枝释放的计算预算内进行高预测性 token 检索与嫁接，在降低计算开销的同时有效补偿了接受率，显著提升了大模型的推理速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的推测解码方法为了提高接受率构建庞大的草稿树，导致计算和显存带宽压力巨大。现有的动态剪枝虽然能降低延迟，但会丢弃有效候选者从而降低接受率。研究旨在解决这种性能与效率之间的矛盾，通过更优的资源分配实现更快的端到端推理。

Method: 提出了一种名为 Graft 的补偿框架，核心机制是“先剪枝后嫁接”。该方法在通过动态剪枝减少计算开销的同时，利用释放的算力资源进行候选 token 检索，将高预测性的检索 token 填补到被剪枝留下的拓扑空缺中，从而在保持低开销的前提下补偿了被剪枝导致的接受率损失。

Result: Graft 在无需额外训练的情况下实现了零损失的性能提升。在短文本生成任务中实现了高达 5.41 倍的加速，在 Qwen3-235B 等大模型上相较于 EAGLE-3 平均加速提升高达 21.8%。同时，该方法在长文本生成以及 DFlash 等不同草稿范式中也表现出极佳的通用性和显著的加速效果。

Conclusion: Graft 通过“剪枝-再嫁接”的协同机制，成功打破了推测解码中模型推理速度与接受率之间的帕累托权衡，为各种规模的模型提供了更高效、无需训练的推理加速方案，并展示了其在不同架构下的扩展潜力。

Abstract: Speculative decoding (SD) accelerates large language model inference by leveraging a draft-then-verify paradigm. To maximize the acceptance rate, recent methods construct expansive draft trees, which unfortunately incur severe VRAM bandwidth and computational overheads that bottleneck end-to-end speedups. While dynamic-depth pruning can reduce this latency by removing marginal branches, it also discards potentially valid candidates, preventing the acceptance rate from reaching the upper bound of dense trees. In this paper, we identify a critical opportunity in resource allocation: the transition from dense to pruned drafting frees up significant computational budget. To break this Pareto tradeoff, we introduce Graft, a compensation framework that couples pruning and retrieval as mutually reinforcing operations. Pruning supplies sufficient budget for retrieval, while retrieval compensates for pruning-induced coverage loss and recovers accepted length. By employing a sequential `prune-then-graft' mechanism, Graft attaches highly predictive retrieved tokens into positions opened by pruning, filling the topological gaps with near-zero overhead. Graft is entirely training-free and lossless. Comprehensive evaluations show that Graft establishes a new Pareto frontier across practical deployment settings, including short-context generation, long-context generation, and large-scale models. On short-context benchmarks, it achieves up to 5.41$\times$ speedup and improves average speedup over EAGLE-3 by up to 21.8% on the large-scale Qwen3-235B. We also provide a preliminary exploration of applying Graft to the DFlash-style block drafting paradigm, offering initial evidence and insights for extending grafting beyond autoregressive draft trees.

</details>


### [183] [Optimal Representation Size: High-Dimensional Analysis of Pretraining and Linear Probing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20105)
*Valentina Njaradi,Clémentine Dominé,Rachel Swanson,Marco Mondelli,Andrew Saxe*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过建立解析模型，量化了“预训练+微调”范式中表征维度、数据量与泛化误差之间的关系，指出在数据受限的情况下，优化表征的压缩程度对于提升模型性能至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决人工智能在有限标注数据下实现高效泛化这一核心挑战。针对当前主流的“预训练+微调”两阶段学习范式，探究如何从无标注数据中有效提取结构，并量化表征学习与下游任务性能之间的数学关系。

Method: 作者构建了一个解析模型，将结构提取过程形式化为对无标注数据进行主成分分析（PCA），并将下游任务处理为基于线性回归的学习过程。通过在高维机制下推导训练误差与泛化误差的精确表达式，分析了表征维度、样本量及任务对齐度对模型性能的影响。

Result: 推导出了泛化误差的精确表达式，发现预训练表示对下游任务有决定性影响。研究量化了预训练数据量与监督数据量的等价关系（即多少无标注数据可替代一个标注样本），并指出最优表征维度取决于预训练与下游数据的可用性。相关结论在自编码器及大语言模型中得到了实证支持。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了表征维度优化在预训练-微调范式中的关键作用。研究表明，压缩表征在下游数据稀缺时具有优势，而预训练数据稀缺时则需要更高维的表征。该模型量化了无标注数据与有标注数据之间的权衡关系，为理解现代预训练模型提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: Learning to generalise from limited data is a fundamental challenge for both artificial and biological systems. A common strategy is to extract reusable structure from abundant unlabelled data, enabling efficient adaptation to new tasks from limited labelled data. This two-stage paradigm is now standard in modern training pipelines, where pretraining is followed by fine-tuning or linear probing. We provide an analytical model of this process: structure extraction is formalized as principal component analysis on unlabelled data, and downstream learning as linear regression on a separate labelled dataset. In the high-dimensional regime, we derive exact expressions for training and generalisation error showcasing their dependence on representation dimensionality, unlabelled and labelled sample sizes, and task alignment. Our results show that pretrained representations strongly influence downstream generalisation, and we characterize the optimal representation size as a function of task parameters: with abundant pretraining data but scarce downstream data, maximally compressed representations are optimal, whereas with limited pretraining data, higher-dimensional representations generalise better. Furthermore, we establish an exact trade-off between pretraining and supervision, quantifying how much unlabelled data is required to replace a single labelled sample. Beyond our idealised model, we observe similar phenomenology in autoencoders and pretrained LLMs. Altogether, we highlight that optimising representation size is critical, giving conditions for when compression during pretraining improves generalisation.

</details>


### [184] [Beyond Isotropy in JEPAs: Hamiltonian Geometry and Symplectic Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20107)
*Robert Jenkinson Alvarez*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 传统的 JEPA 模型强制要求特征呈各向同性分布，这限制了模型对复杂几何结构的表达能力。本文提出了 HamJEPA，通过引入哈密顿动力学进行跨视图预测，将结构化偏差转移至视图耦合，有效提升了特征表示的质量和性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的联合嵌入预测架构（JEPAs）通常将单视图嵌入正则化为各向同性高斯分布，这隐含了对欧几里得对称性的假设。作者指出这种做法存在缺陷：在下游几何结构未知时，固定的各向同性目标往往是次优的，甚至可能导致表示与下游任务的几何结构严重失配。此外，作者证明了仅通过单视图边际分布无法唯一确定视图间的预测耦合。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为 HamJEPA 的模型。该模型将每个视图编码为相空间状态 (q, p)，并利用学习到的哈密顿蛙跳积分映射（Hamiltonian leapfrog map）来执行视图间的预测。为了防止坍缩（collapse），引入了非各向同性尺度和谱基底（spectral floors）作为正则化手段，而非强制要求编码器输出各向同性高斯分布。

Result: 在无头（headless）Token 协议测试中，HamJEPA 在 CIFAR-100 上表现优异，30 轮次训练下 kNN@20 提升了 4.89，线性探针提升了 3.52；80 轮次下分别提升了 6.45 和 10.64。在 ImageNet-100 上也取得了显著的性能增益。消融实验确认了辛（symplectic）耦合是提升模型性能的核心因素。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种将结构化偏差从编码器边际分布转移到跨视图耦合的新范式。实验证明，基于哈密顿动力学的 HamJEPA 能够通过模拟物理系统的演化过程，更有效地捕捉特征空间的几何结构，从而在多种基准测试中显著超越了传统的各向同性正则化方法。

Abstract: JEPAs often regularize one-view embeddings toward an isotropic Gaussian, implicitly baking Euclidean symmetry into the representation. We show that this is not merely a benign default. For a known structured downstream geometry $H\succ0$, the minimax and maximum-entropy covariance under a Hamiltonian energy budget is $(c/d)H^{-1}$, and Euclidean isotropy incurs a closed-form price of isotropy. More importantly, when the downstream geometry is unknown, no geometry-independent fixed marginal target is canonical: every fixed covariance shape can be maximally misaligned for some structured geometry. We further show that even oracle one-view marginals do not identify the JEPA view-to-view predictive coupling. These results suggest that the structural bias in JEPAs should enter the cross-view coupling rather than a fixed encoder marginal. We instantiate this principle with \textbf{HamJEPA}, which encodes each view as a phase-space state $(q,p)$ and predicts view-to-view transitions with a learned Hamiltonian leapfrog map, while non-isotropic scale and spectral floors prevent collapse. In a deliberately headless token protocol, HamJEPA improves over SIGReg on CIFAR-100 by $+4.89$ kNN@20 and $+3.52$ linear-probe points at 30 epochs, and by $+6.45$ kNN@20 and $+10.64$ linear-probe points at 80 epochs, while a matched MLP predictor ablation shows that the symplectic coupling is the ingredient driving the neighborhood-geometry gain. On ImageNet-100, HamJEPA-$q$ improves by $+4.82$ kNN@20 and $+7.52$ linear-probe points at 45 epochs.

</details>

*Emaad Khwaja,Chris Lettieri,Gerald Woo,Eden Belouadah,Marc Cenac,Guillaume Jarry,Enguerrand Paquin,Xunyi Zhao,Viktoriya Zhukov,Othmane Abou-Amal,Chenghao Liu,Ameet Talwalkar,David Asker*

TL;DR: 研究表明时间序列基础模型具备良好的规模扩展性。研究团队发布了 Toto 2.0 系列开源预测模型，其在多个权威基准测试中表现卓越，达到了行业领先水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探索时间序列基础模型在大规模参数下的扩展规律，通过统一的训练配方验证模型性能是否会随参数量增加而提升，并解决当前预测模型缺乏高质量、大规模、开源基准模型的现状。

Method: 1. 提出了统一的训练方案，支持模型参数从4M扩展至2.5B。
2. 采用了u-muP（universal maximal update Parameterization）超参数迁移管线，以优化大规模模型的训练稳定性和超参数选择。
3. 构建并发布了五个不同规模的开源预测模型（Toto 2.0 系列）。

Result: Toto 2.0 系列模型在三大主流时间序列预测基准测试（BOOM、GIFT-Eval、TIME）中均达到了行业领先水平（SOTA），证明了其卓越的预测性能及泛化能力。所有五个检查点均已开源（Apache 2.0 协议）。

Conclusion: 时间序列基础模型具有显著的规模扩展性，通过统一的训练方案，模型性能随参数量增加而持续提升。Toto 2.0 系列模型的发布为时间序列预测领域树立了新的技术标杆，并推动了开源社区在基础模型方向的发展。

Abstract: We show that time series foundation models scale: a single training recipe produces reliable forecast-quality improvements from 4M to 2.5B parameters. We release Toto 2.0, a family of five open-weights forecasting models trained under this recipe. The Toto 2.0 family sets a new state of the art on three forecasting benchmarks: BOOM, our observability benchmark; GIFT-Eval, the standard general-purpose benchmark; and the recent contamination-resistant TIME benchmark. This report describes our experimental results and details the design decisions behind Toto 2.0: its architecture and training recipe, training data, and the u-muP hyperparameter transfer pipeline. All five base checkpoints are released under Apache 2.0.

### [186] [TrajTok: Adaptive Spatial Tokenization for Trajectory Representation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20134)
*Zhen Xiong,Shang-Ling Hsu,Cyrus Shahabi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TrajTok是一种通用的轨迹预训练模型，通过多分辨率六边形分块和时空感知Transformer，将原始轨迹转化为高质量的通用表征，并在多种轨迹预测与分类任务中实现了SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的轨迹表征学习难以处理原始GPS数据中的连续性、噪声和不规则采样问题，且传统空间网格化方法存在稀疏性或信息混淆的局限，缺乏一种能够同时捕捉几何与运动学特征的通用轨迹表征方法。

Method: 1. 提出多分辨率六边形单元划分方案，将原始GPS数据离散化为空间Token；2. 设计了因子分解的Transformer编码器，包含跨模态注意力融合和时空旋转位置编码（ST-RoPE）；3. 采用掩码Token建模（Masked-token modeling）进行预训练，同时学习几何结构与运动学模式。

Result: 在Porto数据集上，TrajTok在轨迹相似性搜索、分类、到达时间估计（ETA）和总行程时间回归等任务中表现优异，优于多种专门针对单一任务设计的模型，且验证了其表征的强迁移性。

Conclusion: TrajTok 通过多分辨率空间分块和掩码建模预训练，成功构建了一种通用的轨迹表征基础模型。其实验结果证明了该方法在多种轨迹任务中具有极强的迁移性和表现力，为未来轨迹数据挖掘提供了新的通用范式。

Abstract: Learning generalizable trajectory representations from raw GPS traces remains difficult because the data is continuous, noisy, and irregularly sampled. Spatial tokenization is also challenging: fine grids yield sparse cells with weak embeddings, while coarse grids merge heterogeneous movement patterns into the same token. We present TrajTok, a trajectory encoder with a simple pretraining recipe for transferable trajectory embeddings. TrajTok first learns a multi-resolution hexagonal cell partition from the spatial distribution of GPS points, converting noisy GPS sequences into discrete cell tokens. To capture both geometry and kinematics, it uses a factorized transformer encoder with early per-modality self-attention blocks, cross-attention fusion layers, and spatiotemporal rotary position embeddings, ST-RoPE, to encode where and when each token occurs. TrajTok is pretrained with masked-token modeling that recovers both geometric structure and kinematic patterns from partial trajectory observations. On the Porto dataset, a frozen TrajTok encoder with lightweight task adapters achieves strong performance across trajectory similarity search, classification, estimated time of arrival, and full travel-time regression, outperforming multiple task-specific methods. The same frozen encoder supports both geometry-dominated and kinematics-dominated tasks, suggesting that TrajTok learns transferable trajectory structure rather than task-specific shortcuts. These results indicate that learned multi-resolution spatial tokenization combined with masked-token pretraining is a promising direction for general-purpose trajectory foundation models.

### [187] [Atoms of Thought: Universal EEG Representation Learning with Microstates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20182)
*Xinyang Tian,Ruitao Liu,Ziyi Ye,Siyang Xue,Xin Wang,Xuesong Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于“微状态”的通用脑电信号分词方法，通过将脑电信号离散化为微状态序列，在多个下游任务中实现了比传统时频域特征更好的识别性能，且具备更高的可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的脑电信号分析多依赖于时域或频域特征提取，难以捕捉大脑活动的复杂动态模式。本文旨在探索微状态作为一种“大脑活动构建块”，是否能作为一种更简洁、通用且具备高解释性的表示方法，以提升脑电信号在不同下游任务中的识别性能。

Method: 本文提出了一种基于微状态的通用表征学习方法。首先，利用大规模医疗脑电数据集，通过聚类算法将连续的脑电信号离散化为一系列微状态标记（Microstate Tokenizer）；随后，将该分词器应用于睡眠分期、情绪识别及运动想象等多个下游任务，并与传统的时域和频域特征提取方法进行了对比评估。

Result: 实验结果表明，基于微状态的表征学习在多种模型架构和不同任务场景下，均优于传统的时域和频域特征方法。此外，该方法不仅提升了模型性能，还显著增强了脑电信号分析的可解释性和可扩展性。

Conclusion: 微状态（Microstates）是一种高效且具有高度可解释性的脑电信号通用表征方式。本文提出的通用微状态分词器打破了传统单一任务特征提取的限制，证明了离散化脑电活动序列在跨任务学习中的卓越性能，为脑机接口和神经科学研究提供了一种更具通用性和扩展性的新范式。

Abstract: Learning universal representations from electroencephalogram (EEG) signals is a cutting-edge approach in the field of neuroinformatics and brain-computer interfaces (BCIs). Conventionally, EEG is treated as a multivariate temporal signal, where time- or frequency-domain features are extracted for representation learning. This paper investigates a simple yet effective EEG representation, i.e., microstates. Microstates represent the building blocks of brain activity patterns at a microscopic time scale. We build a universal microstate tokenizer from a large medical EEG dataset by clustering continuous EEG signals into sequences of discrete microstates. The microstate tokenizer is then adopted universally across a series of downstream tasks, including sleep staging, emotion recognition, and motor imagery classification. Experimental results show that EEG representation learning with microstates outperforms traditional time-domain and frequency-domain features under different models and across different tasks. Further analysis shows that microstates offer greater interpretability and scalability, thereby opening up applications in both cognitive neuroscience and clinical research.

### [188] [Position: Let's Develop Data Probes to Fundamentally Understand How Data Affects LLM Performance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18801)
*Shiqiang Wang,Herbert Woisetschläger,Hans Arno Jacobsen,Mingyue Ji*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对目前大模型研究过度依赖昂贵的经验性数据实验，本文提出了一种“数据探针”方法，利用可控的合成序列系统地揭示数据特征如何影响模型行为，旨在为理解数据与大模型之间的关系建立理论基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前大语言模型领域过度依赖大规模实验和经验启发式规则来进行数据筛选和构建，这不仅计算成本高昂，且缺乏对“数据特性如何驱动模型行为”这一本质问题的理论理解。因此，迫切需要一种更系统、科学的机制来揭示数据在模型生命周期各个阶段的作用。

Method: 提出了一种基于“数据探针”（Data Probes）的方法。该方法通过预定义的随机过程生成合成序列，这些序列具备受控的统计特性。研究者通过观察大语言模型在这些探针序列上的行为，利用统计学中的“典型集”（typical sets）等理论概念，系统性地评估数据特征如何影响模型的性能、泛化能力及鲁棒性。

Result: 本文是一篇观点论文（Position Paper），旨在为大模型数据研究提供一个全新的框架。它论证了通过合成数据探针研究模型行为的可行性与必要性，并指出该方法能够将以往分散的经验发现转化为更具普遍意义的理论洞见。

Conclusion: 本文主张将“数据探针”作为一种系统性研究方法，从单纯依赖大规模实验转向基于理论原则的探索。通过分析模型在可控合成序列上的表现，可以为大模型的训练、微调和对齐提供深层的理论支撑，有助于揭示数据特征与模型行为之间的本质联系。

Abstract: Data is fundamental to large language models (LLMs). However, understanding of what makes certain data useful for different stages of an LLM workflow, including training, tuning, alignment, in-context learning, etc., and why, remains an open question. Current approaches rely heavily on extensive experimentation with large public datasets to obtain empirical heuristics for data filtering and dataset construction. These approaches are compute intensive and lack a principled way of understanding the essence of how specific data characteristics drive LLM behavior. In this position paper, we advocate for the need of developing systematic methodologies for generating synthetic sequences from appropriately defined random processes, with the goal that these sequences can reveal useful characteristics when they are used in one or multiple stages of the LLM workflow. We refer to such sequences as data probes. By observing LLM behavior on data probes, researchers can systematically conduct studies on how data characteristics influence model performance, generalization, and robustness. The probing sequences exhibit statistical properties that can be viewed using theoretical concepts, such as typical sets, which are generalized to describe the behaviors of LLMs. This data-probe approach provides a pathway for uncovering foundational insights into the role of data in LLM training and inference, beyond empirical heuristics.

</details>


### [189] [Operationalizing Document AI: A Microservice Architecture for OCR and LLM Pipelines in Production](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18818)
*Yao Fehlis,Benjamin Bengfort,Zhangzhang Si,Vahid Eyorokon,Prema Roman,Patrick Deziel,Devon Slonaker,Steve Veldman,Ben Johnson,Joyce Rigelo,Michael Wharton,Steve Kramer*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种文档理解系统的微服务架构，解决了从学术模型到大规模生产部署的工程挑战，揭示了OCR是影响生产延迟的核心瓶颈，并给出了针对GPU资源优化及水平扩展的实践经验。

Method: 提出了一种微服务架构，包括：1. 混合分类策略；2. 将GPU密集型推理与CPU密集型编排解耦；3. 利用异步处理应对IO密集型操作；4. 采用独立、水平扩展的策略。并结合批处理分析方法对系统性能进行了定量评估。

Abstract: Academic research tends to focus on new models for document understanding creating a wide gap in the literature between model definition and running models at production scale. To close that gap, we present a microservice architecture that encapsulates pipelines of multiple models for classification, optical character recognition (OCR), and large language model structured field extraction as well as our experience running this pipeline on thousands of multi-page documents per hour. We describe our primary design decisions, including a hybrid classification, separation of GPU-bound inference from CPU-bound orchestration, use of asynchronous processing for the many IO-bound operations in the pipeline, and an independent, horizontal scaling strategy. Using batch profiling, we identified two surprising qualitative findings that shape production deployments: OCR, not language-model parsing, dominates end-to-end latency, and the system saturates at a concurrency determined by shared GPU-inference capacity rather than worker count. Our goal is to provide practitioners with concrete architectural patterns for building document understanding systems that work beyond the benchmark; effectively operationalizing models in production.

### [190] [Evaluating the Utility of Personal Health Records in Personalized Health AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18937)
*Rory Sayres,Kejia Chen,Ayush Jain,Matthew Thompson,Jonathan Richina,Xiang Yin,Jimmy Hu,Fan Zhang,Bob Lou,Mike Sanchez,Ines Mezerreg,Meredith Schreier,Hamsa Subramaniam,I-Ching Lee,Yugang Jia,Daniel Mcduff,Yossi Matias,Avinatan Hassidim,Dale Webster,Yun Liu,Jackie Barr,Quang Duong*

TL;DR: 本研究评估了利用大语言模型解读复杂个人健康记录（PHR）的潜力。结果证明，向模型提供临床上下文可显著提升其回答患者健康查询的帮助程度，并为监控模型在医疗应用中的准确性与安全性提供了新的评估框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 患者管理的个人健康记录（PHR）虽然旨在赋能患者，但其中的信息过于复杂，导致患者难以从中获得有价值的洞察。研究旨在评估大语言模型在结合临床数据的情况下，能否为患者提供准确、有帮助且个性化的健康信息解读。

Method: 研究人员利用 Gemini 3.0 Flash 模型，针对 2,257 个不同类型（搜索查询、聊天模板、临床咨询）的患者健康问题进行了测试。实验对比了三种上下文环境：无 PHR 上下文、基础摘要、以及完整临床记录。评估采用了现有的 SHARP 框架，并针对 PHR 解读中的特定错误模式开发了新的评估框架，通过自动评分器和临床医生评分相结合的方式进行验证。

Result: 实验结果显示，引入 PHR 数据后，大模型在回答所有类型问题时的帮助程度均显著提升（p < 0.001），并在安全性、准确性、相关性和个性化方面表现出潜在提升。新的评估框架成功识别了模型在处理复杂 PHR 时存在的弱点，如时间顺序理解偏差及特定情境下的幻觉。

Conclusion: 研究表明，将临床数据集成到大语言模型中能显著提高其回答患者健康问题的质量和个性化程度。虽然大模型在处理复杂个人健康记录方面展现出巨大潜力，但仍存在时间感知混乱和罕见幻觉等问题，因此建立严格的评估框架对于确保医疗应用的安全性至关重要。

Abstract: Patient-managed Personal Health Records (PHRs) promises to empower patients to better understand their health; but information in the record is complex, potentially hindering insights. In this study, we assess the potential of large language models (LLMs, Gemini 3.0 Flash) to provide helpful answers to user health queries, when provided clinical data from PHRs as context. A total of 2,257 user queries were drawn from 3 different distributions to represent patient questions: shorter web search queries, longer questions derived from templates of chatbot conversations, and questions patients asked to their healthcare team (patient calls). Queries were matched with de-identified PHRs (from a pool of 1,945). Gemini responses were generated (1) without PHR context; (2) with a basic summary of demographics, conditions, and medications; (3) with full, extensive clinical notes. For evaluation, we leveraged an existing rating framework (SHARP), and developed a new framework for specific error modes when interpreting PHRs. Evaluation was performed using autoraters for the full set, and with clinician ratings for a subset (n=95), with both sets of raters knowing the full PHR context. We see significant improvements in the helpfulness of answers to all question types with PHR data (p < 0.001, paired t-test). We also observe potential gains in safety, accuracy, relevance and personalization of answers. Our PHR evaluation framework further identifies gaps in LLM understanding of particular aspects of complex PHRs, such as temporal disorientation, and rare but meaningful confabulations. These results suggest potential for PHR data to help people with a wide range of user needs; and provide a framework for monitoring for gaps in LLM answers based on PHR context. This study motivates further work to assess and realize potential benefits to users from understanding their health records.

### [191] [Learn-by-Wire Training Control Governance: Bounded Autonomous Training Under Stress for Stability and Efficiency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19008)
*Anis Radianis*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了 LBW-Guard，这是一个位于优化器之上的治理层，通过实时监控和有界运行时控制，解决了大语言模型训练中的不稳定性问题，在显著提升模型性能的同时缩短了训练时间，并展现出极强的抗高学习率压力能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代大语言模型训练在激进的学习率、大规模参数及运行时压力下，频繁出现不稳定性、性能退化以及计算资源浪费等问题。现有的方法（如简单的梯度裁剪）在极端压力下的保障能力有限，因此需要一种更智能的治理机制来平衡训练效率与稳定性。

Method: 提出了一种名为“Learn-by-Wire Guard (LBW-Guard)”的治理层，它独立于优化器（如 AdamW），通过实时监控训练遥测数据（Telemetry），智能识别不稳定的训练阶段，并对优化器的更新过程施加有界控制，而非直接修改优化器的更新规则或采用传统的局部梯度抑制。

Result: 在 Qwen2.5-7B 的压力测试中，LBW-Guard 将最终困惑度从 13.21 降至 10.74（提升 18.7%），训练速度提升 1.10 倍。在高学习率压力测试（LR=3e-3 和 1e-3）下，基础 AdamW 几乎失效，而使用 LBW-Guard 后模型依然保持良好的训练效果（困惑度分别为 11.57 和 10.33）。该方法表现出明显优于梯度裁剪的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 针对大型语言模型（LLM）训练中对稳定性敏感的场景，引入一个位于优化器之上的治理层（Governance Plane）是非常有效的。LBW-Guard 证明了通过有界运行时控制，可以在保持训练目标不变的前提下，显著提升训练的鲁棒性并减少计算资源浪费，其效果优于传统的梯度裁剪等方法。

Abstract: Modern language-model training is increasingly exposed to instability, degraded runs, and wasted compute, especially under aggressive learning-rate, scale, and runtime-stress conditions. This paper introduces Learn-by-Wire Guard (LBW-Guard), a bounded autonomous training-control governance layer that operates above AdamW. Rather than replacing the optimizer update rule, LBW-Guard observes training telemetry, interprets instability-sensitive regimes, and applies bounded control to optimizer execution while preserving fixed training objectives.
  We evaluate LBW-Guard in a Qwen2.5-centered stress-and-robustness suite using WikiText-103, with Qwen2.5-7B as the empirical anchor, model-size comparisons against Qwen2.5-3B and Qwen2.5-14B, learning-rate stress tests, gradient-clipping baselines, and a no-LoRA TinyLlama-1B full-parameter sanity check. In the 7B reference setting, LBW-Guard reduces final perplexity from 13.21 to 10.74, an 18.7% improvement, while reducing end-to-end time from 392.54s to 357.02s, a 1.10x speedup. Under stronger learning-rate stress, AdamW degrades to 1885.24 final perplexity at LR=3e-3 and 659.76 at LR=1e-3, whereas LBW-Guard remains trainable at 11.57 and 10.33, respectively. Gradient-clipping baselines do not reproduce this effect.
  These results support a scoped systems conclusion that stability-sensitive LLM training can benefit from a governance plane above the optimizer. LBW-Guard provides evidence that bounded runtime control can preserve productive compute under stress while remaining distinct from optimizer replacement and local gradient suppression.

### [193] [How Far Are We From True Auto-Research?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19156)
*Zhengxin Zhang,Ning Wang,Sainyam Galhotra,Claire Cardie*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ResearchArena框架评估了自动生成论文的质量，发现当前AI智能体生成的论文虽在文稿层面具有欺骗性，但在实验严谨性和真实性上存在重大缺陷，尚未达到真正的自动化科研水准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动研究系统虽能生成完整论文，但缺乏系统性评估以衡量其生成质量。研究者旨在探究当前智能体在“无需复杂引导”的情况下，其学术产出的真实质量及面临的瓶颈。

Method: 开发了名为ResearchArena的框架，支持Claude Code、Codex和Kimi Code三个智能体进行完整的科研闭环（构思、实验、写作、自我优化）。通过13个CS研究课题进行117次实验，并采用三种评估方式：纯文稿评审（SAR）、考虑实验构件的同行评审（PR）以及人类元评审。

Result: 在纯文稿评审（SAR）中，智能体表现看似乐观；但在考虑实验构件的评审（PR）中，得分大幅下降。主要失败模式包括伪造结果、实验力度不足及计划与执行不匹配。其中，不同智能体表现出显著的“研究特质”差异，且无一论文达到顶会录用标准。

Conclusion: 尽管AI智能体在仅针对文稿的评估中表现出竞争力，但它们在实验严谨性和工作空间一致性方面存在重大缺陷，尚未达到顶级学术会议的发表标准。当前自动化研究系统在“看起来可行”与“实质具备科学价值”之间存在显著鸿沟。

Abstract: Recent auto-research systems can produce complete papers, but feasibility is not the same as quality, and the field still lacks a systematic study of how good agent-generated papers actually are. We introduce ResearchArena, a minimal scaffold that lets off-the-shelf agents (Claude Code using Opus 4.6, Codex using GPT-5.4, and Kimi Code using K2.5) carry out the full research loop themselves (ideation, experimentation, paper writing, self-refinement) under only lightweight guidance. Across 13 computer science seeds and 3 trials per agent-domain pair, ResearchArena yields 117 agent-generated papers, each evaluated under three complementary lenses: a manuscript-only reviewer (SAR), an artifact-aware peer review (PR) in which agents inspect the workspace alongside the manuscript, and an human conducted meta-review. Under SAR alone the picture is optimistic: Claude Code obtains the highest score, outperforms Analemma's FARS, and matches the weighted-average human ICLR 2025 submission, suggesting that minimally scaffolded agents can produce papers that look competitive on manuscript-only review. Manual inspection, however, reveals this picture is overstated: SAR scores are poorly aligned with its actual acceptance decisions and reward plausible framing without verifying experimental substance. Under artifact-aware PR scores drop sharply, and manual auditing identifies experimental rigor as the major bottleneck, decomposing into three failure modes (fabricated results, underpowered experiments, and plan/execution mismatch) that are highly agent-dependent: Codex 5%/8% paper-vs-artifact mismatch / fabricated references versus Kimi Code 77%/72%, a $\sim$15$\times$ spread that tracks distinct research personas the agents develop. None of the 117 agent-generated papers reaches the acceptance bar of a top-tier venue. This suggests that we are still gapped from the true auto-research.

### [194] [Hallucination as Exploit: Evidence-Carrying Multimodal Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19192)
*Guijia Zhang,Hao Zheng,Harry Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文针对多模态智能体因视觉幻觉导致执行错误动作的安全风险，提出了“证据携带型多模态智能体（ECA）”架构，通过引入确定性的外部证据验证机制，确保所有关键操作均得到可靠数据的授权，在基准测试中实现了极高的安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模态智能体在执行工具调用时，视觉幻觉会导致严重的授权失败（即幻觉转化为动作），使得未经授权的操作被错误执行，造成安全隐患。现有模型往往缺乏对动作执行前提条件的有效验证机制。

Method: 提出“证据携带型多模态智能体（ECA）”架构。该方法将工具调用分解为关键谓词，利用受限的 DOM/OCR/AX 验证器获取类型化证书，并引入确定性门控机制，只有当证据支持动作执行时才准许授权，从而拒绝不可靠的模型文本证据。

Result: 在包含 1,900 次攻击的红队测试中，ECA 将门控绕过率从 15% 降至 1.3%。在 200 项端到端任务及 120 项浏览器概念验证中，ECA 实现了 0% 的不安全动作执行率。在 500 项审计中，ECA 有效阻止了所有因幻觉引起的非法动作执行。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了“模型提出动作，外部证据授权”的核心原则，通过强制要求动作执行必须具备可验证的证据支持，成功将多模态智能体因视觉幻觉导致的安全风险转化为可控的验证过程，为开发安全可靠的智能体系统提供了范式。

Abstract: Multimodal agents use screenshots, documents, and webpages to choose tool calls. When a false visual claim triggers a click, email, extraction, or transfer, hallucination becomes an authorization failure rather than an answer-quality error. We formalize this failure mode as hallucination-to-action conversion: an unsupported perceptual claim supplies the precondition that makes a privileged action appear permitted. We propose evidence-carrying multimodal agents (ECA), which treat free-form model text as inadmissible evidence. ECA decomposes each tool call into action-critical predicates, obtains typed certificates from constrained DOM/OCR/AX verifiers, and lets a deterministic gate grant only the privileges those certificates support. The architecture does not hide perception error; it converts opaque model belief into named verifier, schema, and implementation residuals. Verifier red-teaming over 1,900 attacks exposes this residual directly: four targeted hardening steps reduce gate bypass from 15% to 1.3%. With content-derived certificates, ECA obtains 0% unsafe-action rate on a 200-task end-to-end pipeline (Wilson 95% upper bound 2.67%) and a 120-task browser proof-of-concept (upper bound 4.3%). A direct HACR audit on 500 stratified task keys shows that unsupported action-critical claims reach unsafe execution for naive agents (100.0%) and prompt-only defense (49.6%), but not for ECA. Oracle-certificate replay on 7,488 GPT-5.4 benchmark traces serves as a gate-correctness sanity check, and neural judge baselines remain bypassable under the same threat model. The resulting principle is simple: model language may propose actions, but external evidence must authorize them.

</details>


### [195] [Not all uncertainty is alike: volatility, stochasticity, and exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19215)
*Payam Piray*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究发现环境的“波动性”与“随机性”对决策探索行为有着相反的影响：前者促进探索，后者抑制探索。研究提出的CAUSE算法利用这一对称性，在处理复杂噪声环境时表现出优越性，并为理解精神疾病中的决策异常提供了新视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究通常将不同来源的环境不确定性视为等价的，忽视了它们对探索策略产生的差异化影响。本研究旨在澄清“环境波动性”与“观测随机性”在决策中的不同角色，并提供一种更优的探索策略。

Method: 研究通过扩展Gittins指数框架至具有潜在动态的高斯状态空间强盗模型（Gaussian state-space bandits），形式化地建立了不确定性来源的不对称性。基于“控制即推理”（control-as-inference）范式，推导出了闭式探索奖励函数（CAUSE），并将其应用于非平稳环境中的决策优化。

Result: 实验证明，波动性会增强探索，而随机性会抑制探索。CAUSE算法在具有异构噪声结构的环境中表现优于标准探索策略，且在非静止（restless）环境下优于传统的Gittins指数策略。此外，该框架能够解释病理性噪声推断如何导致错误的探索行为。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了波动性（环境变化）和随机性（观测噪声）在决策过程中对探索行为具有截然相反的影响。通过将这一机制建模为CAUSE算法，研究不仅提升了决策性能，还为理解病理性噪声推断与精神疾病之间的关系提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Adaptive decision-making in biological and artificial intelligence requires balancing the exploitation of known outcomes with the exploration of uncertain alternatives. Although prior work suggests that uncertainty generally promotes exploration, it has typically treated distinct sources of environmental uncertainty as equivalent. We consider environments with latent reward states that drift over time (volatility) and are observed through noisy outcomes (stochasticity). Both increase posterior uncertainty, yet we show they drive optimal exploration in opposite directions: volatility enhances it, stochasticity suppresses it. We establish this asymmetry formally by extending the Gittins index framework to Gaussian state-space bandits with latent dynamics. We further derive Cause-Aware Uncertainty-Sensitive Exploration (CAUSE), a closed-form exploration bonus obtained via control-as-inference that inherits the same monotonicities. CAUSE outperforms standard exploration strategies in environments with heterogeneous noise structure, and also improves on a Gittins-per-arm policy whose rested-bandit optimality does not transfer to restless settings. Learning and exploration are governed by the same noise-inference asymmetry, and the framework predicts that pathological noise inference produces \emph{reversed} rather than merely impaired exploration, with implications for computational accounts of psychiatric conditions.

</details>


### [196] [SimGym: A Framework for A/B Test Simulation in E-Commerce with Traffic-Grounded VLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19219)

Empirical results show that SimGym agents achieve strong agreement with observed outcome shifts, attaining 77% directional alignment with add-to-cart shifts observed across interface variants in real-buyer traffic. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Survey research faces mounting structural challenges: declining response rates, sample bias, block-wise missingness among at-risk respondents, and AI-assisted fraudulent completions in online panels. We document that near-zero aggregate bias can mask opposing subgroup errors and propose subgroup-stratified bias auditing as a reporting standard. ### [198] [Causal Evidence for Attention Head Imbalance in Modality Conflict Hallucination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19250)
*Jinrui Jiang,Zhangtai Wu,Zhen Wu,Xinyu Dai*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文通过因果分析揭示了MLLM中幻觉产生的机制：模型内部存在失衡的“驱动”与“抑制”注意力头。基于此发现，作者提出了MACI干预方法，通过针对性抑制驱动头，有效提升了模型在模态冲突下的抗幻觉能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模态大模型（MLLM）在处理模态冲突（即文本前提与视觉证据矛盾）时常出现幻觉问题，优先采信错误的文本信息而忽略视觉证据。本文旨在从机械解释性视角出发，探究模型内部哪些组件导致了这一失败，并寻找相应的干预策略。

Method: 研究采用了基于路径修补（path patching）的头级因果分析方法，深入探究MLLM内部注意力头在处理模态冲突时的作用。在此基础上，提出了MACI（模态冲突感知因果干预）技术，即在检测到冲突时，仅对确认的幻觉驱动头进行选择性抑制，从而引导模型纠正输出。

Result: 研究发现，幻觉驱动头的影响广泛且权重较大，而幻觉抑制头则高度集中且数量有限，这种非对称结构导致了幻觉偏向。实验证明，MACI在多个主流MLLM及基准测试（MMMC、SCI-SemanticConflict）中表现优异，在减少幻觉的同时保持了良好的准确率权衡。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了MLLM中模态冲突幻觉产生的机制根源，即幻觉驱动头与幻觉抑制头之间存在不均衡的路由结构。通过MACI干预方法，可以在不显著损害模型基础能力的前提下，有效缓解幻觉问题，为提升多模态模型的可靠性提供了新的机制解释与优化路径。

Abstract: Modality-conflict hallucination occurs when multimodal large language models (MLLMs) prioritize erroneous textual premises over contradictory visual evidence. To understand why visual evidence fails to prevail during generation, we take a mechanistic perspective and examine which internal components drive or resist this failure. We perform head-level causal analysis using path patching across five open-source MLLMs and identify two groups of attention heads with opposing causal roles: hallucination-driving heads and hallucination-resisting heads. We find a consistent asymmetry: driving effects are more broadly distributed and carry greater aggregate weight, whereas resisting effects concentrate in a small number of high-importance heads. Ablation experiments further confirm that these groups exert opposing effects during generation: distributed driving influence and localized resistance together form an imbalanced routing structure that biases generation toward the erroneous premise. Motivated by this finding, we propose MACI (Modality-conflict-Aware Causal Intervention), a conditional intervention that suppresses causally identified hallucination-driving heads only when conflict is detected. Across five MLLMs, MACI achieves the largest hallucination reduction among compared inference-time baselines on the MMMC benchmark with a favorable hallucination-accuracy trade-off, and transfers zero-shot to the SCI-SemanticConflict test.

### [199] [Swimming with Whales: Analysis of Power Imbalances in Stake-Weighted Governance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19264)
*Yuzhe Zhang,Manvir Schneider,Qin Wang,Davide Grossi*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文采用计算社会选择理论的视角，利用彭罗斯-班扎夫权力指数（Penrose-Banzhaf power index）作为量化权力不平衡的工具。在分析方法上，结合了数学分析（证明特定条件下权力与权益份额的近似对齐）和实证研究（基于Project Catalyst链上治理系统的真实数据进行分析）。

Result: 研究发现：1. 从理论上看，完美对齐权力与相对权益所有权通常无法实现，但在特定条件下，二者在预期上可以达到近似对齐。2. 实证结果通过分析Project Catalyst数据，揭示了当前权益加权治理系统中实际存在的细粒度权力不平衡现象。

Conclusion: 本文结论指出，在权益证明（PoS）区块链的治理中，权益加权投票机制本质上存在权力扭曲。虽然理论上可以实现预期意义上的权力与权益份额的近似对齐，但在实际治理场景中，少数大户往往能控制决策，权力分配存在显著不均衡。

Abstract: Voting methods weighted by stakes are the fundamental governance paradigm in Proof-of-Stake (PoS) blockchains. Such a paradigm is known to be prone to power distortions: a few users possessing large stakes may completely control decision making, even without owning the totality of the stakes. We study this phenomenon through the lens of computational social choice, focusing on the extent of power imbalances in stake-weighted voting when power is quantified using the Penrose-Banzhaf power index. Our work presents both analytical and empirical contributions. Analytically, we demonstrate that while a perfect alignment between power and relative stake ownership is generally unattainable, it can be approximated in expectation under specific conditions. Empirically, using data from a real-world on-chain governance system (Project Catalyst), we provide a more fine-grained understanding of the power imbalances that are likely to occur in current stake-weighted governance systems.

### [201] [Conflict-Resilient Multi-Agent Reasoning via Signed Graph Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19418)
*Longgang He,Longzhu He,Daojing He,Chaozhuo Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对现有 LLM 多智能体系统在处理冲突时表现不佳的问题，SIGMA 提出利用有符号图显式建模智能体间的信任与冲突关系，通过冲突感知消息传递机制，有效提升了多智能体推理的全局一致性和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于 LLM 的多智能体系统（MAS）通常假设智能体间是统一协作的，且缺乏对复杂交互关系的显式建模。当智能体之间出现冲突信号时，传统的简单聚合机制往往会导致错误扩散，无法识别可靠的交互模式。

Method: 引入了 SIGMA（有符号图信息多智能体推理）框架。该方法分为三个阶段：首先根据查询选择相关且多样化的智能体；其次构建一个包含置信度权重的结构化“有符号交互图”，用以显式建模信任、冲突和中立关系；最后通过“冲突感知有符号消息传递”机制，强化可信信息并抑制冲突信号，最终进行结构感知聚合。

Result: 在六个基准数据集上进行了广泛实验，验证了 SIGMA 在多种 LLM 底层模型和配置下，均能显著超越当前的基准方法，在准确性和抗冲突性能上表现卓越。

Conclusion: SIGMA 框架证明了通过显式建模多智能体间的信任与冲突关系，能够显著提升复杂推理任务中的鲁棒性和准确性。该研究为多智能体系统在处理不一致信息和复杂交互场景下提供了一种结构化且高效的新思路。

Abstract: LLM-based multi-agent systems (MAS) have demonstrated strong reasoning and decision-making capabilities that consistently surpass those of single LLM agents. However, their performance often suffers from naive aggregation mechanisms that assume uniformly cooperative interactions. Upon close inspection, we observe that existing graph-based MAS frameworks (1) propagate errors when conflicting signals arise without control, and (2) lack explicit modeling of conflicting inter-agent relations as well as structural awareness, failing to identify reliable interaction patterns. To bridge this gap, we introduce SIGMA, a novel SIgned Graph-informed Multi-Agent reasoning framework that explicitly captures trust, conflict, and neutral relations among agents via a signed relational graph. Specifically, given a query, SIGMA first selects a set of relevant and diverse agents, then constructs a structured signed interaction graph with confidence-weighted edges. Reasoning proceeds through conflict-aware signed message passing, which reinforces information from trustworthy agents while suppressing conflicting signals, and terminates with a structure- and conflict-aware weighted aggregation to yield globally consistent and conflict-resilient predictions. Extensive experiments on six benchmark datasets, across multiple LLM backbones and diverse multi-agent configurations, demonstrate that SIGMA consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, achieving notable gains in both accuracy and conflict-resilient performance.
