### [202] [Beyond Mode Collapse: Distribution Matching for Diverse Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19461)
*Xiaozhe Li,Yang Li,Xinyu Fang,Shengyuan Ding,Peiji Li,Yongkang Chen,Yichuan Ma,Tianyi Lyu,Linyang Li,Dahua Lin,Qipeng Guo,Qingwen Liu,Kai Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对在线强化学习中常见的模式坍缩问题，本文提出 DMPO 算法，通过采用前向 KL 散度最小化策略取代传统的反向 KL 最小化，有效地实现了多样性驱动的探索，显著提升了模型在复杂推理任务中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 指出 GRPO 等在线强化学习方法存在“模式坍缩”问题，即模型在发现第一个高奖励解后会集中概率质量，停止对其他潜在策略的探索，这是由于反向 KL 最小化算法固有的模式寻求行为所致。

Method: 提出了一种新的算法 DMPO（分布匹配策略优化），它通过对采样轨迹建立与奖励成正比的目标分布，并利用前向 KL 散度最小化（Forward KL Minimization）的思想来对齐策略分布，从而实现覆盖式的探索而非传统的模式聚焦。

Result: 在 NP-Hard 组合优化基准测试（NP-Bench）中，DMPO 在文本和视觉模态上分别取得了 43.9% 和 43.1% 的质量比，显著优于 GRPO（分别为 40.1% 和 38.4%），并在数学推理及跨域任务中展现了更好的泛化能力。

Conclusion: DMPO 证明了通过分布匹配进行策略优化是一种解决在线强化学习模式坍缩问题的有效、有原则的方法，能够促进持续的探索并显著提升模型在复杂推理任务中的泛化性能。

Abstract: On-policy reinforcement learning methods like GRPO suffer from mode collapse: they exhibit reduced solution diversity, concentrating probability mass on a single solution once discovered and ceasing exploration of alternative strategies. We show this stems from reverse KL minimization's mode-seeking behavior, which reinforces the first high-reward trajectory found rather than maintaining a distribution over multiple diverse solutions. We propose DMPO (Distribution-Matching Policy Optimization), which prevents mode collapse through principled approximation of forward KL minimization. DMPO constructs a group level target distribution over sampled trajectories proportional to their rewards, then aligns the policy distribution to this target. This provides mode-covering behavior without requiring sampling from the intractable global target distribution, enabling sustained exploration throughout training. We validate DMPO on NP-hard combinatorial optimization, where exponentially many feasible solutions exist but only a few approach optimality, an ideal testbed for evaluating exploration. DMPO achieves 43.9% Quality Ratio on text-based NP-Bench (vs. GRPO's 40.1%) and 43.1% on vision-based NP-Bench (vs. 38.4%), demonstrating 9% and 12% relative improvements respectively. These gains generalize to mathematical reasoning (+2.0%) and out-of-domain tasks (+2.3%), showing that diversity-preserving training enhances general reasoning capabilities across modalities. Our work establishes distribution matching as a practical, principled approach to preventing mode collapse in on-policy RL, with consistent quality improvements demonstrating sustained exploration across diverse reasoning tasks.

</details>


### [203] [Attention-Guided Reward for Reinforcement Learning-based Jailbreak against Large Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19485)
*Zheng Lin,Zhenxing Niu,Haoxuan Ji,Yuzhe Huang,Haichang Gao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文揭示了大型推理模型（LRM）的注意力模式是导致其易受越狱攻击的关键因素，并提出了一种基于强化学习、引入注意力奖励机制和多样化说服策略的攻击方法，有效提升了针对LRM的攻击成功率和效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型推理模型（LRM）虽然在解决复杂问题上表现出色，但其暴露出的中间推理步骤带来了新的安全风险。研究人员发现LRM比标准LLM更易受到越狱攻击，且攻击成功率与模型的注意力模式（attention patterns）紧密相关。因此，论文旨在揭示这一机制并开发更有效的攻击方法，以评估模型的脆弱性。

Method: 该研究提出了一种基于强化学习（RL）的新型越狱攻击方法。主要创新点包括：1. 将注意力分配信号显式地纳入强化学习的奖励函数中，引导模型关注诱导性内容；2. 构建了多样化的说服策略（persuasion strategies）以丰富强化学习的动作空间，从而更有效地操纵模型的推理路径。

Result: 在五个主流开源和闭源LRM模型及三个基准测试上的实验表明，该方法在攻击成功率（ASR）上显著优于现有的攻击手段。此外，该方法在攻击的有效性、效率以及跨模型的可迁移性方面均表现出显著优势。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了LRM在推理过程中注意力分配机制与其安全防御漏洞之间的内在联系。通过证明将注意力引导至有害信息可以显著提高攻击成功率，该论文为评估和增强大型推理模型的安全性提供了新的理论视角和防御方向，同时也强调了对推理过程进行安全控制的必要性。

Abstract: Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) have demonstrated remarkable capabilities in solving complex problems by generating structured, step-by-step reasoning content. However, exposing a model's internal reasoning process introduces additional safety risks; for example, recent studies show that LRMs are more vulnerable to jailbreak attacks than standard LLMs. In this paper, we investigate jailbreak attacks on LRMs and reveal that the attack success rate (ASR) is closely correlated with LRMs' attention patterns. Specifically, successful jailbreaks tend to assign lower attention to harmful tokens in the input prompt, while allocating higher attention to those tokens in the reasoning content. Motivated by this finding, we propose a novel jailbreak method for LRMs that leverages reinforcement learning (RL) to enhance attack effectiveness, explicitly incorporating attention signals into the reward function design. In addition, we introduce diverse persuasion strategies to enrich the RL action space, which consistently improves the ASR. Extensive experiments on five open-source and closed-source LRMs across three benchmarks demonstrate that our method achieves substantially higher ASR, outperforming existing approaches in terms of effectiveness, efficiency, and transferability.

</details>


### [204] [Position: The Turing-Completeness of Real-World Autoregressive Transformers Relies Heavily on Context Management](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19514)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献在探讨Transformer的“图灵完备性”时，往往混淆了“固定Transformer系统”与“模型规模族”两个不同概念，导致对模型计算能力的误读。研究旨在正本清源，明确现实世界中LLM的计算能力边界。

Method: 本文采用了理论形式化方法，对Transformer的两种计算设置（固定系统设置与规模族设置）进行了严谨的分类和定义；通过对比分析，指出了现有文献在定义上的混淆，并探讨了上下文管理方法对计算能力的影响。

Result: 研究证明了规模族设置下的结论并不能等同于图灵完备性；形式化了固定系统设置，指出该设置更符合LLM的实际部署场景；揭示了不同的上下文管理方法会显著改变Transformer的计算能力。

Conclusion: 本文明确区分了Transformer在“固定系统”和“规模族”设置下的计算能力差异。研究强调，必须在固定系统设置下探讨图灵完备性，并指出上下文管理机制对于确定现实世界Transformer的计算能力至关重要。

Abstract: Many works make the eye-catching claim that Transformers are Turing-complete. However, the literature often conflates two distinct settings: (i) a fixed Transformer system setting, in which a fixed autoregressive Transformer is coupled with a fixed context-management method to process inputs of different lengths step by step, and (ii) a scaling-family setting, in which a family of different models (with increasing context-window length or numerical precision) is used to handle different input lengths. Existing proofs of Transformer Turing-completeness are frequently established in setting (ii), whereas real-world LLM deployment and the standard notion of Turing-completeness correspond more naturally to setting (i). In this paper, we first formalize the fixed-system setting, thereby providing a concrete characterization of how real-world LLMs operate. We then argue that results proved in the scaling-family setting provide theoretically meaningful resource bounds but do not establish Turing-completeness, thereby clarifying a common misinterpretation of existing results. Finally, we show that different context-management methods can yield sharply different computational power, and we advocate the position that context management is a central component that critically determines the computational power of real-world autoregressive Transformers.

Additionally, we define a set of requirements for achieving (semi)automated (LLM-driven) KG construction, opening new research lines in this area.

### [206] [Efficient Elicitation of Collective Disagreements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19521)
*Mohamed Ouaguenouni,Felipe Garrido-Lucero,Umberto Grandi,César Hidalgo,Magdalena Tydrichova*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文指出两两比较无法揭示投票者的深层分歧结构，因此提出“多数矩阵”框架，量化了计算各种分歧指标所需的最少子集信息，并为平衡调查难度与数据精度提供了可操作的采集协议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的投票调查通常仅基于两两比较或完整排序。然而，两两比较无法区分真正的结构性分歧与随机噪声。因此，本文旨在通过更具结构化的数据框架，识别计算不同分歧度量所需的最少信息量，并优化调查过程。

Method: 1. 提出“多数矩阵”（Plurality Matrix）框架：记录在所有候选子集中，每个候选项被选为第一的概率；2. 定义“分歧度量的层级”（Level of a disagreement measure）：即计算特定度量所需的最小子集规模；3. 设计两种采集协议：平衡参与者人数与认知负荷，用于估计多数矩阵。

Result: 1. 证明了许多经典的分歧度量（如秩方差、分裂度等）处于层级3，即两两比较的信息不足以计算这些指标；2. 从理论和实验层面论证了超越层级3（即使用更高阶子集信息）的重要性；3. 提出的采集协议能够有效权衡参与者数量与认知压力。

Conclusion: 本文确立了理解投票群体分歧结构的理论基础。通过引入“多数矩阵”概念，研究证明了仅依靠两两比较无法捕捉深层的分歧结构，并指出处理复杂分歧度量至少需要三元组及以上层级的信息。该框架为投票系统设计与数据采集策略提供了科学的参考标准。

Abstract: We analyze the structure of the disagreement among a population of voters over a set of alternatives. Surveys typically ask either for pairwise comparisons, simple and intuitive for participants, or full rankings over alternatives, eliciting the entire voters' preferences. Building on the observation that pairwise comparisons cannot distinguish structural disagreement from noise, we propose a stratified framework to identify the minimal aggregated preference information needed to compute a number of disagreement measures from the literature. Specifically, we introduce the plurality matrix, a generalization of pairwise comparisons that records, for every subset $S$ of alternatives, the probability that each $a \in S$ ranks first in $S$. We define the level of a disagreement measure as the smallest subset size needed to express it, showing that many existing notions, including rank-variance and divisiveness, sit at level $3$, proving that pairwise comparisons are not enough. In addition, we demonstrate the interest of going beyond level $3$ both theoretically and experimentally. To make these results actionable, we design two elicitation protocols to estimate the plurality matrix, exploring the trade-off between the number of required participants and the cognitive load requested to each of them.

### [207] [Generative-Evaluative Agreement: A Necessary Validity Criterion for LLM-Enabled Adaptive Assessment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19529)
*Grandee Lee,Yue Wang,Che Yee Lye,Luke Peh*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出了“生成-评估一致性”（GEA）框架，用于量化检测大模型在自动化测评闭环中的可靠性，发现模型虽能处理简单技能，但在复杂设计任务上存在严重一致性偏差，并提出了改进评分标准的应对策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大模型在生成评估题目、模拟学生回答及评分的过程中形成了闭环，容易产生自我指涉偏差。现有研究缺乏对该闭环有效性的量化衡量标准，因此需要一种方法来验证大模型生成的内容与评分的一致性。

Method: 提出了“生成-评估一致性”（GEA）这一指标，用于衡量大模型的评分函数是否能准确还原其生成函数所设定的学生能力水平。通过在两阶段自适应评估中进行直接测量，并对比不同类型技能的评分表现来验证其有效性。

Result: 实验显示GEA整体相关系数为0.698，存在系统性正向偏差。模型在语法可验证技能上表现强劲（r > 0.7），但在设计类技能上接近零相关；此外，低技能水平下的高估现象会导致路由阈值附近的评分虚高。

Conclusion: GEA是评估大模型自动化测试流程有效性的关键指标。研究发现大模型在处理结构化技能时表现较好，但在设计类技能上失效，且存在系统性偏见。通过使用细粒度、基于技能分解的评分标准，可以有效提升模型生成与评估的一致性。

Abstract: When the same LLM generates assessment items, simulates student responses, and scores them, the validation loop is self-referential. We introduce Generative-Evaluative Agreement (GEA), a validity criterion measuring whether an LLM's scoring function recovers the skill levels its generative function was instructed to produce. In the first direct measurement of GEA on a two-stage adaptive assessment, the model recovers roughly half the intended variance r = 0.698 with systematic positive bias. GEA is strong r > 0.7 for syntactically verifiable skills but near zero for design-level skills, and low-skill overestimation inflates scores near the routing threshold. We argue that granular, skill-decomposed rubrics are the principal proposed mechanism for strengthening GEA and outline complementary mitigations.

### [208] [Library Drift: Diagnosing and Fixing a Silent Failure Mode in Self-Evolving LLM Skill Libraries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19576)
*Xing Zhang,Yanwei Cui,Guanghui Wang,Ziyuan Li,Wei Qiu,Bing Zhu,Peiyang He*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自演进技能库存在“库漂移”现象，即技能无限制累积且缺乏生命周期管理，导致检索质量下降、误报增加及性能停滞。现有研究发现LLM自动编写的技能往往无法带来性能提升，本文旨在探究其深层机制并提出治理方案。

Method: 1. 实验重现：通过切片实验（消融研究）分离并确认库漂移现象；2. 追踪诊断：构建包含技能贡献分数、归因判断和路由指标的追踪日志；3. 治理策略：引入结果驱动的退休机制、有界主动上限和元技能编写先验，并进行了八项消融实验以验证各治理组件的有效性。

Result: 在MBPP+ hard-100数据集上，通过实施治理策略，将模型保持集的pass@1准确率从0.258提升至0.584（提升了0.328），证明了该治理方案能有效抑制库漂移并显著提升模型表现。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了“库漂移”是自演进技能库性能停滞的核心原因，并证明了通过结果驱动的生命周期管理（退休机制、容量上限和元技能先验）可以有效解决该问题，为构建稳健的智能体技能库提供了具体的治理方案。

Abstract: Self-evolving skill libraries face a silent failure mode we term \emph{library drift}: unbounded skill accumulation without outcome-driven lifecycle management causes retrieval degradation, false-positive injections, and performance stagnation. Recent evaluation confirms the symptom--LLM-authored skills deliver +0.0pp gain while human-curated ones deliver +16.2pp (SkillsBench)--yet the underlying mechanism has not been isolated. We provide (1) a reproducible trigger: ablations that isolate drift--one disables skill injection (flat floor, +0.002), one imposes premature retirement (active harm, $-$0.019); (2) trace-level diagnostics: an append-only evidence log with per-skill contribution scores, attribution verdicts, and router engagement metrics that make the failure visible before it reaches end-task scores; and (3) a verified fix: a minimal governance recipe (outcome-driven retirement + bounded active-cap + meta-skill authoring prior) that lifts held-out pass@1 from a 0.258 baseline to a late-window mean of 0.584 (rolling gain $+$0.328) on MBPP+ hard-100 over 100 rounds. Eight ablations decompose which governance mechanisms are load-bearing and which are subsumed, providing a concrete playbook for diagnosing library drift in any self-evolving agent.

### [209] [Towards Multi-Model LLM Schedulers: Empirical Insights into Offloading and Preemption](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19593)
*Mert Yildiz,Pietro Spadaccino,Alexey Rolich,Francesca Cuomo,Andrea Baiocchi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文通过实证研究揭示了在异构硬件上部署多大模型时，层卸载和抢占对性能的复杂影响，并为构建下一代高效LLM服务调度系统提供了关键的设计准则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大模型部署需求日趋多样化，需要在共享的异构硬件上同时运行多个不同架构和规模的模型。然而，现有的系统多针对单模型吞吐量优化，缺乏针对显存受限情况下（需部分卸载或抢占）多模型调度策略的研究。

Method: 作者通过实证研究的方法，分析了不同大语言模型（LLM）在异构硬件平台上的行为，重点考察了层卸载（layer offloading）和抢占（preemption）对推理性能的影响，并量化了模型状态重载、键值（KV）缓存传输、序列长度以及互连带宽对性能的影响。

Result: 研究发现：1) 卸载会导致解码吞吐量呈现强非线性且与模型相关的下降，小模型对GPU驻留率的降低更为敏感；2) 抢占带来的高昂开销主要源于模型状态重载，而非KV缓存的传输，且该成本在不同模型和硬件上差异显著；3) 序列长度和互连带宽会显著放大数据移动和执行效率低下的问题。

Conclusion: 未来的大模型服务调度系统必须考虑模型特定的卸载敏感度、工作负载特性以及抢占与数据传输的成本结构，以应对异构环境下的多模型服务需求。

Abstract: Modern deployments of Large Language Models (LLMs) increasingly require serving multiple models with diverse architectures, sizes, and specialization on shared, heterogeneous hardware. This setting introduces new challenges for resource allocation, dispatching, and scheduling, particularly under GPU memory constraints where partial CPU-GPU offloading and preemption become necessary. While existing systems primarily optimize throughput for a single model, comparatively little work addresses multi-model scheduling under these conditions. In this paper, we present an empirical study of how different LLMs behave across hardware platforms, focusing on the performance implications of layer offloading and preemption. We show that offloading leads to strongly non-linear and model-dependent degradation in decode throughput, with smaller models exhibiting sharper sensitivity to reduced GPU residency. We further demonstrate that preemption incurs substantial overhead, largely dominated by model state reload rather than key-value cache transfer, and that this cost varies significantly across models and hardware platforms. Additionally, we highlight the role of sequence length and interconnect bandwidth in amplifying data movement and execution inefficiencies. Based on these findings, we identify a set of key features that future schedulers must consider, including model-specific offloading sensitivity, workload characteristics, and the cost structure of preemption and data transfer. These insights provide guidance for the design of next-generation LLM serving systems capable of efficiently managing heterogeneous, multi-model workloads with hybrid CPU-GPU execution.

</details>

Thus, generalizing to deepfakes unseen during training is one of the major challenges in current deepfake detection research. To tackle this challenge, we employ high-level semantic cues and argue that these cues can support low-level focused approaches in generalizing to unseen types of manipulations. In this work, we study emotions as a high-level semantic cue. We propose Emo-Boost, a multimodal deepfake detection framework that fuses an off-the-shelf RGB- and acoustic-focused deepfake detector with our emotion-based deepfake detector EmoForensics. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视觉语言模型（VLM）在机器人自动化应用中极易产生幻觉，导致决策失误并带来安全隐患，且由于现实世界任务的复杂性和开放性，缺乏鲁棒的推理策略。

Method: 提出了一种名为 PStar（Pseudocode-guided Structured Reasoning）的框架。该方法设计了一套抽象推理函数和结构化伪代码库，并引入了“难度特征向量”（DFV）来评估任务复杂度，使模型能够根据任务需求动态选择最合适的推理策略。

Result: 实验表明 PStar 显著降低了幻觉率，在 POPE 基准测试中达到 87.1%，在 MMStar 基准测试中达到 68.0%，性能优于 GPT-4V。

Conclusion: PStar 框架通过结构化思维路径和动态难度评估，有效降低了视觉语言模型的幻觉问题，为在现实世界自动化系统中部署更安全、确定性更高的机器人视觉语言模型提供了关键方案。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) are becoming the cornerstone of high-level reasoning for robotic automation, enabling robots to parse natural language commands and perceive their environments. However, their susceptibility to hallucinations introduces critical failures in decision-making, posing significant safety and reliability risks in physical deployments. This challenge is exacerbated by the open-ended nature of real-world tasks, where questions vary vastly in difficulty and modality, demanding robust and adaptable reasoning strategies. To tackle this, we propose the Pseudocode-guided Structured Reasoning framework (PStar), which adaptively selects structured pseudocode reasoning paths to help VLMs perform flexible and step-by-step reasoning. We first design a set of abstract reasoning functions and formulate a structured pseudocode library to represent modular reasoning strategies. Crucially, we design a Difficulty Feature Vector (DFV) that allows the model to assess question complexity and adaptively choose appropriate reasoning strategies-enhancing robustness and interpretability. Extensive experiments demonstrate that PStar significantly reduces hallucination rates, achieving state-of-the-art scores of 87.1% on POPE and 68.0% on MMStar, outperforming even GPT-4V. By providing a validated mechanism to reduce visual-language errors, PStar offers a critical step toward deploying more trustworthy and deterministic VLMs for real-world automated systems, where such errors can lead to catastrophic outcomes.

### [213] [CogScale: Scalable Benchmark for Sequence Processing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19758)
*Yannis Bendi-Ouis,Romain de Coudenhove,Xavier Hinaut*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了 CogScale，一套用于评估AI模型认知与记忆能力的轻量级合成任务基准。它允许研究人员在小规模、低成本下快速筛选模型架构，研究发现注意力机制和状态空间模型在处理复杂推理时的扩展性能远优于传统RNN架构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代AI模型在序列处理任务中虽取得巨大成功，但评估新架构的记忆与推理能力需要在大规模数据集上进行完整训练，导致计算成本高昂且迭代极其缓慢。因此，需要一套轻量级、可扩展的基准测试，以便在早期阶段快速验证模型架构的创新。

Method: 作者提出了 CogScale 基准测试，包含 14 个可参数化缩放的合成任务，旨在隔离并评估特定的认知与记忆能力。研究在严格的参数预算（1k, 10k, 100k）下，对比了七种不同架构（GRU、LSTM、xLSTM、ESN、Mamba、Transformer Decoder 和 Transformer Encoder-Decoder）在不同难度等级下的表现。

Result: 实验结果表明，在严苛的参数预算限制下，传统的RNN（如GRU、LSTM）和Echo State Networks在基础信息留存任务上表现优异；然而，随着任务复杂度和推理难度的增加，只有注意力机制（Transformer）和现代状态空间模型（Mamba）能够保持稳定的高性能。

Conclusion: CogScale 提供了一个高效、标准化的基准框架，能够有效评估不同架构在处理序列信息时的认知与记忆能力。研究证明，注意力机制和现代状态空间模型在处理复杂推理任务时表现出显著的扩展优势，而传统RNN在小参数量下更具效率。该工具能显著加速新型AI架构的研发迭代周期。

Abstract: The ability to maintain and manipulate information over time is a fundamental aspect of living beings and Artificial Intelligence. While modern models have achieved remarkable success in tasks like natural language processing, evaluating the capacity of novel architectures to process sequential information remains computationally expensive and time-consuming. Testing a new architecture often requires scaling up to massive datasets and models, leading to vast computational costs and slow iteration cycles. In this paper, we propose CogScale, a benchmark of 14 scalable synthetic tasks designed to isolate and evaluate specific cognitive and memory abilities at different parametrizable scales. By providing a standardized, lightweight framework, CogScale allows researchers to rapidly validate architectural innovations before committing to large-scale training. To establish a solid baseline, we evaluate seven distinct architectures: Gated Recurrent Unit (GRU), Long Short-Term Memory (LSTM), xLSTM, Echo State Network (ESN), Mamba, Transformer Decoder, and Transformer Encoder-Decoder. These evaluations are conducted under strict parameter budgets (1k, 10k, and 100k) and across different difficulty levels and scales. Our results show that while classical RNNs and Echo State Networks excel at basic retention within strict parameter budgets, only attention mechanisms and modern state-space models consistently maintain high performance as reasoning complexity and task difficulty scale.

### [214] [What Really Improves Mathematical Reasoning: Structured Reasoning Signals Beyond Pure Code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19762)
*Yuze Zhao,Junpeng Fang,Lu Yu,Zhenya Huang,Kai Zhang,Qing Cui,Qi Liu,Jun Zhou,Enhong Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究揭示了代码数据对语言模型能力的真实影响：代码主要提升编程能力而非通用推理，且在复杂任务中与数学推理存在竞争关系；研究指出，结构化的推理轨迹（而非单纯的可执行代码）是提升推理性能的关键，建议采用更精准的数据构成策略来优化特定能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管代码已成为现代基础语言模型训练的标准组成部分，但其在编程以外领域（特别是通用推理）的实际作用机制尚不明确，论文旨在澄清代码数据对模型不同能力维度的真实影响，以实现更精准的数据驱动模型优化。

Method: 通过在大规模的 10T token 语料库上进行细粒度的受控预训练实验，剥离编程能力、通用推理及知识密集型任务的影响，对比不同类型数据（可执行代码、代码-文本混合、结构化数学轨迹）对模型性能的作用，并结合专家路由（Expert-activation）分析探究数据组成与模型内部机制的交互。

Result: 1. 代码数据主要增强编程能力，而非通用推理能力，且与知识密集型任务（尤其是复杂数学推理）存在性能竞争；2. 过去认为的“代码带来的推理提升”更多源于代码-文本混合等结构化推理轨迹；3. 增加结构化数学样本的密度能有效提升复杂数学推理能力，且不损害编程性能；4. 实验证明了不同领域数据在模型内部存在明显的竞争与协同交互。

Conclusion: 研究表明，代码数据并非通用的推理增强器，其对模型性能的影响具有领域特异性。未来的模型训练应超越单纯的“代码增益”假设，转而采用更具针对性的数据构成策略，通过优化结构化推理轨迹（如数学推理轨迹）来实现特定能力的提升，同时平衡不同领域间的竞争与协同效应。

Abstract: Code has become a standard component of modern foundation language model (LM) training, yet its role beyond programming remains unclear. We revisit the claim that code improves reasoning through controlled pretraining experiments on a 10T-token corpus with fine-grained domain separation. Our findings are threefold. First, when code is restricted to standalone executable programs and Code-NL data are controlled for, code substantially improves programming ability but does not act as a general reasoning enhancer; instead, it competes with knowledge-intensive tasks, especially complex mathematical reasoning. Second, the reasoning gains often attributed to code are better explained by cross-domain structured reasoning traces, such as code-text and math-text mixtures, rather than by executable code alone. Third, increasing the density of structured math-domain samples within a fixed math budget yields substantial gains on difficult mathematical reasoning while largely preserving programming performance, suggesting that cognitive scaffolds offer a targeted way to mitigate cross-domain trade-offs. Finally, routing analyses show that data-composition effects are reflected in expert-activation patterns, providing mechanism-level evidence for competitive and synergistic interactions across domains. Our results clarify which data characteristics transfer across capability dimensions and point to more precise data-centric optimization strategies.

### [215] [GroupAffect-4: A Multimodal Dataset of Four-Person Collaborative Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19765)
*Meisam Jamshidi Seikavandi,Alice Modica,Anna Obara,Shan Ahmed Shaffi,Fabricio Batista Narcizo,Tanya Ignatenko,Ted Vucurevich,Karim Haddad,Daniel Barratt,Daniel Overholt,Jesper Bunsow Boldt,Paolo Burelli,Andrew Burke Dittberner*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建了一个包含40名参与者（10个四人小组）的多模态语料库，通过腕戴式生理传感器、眼动眼镜、近讲麦克风、实时自我报告及任务结果记录多维度数据，利用BIDS标准组织数据并进行时间对齐，最终定义了15个涵盖个体、人际与群体层面的基准评估任务。

Result: 该数据集数据质量高（生理数据完整率超91%，眼动数据超98%），通过谈判任务验证了其情感操纵的有效性，并提供了基于“留一小组法”（leave-one-group-out）的基准评估结果，证明了其在多种分析任务下的可行性。

Abstract: Existing affective-computing, social-signal-processing, and meeting corpora capture important parts of human interaction, but they rarely support analysis of affect in co-located groups as a coupled individual, interpersonal, and group-level process. The required signals (per-participant physiology, eye movement, audio, self-report, task outcomes, and personality) are usually fragmented across separate dataset traditions. We introduce GroupAffect-4, a multimodal corpus of 40 participants in 10 four-person groups, each completing four ecologically varied collaborative tasks spanning information pooling, negotiation, idea generation, and a public-goods game. Each participant is instrumented with a wrist-worn physiology sensor, eye-tracking glasses, and a close-talk microphone; sessions include continuous affect self-reports, post-task questionnaires, task outcomes, and Big-Five personality scores, all time-aligned to a shared clock. The dataset covers over 91% of expected physiology windows and 98% of eye-tracking windows, with strong task validity confirmed by a clear affective manipulation check across the negotiation block. We define fifteen benchmarkable targets spanning three analysis levels -- within-person state, between-person traits, and group dynamics -- and report leave-one-group-out feasibility baselines establishing the dataset's evaluative scope. GroupAffect-4 is released with a BIDS-inspired structure, Croissant metadata, a datasheet, per-session quality reports, and open processing scripts. Code and processing scripts are available at https://github.com/meisamjam/GroupAffect-4; the dataset is publicly archived at https://zenodo.org/records/20037847.

### [216] [Minimax Optimal Variance-Aware Regret Bounds for Multinomial Logistic MDPs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19768)
*Pierre Boudart,Pierre Gaillard,Alessandro Rudi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了多项式逻辑（MNL）混合MDP的强化学习，通过引入问题依赖的方差常量 $\bar{\sigma}_T$，提出了一种改进的算法，实现了在结构化问题中优于现有最坏情况的遗憾界，并证明了该界的极小极大最优性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多项式逻辑（MNL）混合MDP算法在最坏情况下的遗憾界为 $\tilde{O}(dH^2\sqrt{T})$，但在面对具有特定结构的MDP时，该界可能不够紧凑。研究动机在于利用问题的结构化信息（如价值函数的方差）来改进遗憾界，从而获得更精确的复杂度刻画。

Method: 作者借鉴逻辑赌博机文献中的思想，引入了一个问题依赖常量 $\bar{\sigma}_T$，该常量衡量了最优下游价值函数沿轨迹的归一化平均方差。基于此，提出了一种新的强化学习算法，实现了 $\tilde{O}(dH^2\bar{\sigma}_T\sqrt{T})$ 的遗憾界。此外，作者还推导了匹配的下界 $\Omega(dH^2\bar{\sigma}_T\sqrt{T})$ 以验证最优性。

Result: 所提出的算法在最坏情况下恢复了现有的遗憾界，并在结构化MDP（如KL约束鲁棒MDP）中，通过将水平依赖性降低了 $H$ 倍，显著提升了性能。同时，通过下界证明，确立了该算法在对数因子范围内的极小极大最优性。

Conclusion: 本文通过引入与问题相关的方差参数，成功刻画了多项式逻辑（MNL）混合MDP的遗憾复杂度，并证明了所提算法的极小极大最优性。该研究完善了此类模型在强化学习中的理论框架，证明了在特定结构化MDP中，性能能够得到显著提升。

Abstract: We study reinforcement learning for episodic Markov Decision Processes (MDPs) whose transitions are modelled by a multinomial logistic (MNL) model. Existing algorithms for MNL mixture MDPs yield a regret of $\smash{\tilde{O}(dH^2\sqrt{T})}$ (Li et al., 2024), where $d$ is the feature dimension, $H$ the episode length, and $T$ the number of episodes. Inspired by the logistic bandit literature (Abeille et al., 2021; Faury et al., 2022; Boudart et al., 2026), we introduce a problem-dependent constant $\barσ\_T \leq 1/2$, measuring the normalised average variance of the optimal downstream value function along the learner's trajectory. We propose an algorithm achieving a regret of $\smash{\tilde{O}(dH^2\barσ\_T\sqrt{T})}$, which recovers the existing bound in the worst case and improves upon it for structured MDPs. For instance, for KL-constrained robust MDPs, $\barσ\_T = O(H^{-1})$, reducing the horizon dependence by a factor $H$. We further establish a matching $\smash{Ω(dH^2\barσ\_T\sqrt{T})}$ lower bound, proving minimax optimality (up to logarithmic factors) and fully characterising the regret complexity of MNL mixture MDPs for the first time.

### [217] [OpenComputer: Verifiable Software Worlds for Computer-Use Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19769)
*Jinbiao Wei,Qianran Ma,Yilun Zhao,Xiao Zhou,Kangqi Ni,Guo Gan,Arman Cohan*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: OpenComputer 由四个核心模块构成：1. 应用状态验证器：为真实应用程序提供结构化的状态检查接口；2. 自进化验证层：利用执行反馈机制持续提升验证器的准确性；3. 任务生成管线：合成真实且可机器验证的桌面任务；4. 评估框架：记录完整操作轨迹并计算可审计的分步奖励。该系统覆盖了 33 种桌面应用及 1,000 个精细化任务。

Conclusion: OpenComputer 框架有效解决了现有计算机使用智能体评估中存在的“幻觉”和评估不准确问题。实验表明，基于程序状态验证的评估比传统的“大模型作为裁判”方法更符合人类评判标准，同时也揭示了当前主流智能体在处理细粒度、长轨迹任务时的稳健性短板。

Abstract: We present OpenComputer, a verifier-grounded framework for constructing verifiable software worlds for computer-use agents. OpenComputer integrates four components: (1) app-specific state verifiers that expose structured inspection endpoints over real applications, (2) a self-evolving verification layer that improves verifier reliability using execution-grounded feedback, (3) a task-generation pipeline that synthesizes realistic and machine-checkable desktop tasks, and (4) an evaluation harness that records full trajectories and computes auditable partial-credit rewards. In its current form, OpenComputer covers 33 desktop applications and 1,000 finalized tasks spanning browsers, office tools, creative software, development environments, file managers, and communication applications. Experiments show that OpenComputer's hard-coded verifiers align more closely with human adjudication than LLM-as-judge evaluation, especially when success depends on fine-grained application state. Frontier agents struggle with end-to-end completion despite partial progress, and open-source models exhibit sharp drops from their OSWorld-Verified scores, exposing a persistent gap in robust computer automation.

### [218] [Distribution-Free Uncertainty Quantification for Continuous AI Agent Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19779)
*Yuxuan Gao,Megan Wang,Yi Ling Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于保形预测（Conformal Prediction）的持续性AI智能体评估框架，通过自适应机制提供无分布覆盖保证，有效量化了多智能体管道中的不确定性，并在实际评估中展现了对性能波动和排名不稳定性的强大监控能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的AI智能体评估方法往往缺乏统计严谨性和动态调整能力，难以应对智能体性能的持续波动以及复杂的多智能体流水线带来的不确定性。研究旨在提供一种具备无分布（distribution-free）覆盖保证的框架，以实现对AI智能体质量评分及排名的持续、可靠评估。

Method: 研究采用了分裂保形预测（split conformal prediction）和自适应保形推断（ACI）方法。通过构建多智能体管道的组合不确定性界，设计了针对成对排名的保形弃权规则，并应用FDR（错误发现率）校正处理大规模排行榜的多重假设检验。评估过程基于18个实时小时级信号，并采用了循环控制验证方法来评估信号的有效性。

Result: 在24小时预测周期内，保形区间校准误差低于0.02；ACI机制在智能体更新后能有效调整区间宽度（扩展35%）；在评估50个智能体时，实现了良好的条件覆盖水平（均值80.4%）；实验表明交叉源情感差异能有效预测排名不稳定性（r=0.64），且该框架能够捕捉到超越传统基准的性能信号。

Conclusion: 本文提出的框架成功地将保形预测应用于持续性AI智能体评估，不仅提供了严谨的无分布覆盖保证，还能在面对智能体性能波动时进行动态调整。这一方法论为评估复杂多智能体系统提供了可靠的统计框架，证明了利用不确定性量化来提升智能体评估的稳健性和可解释性是切实可行的。

Abstract: We adapt split conformal prediction and adaptive conformal inference (ACI) to continuous AI agent evaluation, providing distribution-free coverage guarantees for forecasted quality scores. Conformal intervals achieve calibration error below 0.02 across all nominal levels at the 24h horizon, while ACI correctly widens intervals by 35% following agent releases then reconverges. We further develop compositional uncertainty bounds for multi-agent pipelines (validated via simulation across inter-stage correlations rho in [-0.5, 0.9]), a conformal abstention rule for pairwise rankings with controlled false-ranking rate, and FDR-corrected abstention for leaderboard-scale multiple testing. Evaluating 50 agents via 18 real-time signals collected hourly, we show that per-agent conditional coverage is well-concentrated around the nominal level (mean 80.4%, 90% of agents within [72%, 90%]), and that cross-source sentiment divergence predicts ranking instability (r=0.64, p<0.01). A circularity-controlled validation confirms the framework captures signal beyond benchmarks (rho_s=0.52, p<0.01, n=35). Code and data are released under CC BY 4.0.

</details>

Result: 实验结果显示，引入时间条件限制虽然改变了模型的推理方式，但在标准的NLP正确性指标上并未产生统计学意义上的显著提升。然而，定性分析表明，该方法在预测性危险推理、稳定的纠正行为以及策略性决策方面表现出明显的优势。

Abstract: Recent attempts to support high-level scene interpretation and planning in Autonomous Vehicles (AVs) using ensembles of Large Language Models (LLMs) and Large Multimodal Models (LMMs) continue to treat time as a secondary property. This lack of temporal grounding leads to inconsistencies in reasoning about continuous actions, undermining both safety and interpretability. This work explores whether temporal conditioning within inter-agent communication can preserve or enhance coherence without introducing degradation in semantic or logical consistency. To investigate this, we introduce three planner architectures with progressively increasing temporal integration and evaluate them on curated subsets of the BDD-X dataset using semantic, syntactic, and logical metrics. Results show that while temporal conditioning reshapes reasoning style, it yields no statistically significant improvements in standard NLP-based correctness metrics. However, qualitative analysis reveals predictive hazard reasoning, stable corrective behavior, and strategic divergence in the Sentinel. These findings clarify the limits of prompt-based temporal grounding and establish the first empirical benchmark for temporal scene-to-plan reasoning.

### [220] [Robotics-Inspired Guardrails for Foundation Models in Socially Sensitive Domains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19940)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基础模型防护措施多关注单次输出的安全性，且缺乏可执行的行为保证，难以应对教育、心理健康等领域中累积性、上下文相关的风险。因此，需要一种能够控制整体交互轨迹的方法。

Method: 提出“Grounded Observer”（接地观察者）框架。该方法借鉴机器人学中的闭环控制理论，将防护栏（guardrails）重新定义为对交互轨迹的运行时行为控制，而非单纯对单个输出的过滤，从而在不确定性环境中实现对模型行为的动态干预。

Result: 通过在社交闲聊、自闭症家庭治疗及学校行为降级等三个真实场景中的部署验证，该框架成功实现了对模型交互偏差的运行时抑制，并在保持适应性的同时有效防止了模型进入不理想的交互状态。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了将基础模型视为闭环控制系统并引入形式化约束，能够有效提升其在社会敏感领域中的交互安全性和可靠性，为未来构建具备行为保证的AI系统提供了新范式。

Abstract: Foundation models are increasingly deployed in socially sensitive domains such as education, mental health, and caregiving, where failures are often cumulative and context-dependent. Existing guardrail approaches -- ranging from training-time alignment to prompting, decoding constraints, and post-hoc moderation -- primarily provide empirical risk reduction rather than enforceable behavioral guarantees, and largely treat safety as a property of individual outputs rather than interaction trajectories. We reframe guardrails as a problem of runtime behavioral control over interaction trajectories, drawing on robotics to introduce formal constructs for constraint enforcement in uncertain, closed-loop systems. We instantiate these ideas in the Grounded Observer framework and apply it across three real-world deployments: small talk, in-home autism therapy, and behavioral de-escalation in schools. Across settings, the framework enables runtime interventions that mitigate drift into undesirable interaction regimes while adapting to diverse social contexts. We discuss extensions to the framework and propose research directions toward stronger guarantees.

### [221] [Probabilistic Tiny Recursive Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19943)
*Amin Sghaier,Ali Parviz,Alexia Jolicoeur-Martineau*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: PTRM 通过在微型递归模型的每一步注入噪声进行随机探索，并利用内置的 Q head 择优，以极低的成本显著提升了复杂推理任务的准确率，超越了许多大规模模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的微型递归模型（TRM）因其确定性的递归过程，容易陷入次优解且缺乏脱困机制。现有的解决方法（如输入扰动）通常依赖于特定任务，缺乏通用性，因此需要一种无需重训练且任务无关的通用框架来实现测试时的计算扩展。

Method: 提出“概率性递归模型（PTRM）”框架，在深度递归的每一步注入高斯噪声，从而生成多条并行的求解轨迹；利用模型原有的 Q head（价值评估头）对这些轨迹进行评估并择优，从而避开局部最优解。

Result: PTRM 在无需重新训练的情况下大幅提升了性能。在 Sudoku-Extreme 上准确率从 87.4% 提升至 98.75%；在 Pencil Puzzle Bench 上准确率从 62.6% 提升至 91.2%，且在仅使用 7M 参数的情况下，其准确率达到主流大模型（55.1%）的近两倍，计算成本不到其万分之一。

Conclusion: PTRM 通过在递归过程中引入随机性，有效提升了小规模模型在复杂推理任务上的性能，证明了在有限参数下通过测试时计算（Test-time compute）扩展实现高性能推理的可行性。该方法无需重训练，具有极高的通用性和成本效益。

Abstract: Tiny Recursive Models (TRM) solve complex reasoning tasks with a fraction of the parameters of modern large language models (LLMs) by iteratively refining a latent state and final answer. While powerful, their deterministic recursion can lead to convergence at suboptimal solutions, without escape mechanism. A common workaround relies on task-specific input perturbations at test time combined with answer aggregation via voting. We introduce Probabilistic TRM (PTRM), a task-agnostic framework for test-time compute scaling that addresses this limitation through stochastic exploration. PTRM injects Gaussian noise at each deep recursion step, enabling parallel trajectories to explore diverse solution basins, and selects among them using the model's existing Q head (used for early stopping in the original TRM). Without requiring retraining or task-specific augmentations, PTRM enables substantial accuracy gains across benchmarks, including Sudoku-Extreme (87.4% to 98.75%) and on various puzzles from Pencil Puzzle Bench (62.6% to 91.2%). On the latter, PTRM achieves nearly double the accuracy of frontier LLMs (91.2% vs. 55.1%) at less than 0.0001x the cost, using only 7M parameters.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Geospatial reasoning requires solving image-grounded problems over the complex spatial structure of a scene. However, developing this capability is hindered by the cost of annotating a vast and combinatorial question space. We propose GeoX, a self-play framework that acquires spatial logic through executable programs that yield verifiable rewards, without relying on large-scale human-curated data Given a satellite or aerial image, our framework employs a single multimodal policy that proposes spatial problems as executable programs and solves them under three reasoning modes-abduction, deduction, and induction-over spatial primitives and an image understanding tool. A verifier executes each program to covert a reward signal that jointly optimizes the two roles via reinforcement learning. GeoX consistently improves its base VLMs by up to 5.5 points on average, matching or exceeding conventional baselines trained on millions of curated data. Along-side the proposed method, we release a benchmark for geospatial understanding accumulated through self-play.

### [223] [AutoResearchClaw: Self-Reinforcing Autonomous Research with Human-AI Collaboration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20025)
*Jiaqi Liu,Shi Qiu,Mairui Li,Bingzhou Li,Haonian Ji,Siwei Han,Xinyu Ye,Peng Xia,Zihan Dong,Congyu Zhang,Letian Zhang,Guiming Chen,Haoqin Tu,Xinyu Yang,Lu Feng,Xujiang Zhao,Haifeng Chen,Jiawei Zhou,Xiao Wang,Weitong Zhang,Hongtu Zhu,Yun Li,Jieru Mei,Hongliang Fei,Jiaheng Zhang,Linjie Li,Linjun Zhang,Yuyin Zhou,Sheng Wang,Caiming Xiong,James Zou,Zeyu Zheng,Cihang Xie,Mingyu Ding,Huaxiu Yao*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: AutoResearchClaw 证明了多智能体协作、自我修复机制以及人机协同是提升科研自动化水平的关键。它定位为科研放大器，旨在增强而非取代人类的科学判断力。

Abstract: Automating scientific discovery requires more than generating papers from ideas. Real research is iterative: hypotheses are challenged from multiple perspectives, experiments fail and inform the next attempt, and lessons accumulate across cycles. Existing autonomous research systems often model this process as a linear pipeline: they rely on single-agent reasoning, stop when execution fails, and do not carry experience across runs. We present AutoResearchClaw, a multi-agent autonomous research pipeline built on five mechanisms: structured multi-agent debate for hypothesis generation and result analysis, a self-healing executor with a \textsc{Pivot}/\textsc{Refine} decision loop that transforms failures into information, verifiable result reporting that prevents fabricated numbers and hallucinated citations, human-in-the-loop collaboration with seven intervention modes spanning full autonomy to step-by-step oversight, and cross-run evolution that converts past mistakes into future safeguards. On ARC-Bench, a 25-topic experiment-stage benchmark, AutoResearchClaw outperforms AI Scientist v2 by 54.7%. A human-in-the-loop ablation across seven intervention modes reveals that precise, targeted collaboration at high-leverage decision points consistently outperforms both full autonomy and exhaustive step-by-step oversight. We position AutoResearchClaw as a research amplifier that augments rather than replaces human scientific judgment. Code is available at https://github.com/aiming-lab/AutoResearchClaw.

### [224] [Neurosymbolic Learning for Inference-Time Argumentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20098)
*Gabriel Freedman,Adam Dejl,Adam Gould,Mansi,Lihu Chen,Jianqi Jiang,Francesca Toni*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为ITA的神经符号框架，通过将形式论证语义引入大语言模型，实现了对声明的高忠实度、可解释的三元验证，在保持竞争力的同时解决了模型推理的“黑盒”问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在医疗和金融等高风险领域，声明验证往往面临信息不全或冲突的情况，传统的二元（真/假）分类不足以表达不确定性。此外，现有的大模型推理方法通常依赖于“事后解释（post-hoc reasoning）”，缺乏逻辑忠实度。因此，研究旨在开发一种既能处理三元验证，又能提供忠实、可审查、基于逻辑论证的决策框架。

Method: 作者提出了一种名为“推理时论证（Inference-time Argumentation, ITA）”的神经符号框架。该方法的核心在于利用形式论证语义（Formal Argumentation Semantics）作为模型训练与预测的桥梁：(1) 在训练阶段，利用论证强度来引导大语言模型生成论点并评估其内在强度；(2) 在推理阶段，根据生成的论点及其得分，通过确定性的形式计算得出“真/假/不确定”的三元判决结果，确保预测逻辑与论证过程保持一致。

Result: 实验表明，ITA框架在两个三元声明验证数据集上均优于现有的论证类基准模型，并与非论证类直接预测模型表现相当。最重要的是，ITA产生的决策具备确定性，直接源于可检查的显式论证结构，而非黑盒预测。

Conclusion: 推理时论证（ITA）框架成功将形式论证语义与大语言模型结合，通过提供可解释且忠实的推理过程，为三元声明验证任务提供了一种既具备高性能又具备透明度的新范式。它证明了模型推理过程可以与最终判决逻辑保持一致，从而解决了传统模型中“事后解释”可能存在的不可靠问题。

Abstract: Claim verification is an important problem in high-stakes settings, including health and finance. When information underpinning claims is incomplete or conflicting, uncertain answers may be more appropriate than binary true or false classifications. In all cases, faithful explanations of the considerations determining the final verdict are crucial. We introduce inference-time argumentation (ITA), a trainable neurosymbolic framework for ternary claim verification in which a formal argumentation semantics giving the strength of claims is used both (i) to guide LLM training as models learn to generate arguments and assign them base scores (representing intrinsic strengths) and (ii) to compute ternary (true/false/uncertain) predictions from generated, scored arguments. As a result, at training time, argument generation and scoring can be optimised according to the quality of the induced argumentative predictions. Moreover, at inference time, the final prediction is faithful, by construction, to the arguments and scores determining the verdict, rather than being justified by a potentially unfaithful post-hoc reasoning trace as in conventional reasoning models. We finally show that, on two datasets for ternary claim verification, ITA improves upon argumentative baselines and can perform competitively against non-argumentative direct-prediction baselines, while providing verdicts that are computed deterministically from explicit, inspectable argumentative structures.

</details>


### [225] [Using Aristotle API for AI-Assisted Theorem Proving in Lean 4: A Formalisation Case Study of the Grasshopper Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20120)
*Gabriel Rongyang Lau*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文通过对IMO 2009 Grasshopper问题的Lean 4形式化案例分析，揭示了AI辅助定理证明的现状：AI擅长处理局部推导，但在处理需要复杂全局组合逻辑的证明时，仍存在严重的逻辑缺口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管AI在生成奥林匹克数学竞赛水平的Lean形式化证明方面已取得进展，但其证明的可靠性取决于最终代码的实际可验证性。本研究旨在探讨AI生成证明在实际形式化验证过程中的局限性，特别是局部证明搜索与全局数学逻辑整合之间的脱节问题。

Method: 研究采用案例分析法，对由Aristotle API生成的关于IMO 2009第六题（Grasshopper问题）的Lean 4形式化证明进行审计。研究者将AI生成的证明代码转化为Lean 4代码，逐一验证其中的辅助引理（helper lemmas），并明确界定了哪些部分通过了形式化验证，哪些部分仍处于未证明状态（sorry）。

Result: 研究表明，该AI模型成功证明了四个关键的辅助引理，涵盖了最大化策略和相邻交换策略的局部组件，但最终未能证明主要定理，遗留了一个核心的“sorry”点。Aristotle API虽识别出了所需的全局计数步骤，但未能将其转化为可验证的形式化逻辑。该研究提供了一个可复现的Lean工件，精确剖析了AI生成证明中已验证与未验证内容的比例。

Conclusion: 该研究通过具体的案例分析指出，当前人工智能辅助定理证明在处理奥赛级别数学问题时存在核心局限：AI能够有效地完成局部逻辑推理和辅助引理的证明，但在处理需要全局组合逻辑会计（global combinatorial bookkeeping）的复杂步骤时，往往难以自动收尾，仍需人工干预。

Abstract: AI-assisted theorem proving can now generate substantial Lean developments for olympiad-level mathematics, but the evidential status of such developments depends on which declarations are actually verified. This paper reports a Lean 4 formalization case study of an Aristotle API proof attempt for the Grasshopper problem, originally posed as IMO 2009 Problem 6. The generated artifact states a generalized Lean version of the theorem, contains four verified helper lemmas for local components of a maximality and adjacent-swap exchange strategy, and leaves the main theorem grasshopper closed directly by one unresolved sorry. The verified components establish that the final partial sum equals the total sum, that an adjacent transposition can affect only the relevant intermediate partial sum, that the changed partial sum has the expected form, and that maximality at a position admitting an adjacent successor swap forces a corresponding forbidden-set membership fact. The Aristotle output summary identifies the intended remaining mathematical step as the global counting step needed to show that these membership facts produce at least n distinct forbidden values, contradicting the cardinality assumption |M| < n; the Lean source itself does not reduce the main theorem to a separately encoded counting lemma. This case study gives an inspectable example of a central limitation in AI-assisted formalization, namely that local proof search can succeed while the global combinatorial bookkeeping required for a theorem remains unresolved. The paper contributes a reproducible Lean artifact and a precise analysis of its verified and unverified proof content.

### [226] [Not Every Rubric Teaches Equally: Policy-Aware Rubric Rewards for RLVR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20164)
*Utkarsh Tyagi,Xingang Guo,MohammadHossein Rezaei,Daniel George,Anas Mahmoud,Jackson Lee,Bing Liu,Yunzhong He*

TL;DR: 论文提出了POW3R框架，通过将“评估指标”与“学习引导信号”解耦，在保持模型最终评估标准不变的情况下，动态调整强化学习过程中的准则权重，有效提升了模型训练的收敛速度和整体性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于准则（Rubric-based）的强化学习方法通常使用静态聚合方式将多个准则加权求和，这导致评估目标与优化信号混淆。在训练中，重要但已饱和或无法触及的准则会干扰模型学习，而真正对提升当前策略有帮助的区分性准则权重却不足，限制了训练效率和模型最终性能。

Method: 提出了一种名为POW3R的策略感知评分奖励框架。该方法在保留原始人工定义的评分准则及其权重作为最终优化目标的前提下，引入了基于Rollout层面的对比机制，根据策略当前阶段的表现动态调整各准则在训练过程中的权重，从而使得奖励信号更具区分度和信息量。

Result: 在多模态和纯文本两个数据集上，使用三个基础模型进行测试，POW3R在30次对比实验中获胜24次。与传统GRPO相比，不仅显著提高了平均奖励分和严格满足所有准则的比例，还将训练效率提升了2.5至4倍。

Conclusion: POW3R通过动态调整训练过程中的准则权重，成功解耦了“评估目标（人设权重）”与“学习信号（优化动力）”，证明了在强化学习训练中，区分“最终期望表现”与“当前教学重点”对提升模型训练效率和表现至关重要。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards has made post-training highly effective when correctness can be checked automatically. However, many important model behaviors require satisfying several qualitative criteria at once. Rubric-based rewards address this setting by grading prompt-specific criteria and aggregating them into a scalar reward. Yet standard static aggregations conflate a criterion's human-assigned importance with its current usefulness as an optimization signal. We show that this assumption breaks down in rubric RL: many important criteria are already saturated or currently unreachable, while criteria that distinguish rollouts are not necessarily those with the largest human weights. We introduce POW3R, a policy-aware rubric reward framework that preserves human weights and category balance as the rubric objective while adapting criterion-level reward weights during training. POW3R uses rollout-level contrast to emphasize criteria that currently separate the policy's outputs, making the GRPO reward more informative without changing the underlying evaluation target. Across three base policies on two datasets spanning multimodal and text-only settings, POW3R wins $24$ of $30$ base-policy/metric comparisons, improving both mean rubric reward and strict completion (the fraction of prompts whose response satisfies every required rubric criterion) over vanilla GRPO with rubric rewards, and reaches the same plateau in $2.5$--$4\times$ fewer training steps. Rubric rewards should therefore distinguish what should matter in the final answer from what can teach the current policy.

</details>


### [227] [A Methodology for Selecting and Composing Runtime Architecture Patterns for Production LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20173)
*Vasundra Srinivasan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了“随机-确定性边界（SDB）”架构概念，将其作为生产级LLM智能体运行时的核心原语，并提供了一套系统化的设计模式与方法论，以解决模型随机性与系统确定性之间的兼容问题，从而提升智能体的长期运行可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的生产级LLM智能体在结合随机性模型输出与确定性软件系统时，缺乏统一的架构范式。作者旨在填补这一空白，通过将模型与系统间的交互边界形式化，为构建可靠、可控的生产级智能体提供架构指导。

Method: 本文将智能体运行时设计分解为协调、状态和控制三个维度，定义了包含提案者、验证者、提交步骤和拒绝信号的SDB四部分契约。在此基础上，提出了六种针对不同智能体类型（对话式、自主式等）的运行模式，引入了五步选择方法论及故障诊断流程，并识别了“重放分歧（Replay Divergence）”这一特有失效模式。

Result: 通过五个工作负载验证了方法论，并提供了一个90天合同续签智能体的可运行参考实现。研究表明，通过规范化SDB并选择合适的运行模式，可以有效管理模型随机性带来的不确定性，提高长周期智能体运行的可靠性。

Conclusion: 本文提出了“随机-确定性边界（SDB）”作为构建生产级LLM智能体运行时的核心原语。随着LLM模型本身方差的降低，系统的可靠性将越来越依赖于合理的架构模式设计与SDB契约的严密性。该方法论为开发者提供了系统化构建高可靠智能体的方法。

Abstract: Production LLM agents combine stochastic model outputs with deterministic software systems, yet the boundary between the two is rarely treated as a first-class architectural object. This paper names that boundary the stochastic-deterministic boundary (SDB): a four-part contract among a proposer, verifier, commit step, and reject signal that specifies how an LLM output becomes a system action. We argue that the SDB is the load-bearing primitive of production agent runtimes.
  Around this primitive, we organize agent runtime design into three concerns: Coordination, State, and Control. We present a catalog of six runtime patterns that compose the SDB differently across conversational, autonomous, and long-horizon agents: hierarchical delegation, scatter-gather plus saga, event-driven sequencing, shared state machine, supervisor plus gate, and human in the loop. For each pattern, we trace its lineage to distributed-systems concepts and identify what changes when the worker is stochastic.
  The paper contributes a five-step methodology for selecting runtime patterns, a diagnostic procedure that maps production failures to pattern weaknesses, and a failure mode called replay divergence, in which LLM-based consumers of a deterministic event log produce different downstream outputs under model-version or prompt changes. A stylized reliability decomposition separates per-call model variance from architectural momentum, motivating the claim that as model variance decreases, pattern choice and SDB strength become increasingly important levers for long-run reliability. We apply the methodology to five workloads and provide one runnable reference implementation for a 90-day contract-renewal agent.

</details>

### [228] [DOTRAG: Retrieval-Time Reasoning Along Paths](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18760)
*Larnell Moore,Naihao Deng,Rada Mihalcea,Farnaz Jahanbakhsh*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: DotRAG 是一种创新的免训练 GraphRAG 框架，通过引入“思维拆分”机制，将检索过程转化为基于查询条件的迭代式推理与路径探索，从而在处理复杂多跳任务时展现出卓越的准确性与鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 GraphRAG 方法主要基于“先检索、后推理”的范式，依赖启发式检索。这种方式难以适应复杂多跳任务所需的查询特定逻辑，容易导致无关上下文的冗余或关键关系路径的丢失。因此，作者旨在构建一种能够将检索过程本身转化为推理过程的新框架。

Method: 提出了一种名为 DotRAG 的免训练 GraphRAG 框架。该框架引入了“思维拆分”（Division of Thought, DOT）机制，将检索任务分解为多个局部搜索空间，并根据查询生成特定的约束条件来引导图探索。这种方法能够实时剪枝无关区域，并以迭代方式发现潜在的关系路径，而无需依赖显式的步骤推理链。

Result: DotRAG 在 MetaQA 和 UltraDomain 数据集上均达到了 SOTA（最先进）性能水平，在多跳任务中表现出了显著且一致的性能提升，验证了推理引导检索的有效性。

Conclusion: DotRAG 通过将检索过程重新定义为推理过程，有效克服了传统 GraphRAG 在处理复杂多跳任务时的局限性。该方法证明了将推理引导与图检索相结合，能够显著提升模型在处理复杂逻辑任务时的准确性和适应性。

Abstract: Graph Retrieval-Augmented Generation (GraphRAG) is dominated by a retrieve-then-reason paradigm, where context is retrieved using heuristics and then reasoned over. Such methods struggle to adapt to the query-specific logic required for complex multi-hop tasks, often accumulating irrelevant context or missing correct relational paths. We propose DotRAG, a training-free GraphRAG framework that reformulates retrieval as a reasoning process over paths. Our approach generates query-conditioned constraints that guide graph exploration, prune irrelevant regions, and iteratively discover relational paths without relying on explicit step-by-step reasoning chains. We introduce Division of Thought (DOT), an abstraction that decomposes retrieval into localized search spaces and adapts the search strategy to each query. DotRAG achieves SOTA performance on MetaQA and UltraDomain, with consistent gains on multi-hop tasks, demonstrating the effectiveness of reasoning-guided retrieval.

</details>


### [229] [ALDEN: Boosting Private Data Extraction from Retrieval-Augmented Generation Systems via Active Learning and Distribution Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18762)
*Xingyu Lyu,Jianfeng He,Ning Wang,Yidan Hu,Tao Li,Danjue Chen,Shixiong Li,Yimin Chen*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出了 ALDEN 攻击框架，通过主动学习和知识库主题分布估计，显著增强了从 RAG 系统中窃取私有数据的能力，证明了现有 RAG 系统的安全性漏洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然检索增强生成（RAG）技术被广泛应用，但其仍面临数据提取攻击的威胁。现有攻击方法存在数据提取率低和实际效果有限的问题，作者旨在开发一种更高效、更具攻击性的方法以揭示 RAG 系统的脆弱性。

Method: ALDEN 攻击框架主要包含两个核心模块：1. 利用主动学习（Active Learning）技术生成多样化的恶意查询，以提高对私有数据的提取覆盖率；2. 引入基于衰减的动态算法（Decay-based Dynamic Algorithm），通过估计知识库的主题分布来指导恶意查询的生成，从而更精准地定位目标数据。

Result: 实验评估表明，ALDEN 能够显著超越现有的前沿攻击方法，在提取效率和成功率上均有大幅提升。

Conclusion: ALDEN 证明了通过结合主动学习和知识库分布估计，能够显著提升针对 RAG 系统的私有数据提取攻击的效率与成功率，揭示了当前 RAG 系统在安全性方面的严峻挑战。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) is widely used to augment large language models with external knowledge retrieval to improve reliability and generalization. However, recent studies have shown that RAG systems remain vulnerable to data extraction attacks, where adversaries can extract private data by embedding malicious commands into user queries. Despite their feasibility, existing attacks typically suffer from low data extraction rates and limited practical effectiveness. Here, we propose ALDEN, a novel attack that effectively and efficiently extracts private data from RAGs. First, we employ active learning to diversify malicious queries and improve data extraction rates. Second, we observe that the data distribution of the underlying knowledge base provides valuable guidance for query generation and introduce a decay-based dynamic algorithm to estimate the corresponding topic distribution. By combining them together, we demonstrate that ALDEN substantially outperforms state-of-the-art methods through comprehensive evaluations.

</details>


### [230] [Query-Conditioned Graph Retrieval for Contextualized LLM Reasoning in Personalized Wearable Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18763)
*Zhenyu Lu,Mahyar Abbasian,Amir M. Rahmani*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在处理可穿戴传感数据时，面临如何在有限的上下文窗口内，平衡数据完整性、推理效率与生成质量的挑战。现有的简单检索方法难以应对可穿戴数据长期、多模态且高度个性化的特性。

Method: 提出了“Wearable As Graph (WAG)”框架，将可穿戴指标和用户信号组织成个性化知识图谱。该方法整合了分层贝叶斯建模捕获的全局关系（包含先验知识及群体/个体模式）与反映短期信号偏差的局部关系，并利用查询开放性信号（Query Openness Signal）动态控制检索广度，以实现查询自适应的子图检索。

Result: 在超过10,000个真实世界数据查询的基准测试中，WAG框架在基于LLM和人工评估中表现优异，胜率较基准方法和标准RAG方法提升了约70%。

Conclusion: WAG框架通过结构化知识图谱和查询自适应检索机制，有效解决了大型语言模型在处理长期、多模态及高度个性化可穿戴传感数据时的上下文选择难题，是实现精准可穿戴数据分析的有效方案。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly applied to analyzing wearable sensing data, which are long-term, multimodal, and highly personalized. A key challenge is context selection: providing insufficient context limits reasoning, while including all available data leads to inefficiency and degraded generation quality. We propose Wearable As Graph (WAG), a graph-based context retrieval framework that enables query-adaptive reasoning over wearable data with LLMs. WAG organizes wearable metrics and user-specific signals into a personalized knowledge graph, and retrieves a query-conditioned subgraph to support downstream generation. The retrieval process integrates global relationships, capturing prior knowledge and population- and individual-level patterns via hierarchical Bayesian modeling, with local relationships that reflect short-term signal deviations. A query openness signal further controls retrieval breadth. We evaluate WAG on over 10,000 data-grounded queries from real-world wearable datasets. Across LLM-based and human evaluations, WAG achieves an approximately 70% win rate over baseline and standard RAG methods, demonstrating the effectiveness of structured, query-adaptive context retrieval for LLM-driven analysis of wearable data.

### [231] [STAR: Semantic-Tuned and Tail-Adaptive Retriever for Graph-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18765)
*Shuai Li,Chen Huang,Duanyu Feng,Wenqiang Lei,See-Kiong Ng*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对GraphRAG在知识图谱检索中存在的语义建模不足问题，STAR通过引入词级交互学习和尾部自适应对比学习，显著减少了检索偏差，提升了多跳问答的整体性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的GraphRAG方法在多跳问答任务中存在显著局限性，具体表现为“语义捷径偏差”（Semantic Shortcut Bias）和“长尾路径偏差”（Long-Tail Path Bias），导致模型对复杂图结构的语义建模能力不足，检索准确性受限。

Method: 提出STAR（Semantic-tuned and Tail-adaptive Retriever）模型，包含两个核心模块：1. 基于交叉注意力机制和硬路径挖掘的词级交互学习，旨在增强查询与路径的深度语义建模，消除语义捷径偏差；2. 基于尾部自适应路径加权的对比学习目标，通过优化训练过程，解决长尾路径带来的偏差问题。

Result: 在多个基准测试数据集上的实验表明，STAR模型在检索性能和LLM问答准确率上均优于现有基线方法，平均检索性能提升1.8%，LLM问答效果提升2.2%。

Conclusion: 本文提出的STAR框架通过语义调优和长尾适应性策略，有效缓解了GraphRAG在多跳问答中存在的语义捷径偏差和长尾路径偏差问题，提升了检索质量及问答效果，为图检索增强生成提供了一种鲁棒的解决方案。

Abstract: To augment Large Language Models (LLMs) for multi-hop question answering, a mainstream solution within Graph Retrieval Augmented Generation (GraphRAG) leverages lightweight retrievers to efficiently extract information from a given Knowledge Graph (KG). However, existing methods often overlook the inherent challenge of sparse semantic information in graphs. Specifically, our experiments reveal that these methods produce biased retrieval Semantic Shortcut Bias and Long-Tail Path Bias, leading to inadequate semantic modeling and limited GraphRAG effectiveness. To address these issues, we propose STAR, a semantic-tuned and tail-adaptive retriever for GraphRAG. STAR integrates two key learning paradigms: token-level interaction learning and path-weighted contrastive learning. The former employs a cross-attention architecture and a hard path mining mechanism to jointly model the query and path, thereby mitigating the Semantic Shortcut Bias. The latter introduces a tailored contrastive learning objective that utilizes tail-adaptive path weighting, designed to optimize the training process and ease the Long-Tail Path Bias. Extensive experiments demonstrate that STAR consistently outperforms baselines, achieving average retrieval performance gains of 1.8\% and LLM QA performance improvements of 2.2\% across all benchmark datasets. Our code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/STAR-C583.

</details>


### [232] [Retrieve Only Relevant Tables Whether Few or Many: Adaptive Table Retrieval Method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18766)
*Taehee Kim,Seungbin Yang,Jihwan Kim,Jaegul Choo*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对文本转SQL任务中表检索固定数量（Top-k）的缺陷，本文提出了一种能够根据查询需求自适应调整检索表数量的方法，有效提升了检索的准确性与下游任务表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的Top-k表检索方法强制要求检索固定数量的表，但这忽略了不同查询对数据需求量的差异，导致要么因表数量不足而丢失关键信息，要么因包含无关表而引入噪声，影响下游任务的性能。

Method: 提出了一种自适应表检索方法，包含两个核心组件：1. 自适应阈值机制，根据查询需求动态确定检索的表数量；2. 滑动窗口重排序算法，用于在大型数据库中高效筛选和排序相关表。

Result: 在Spider、BIRD和Spider 2.0等基准数据集上的广泛实验表明，该方法在表检索准确率及下游文本转SQL任务的性能上均显著优于传统的固定Top-k检索策略。

Conclusion: 自适应表检索方法通过动态调整检索表数量，有效解决了传统Top-k检索策略在处理复杂查询时存在的表覆盖不足或噪声过多的问题，为文本转SQL等任务提供了更高效、准确的基础支撑。

Abstract: Retrieving relevant tables from extensive databases for a given natural language query is essential for accurately answering questions in tasks such as text-to-SQL. Existing table retrieval approaches select a pre-determined set of k tables with the highest similarity to the query. However, the number of required tables varies across queries and cannot be known in advance. Enforcing a fixed number of retrieved tables regardless of the query may either retrieve an undersized set, failing to obtain all necessary evidence, or retrieve an oversized pool, including irrelevant tables. To address this issue, we propose an adaptive table retrieval method that adjusts the number of tables retrieved according to the requirements of each query. Specifically, we utilize an adaptive thresholding mechanism to selectively retrieve tables and integrate a sliding-window reranking algorithm to efficiently process a large table corpus. Extensive experiments on Spider, BIRD, and Spider 2.0 demonstrate that our method effectively addresses the limitations of the top-k retrieval strategy, improving performance in retrieval and downstream tasks. Our code and data are available at https://github.com/sbY99/Adaptive-Table-Retrieval.

</details>


### [233] [DualView: Adaptive Local-Global Fusion for Multi-Hop Document Reranking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18767)
*Litong Zhang,Jiaxin Li,Kuo Zhao*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 论文提出了一种轻量级双视图级联重排序框架，通过整合文档局部相关性和全局依赖，以极低的延迟显著提升了多跳问答检索任务的准确率和召回率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多跳问答需要整合多个文档的信息，核心挑战在于如何从检索到的候选文档中高效地识别出最相关的最小文档集，同时保持高召回率。现有的交叉编码器模型参数量大且延迟高，难以满足高效推理需求。

Method: 提出了一种双视图级联重排序框架，包含两个核心组件：（1）局部评分器（Local Scorer）：使用堆叠式交叉注意力机制捕捉细粒度的查询-文档相关性；（2）全局评分器（Global Scorer）：利用基于Transformer的上下文聚合模型来建模文档间的相互依赖关系。此外，通过一个由查询语义条件驱动的自适应门控机制进行动态融合。

Result: 在MuSiQue数据集上，该模型取得了99.4%的Top-4召回率和97.8%的Full Hit准确率，推理延迟仅为4.0毫秒（249 QPS）。其性能显著超过了参数量高达600M的交叉编码器模型（如BGE-Large和Jina-v3），且延迟降低了5到6倍。

Conclusion: 该论文提出的双视图级联重排序框架通过结合局部相关性和全局文档依赖，在多跳问答任务中实现了极高的检索召回率和推理效率，证明了轻量级模型结合特定任务架构设计在处理复杂检索任务时的有效性。

Abstract: Multi-hop question answering requires aggregating information from multiple documents, a critical capability for knowledge-intensive applications. A fundamental challenge lies in efficiently identifying the minimal relevant document set from retrieved candidates while maintaining high recall.
  We present an efficient dual-view cascaded reranking framework for multi-hop document reranking. Operating as a lightweight post-retrieval stage over E5-base-v2 candidates, our architecture comprises: (1) a Local Scorer employing stacked cross-attention for fine-grained query-document relevance; and (2) a Global Scorer modeling inter-document dependencies via Transformer-based context aggregation. These views are dynamically fused through an Adaptive Gate conditioned on query semantics.
  Under the fixed candidate set reranking setting with offline cached embeddings, our model achieves competitive results, particularly outstanding on MuSiQue with 99.4% Top-4 Recall and 97.8% Full Hit accuracy at 4.0 ms latency (249 QPS). It substantially outperforms 600M-parameter cross-encoders (BGE-Large: 92.0% Recall, Jina-v3: 90.1% Recall) while maintaining 5 to 6 times lower latency. Ablation studies validate that both Local and Global views contribute substantially to multi-hop performance.

</details>


### [234] [ClusterRAG: Cluster-Based Collaborative Filtering for Personalized Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18769)
*Gibson Nkhata,Uttamasha Anjally Oyshi,Quan Mai,Susan Gauch*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出了ClusterRAG框架，通过基于密度的用户聚类和协同过滤机制，利用相似用户群体的知识来优化个性化RAG检索，在保持高效性的同时显著提升了生成任务的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的个性化RAG方法存在检索成本高的问题，且未能充分利用相似用户之间的协作信号（Collaborative Signals）来辅助当前用户的生成任务，导致个性化效果受限。

Method: 提出ClusterRAG框架：利用用户的个人文档构建用户表示，通过基于密度的聚类算法将语义相似的用户归为一组；在检索阶段，实施“集群级相似度检索”与“文档级细粒度排序”的两阶段检索策略，结合目标用户及其相似用户群体的知识进行协同增强。

Result: 在LaMP基准测试中，ClusterRAG在多个任务上均表现出最优性能；实验证明该方法可无缝集成不同的稠密检索器和重排序器，无论是在微调模型还是零样本（zero-shot）语言模型上均表现出卓越的有效性。

Conclusion: ClusterRAG通过聚类机制有效整合了个人资料与协作信号，证明了在个性化RAG任务中利用相似用户群体的知识可以显著提升生成质量，且具备良好的模型兼容性与扩展性。

Abstract: Personalized Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) relies on accurately selecting user-relevant documents. In practice, existing RAG approaches often suffer from high retrieval costs and overlook that collaborative signals from similar users can enhance personalized generation for the current user. We propose ClusterRAG, a Cluster-Based Collaborative Filtering for Personalized Retrieval-Augmented Generation. ClusterRAG represents users through their profile documents, organizes users into semantically coherent clusters using density-based clustering, and performs retrieval at both the cluster and document levels via cluster-level similarity and fine-grained ranking. Extensive experiments on the LaMP benchmark demonstrate that jointly leveraging the target user's profile and profiles from top similar users consistently yields the best performance across diverse tasks. Further analysis shows that ClusterRAG integrates seamlessly with different dense retrievers and rankers, and remains effective when paired with both fine-tuned and zero-shot language models.

</details>

A human-in-the-loop dashboard exposes evidence and execution traces to support transparency and auditability. First, fixed instructions cannot capture the multidimensional heterogeneity of user interests. Second, uncontrollable knowledge fusion may conflict with behavioral signals and harm recommendations. ### [237] [M3DocDep: Multi-modal, Multi-page, Multi-document Dependency Chunking with Large Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18774)
*Joongmin Shin,Jeongbae Park,Jaehyung Seo,Heuiseok Lim*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种名为 M3DocDep 的基于多模态大语言模型（LVLM）的流水线：首先利用 SharedDet 作为预处理层，通过边界感知 SoftROI 池化提取多模态块嵌入；接着利用双仿射头（biaffine head）对块间的父子关系边进行评分，并结合最小生成树（MST）约束解码出全局有效的文档依赖树；最后基于该树结构构建包含章节路径和页码范围标注的文档块。

Abstract: In long, multi-page industrial documents, retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) depends heavily on whether chunk boundaries follow the document's true structure. Existing text-centric chunkers and generative hierarchy parsers often miss cross-page parent-child relations, figure/table-caption bindings, and boundary cues, which leads to fragmented or redundant chunks and degrades both retrieval and answer quality. We propose M3DocDep, an LVLM-based pipeline that first recovers block-level dependencies and then constructs chunks along the recovered document tree. The pipeline uses SharedDet as a common DP+OCR preprocessing layer, extracts multimodal block embeddings with boundary-aware SoftROI pooling, scores candidate parent-child edges with a biaffine head, decodes a globally valid dependency tree with MST constraints, and builds tree-guided chunks annotated with section paths and page ranges. Under a shared-block evaluation protocol, M3DocDep improves STEDS by +28.5 to +39.6 percent on DHP benchmarks, retrieval nDCG by +1.1 to +15.3 percent, and QA ANLS by +4.5 to +15.3 percent on corpus-level RAG benchmarks. *Zhuoping Zhou,Davoud Ataee Tarzanagh,Sima Didari,Wenjun Hu,Baruch Gutow,Oxana Verkholyak,Masoud Faraki,Heng Hao,Hankyu Moon,Seungjai Min*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的图增强生成（Graph RAG）方法主要存在两个问题：一是缺乏子图质量或相关性的理论保障，二是静态探索策略往往忽视查询的深层语义，导致检索到无关的图结构。

Method: 提出了一种无需训练的框架 QAFD-RAG。该方法通过查询感知遍历，根据图节点与查询语义的对齐程度动态加权边，引导信息流在语义相关的路径上扩散，从而生成针对特定查询的推理子图。

Result: 实验结果表明，QAFD-RAG 在问答和 Text-to-SQL 任务中均优于现有的前沿图 RAG 方法。此外，该算法在温和的信噪比条件下具有统计学保证，且具备指数级的收敛速度，计算复杂度仅与检索到的子图规模相关。

Conclusion: QAFD-RAG 提供了一种基于查询感知流扩散的高效、理论可证明的图检索方法，有效地解决了传统方法在子图质量和检索意图对齐方面的不足，为知识图谱增强生成提供了更优的路径探索机制。

Abstract: Graph-based Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) systems leverage interconnected knowledge structures to capture complex relationships that flat retrieval struggles with, enabling multi-hop reasoning. Yet most existing graph-based methods suffer from (i) heuristic designs lacking theoretical guarantees for subgraph quality or relevance and/or (ii) the use of static exploration strategies that ignore the query's holistic meaning, retrieving neighborhoods or communities regardless of intent. We propose Query-Aware Flow Diffusion RAG (QAFD-RAG), a training-free framework that dynamically adapts graph traversal to each query's holistic semantics. The central innovation is query-aware traversal: during graph exploration, edges are dynamically weighted by how well their endpoints align with the query's embedding, guiding flow along semantically relevant paths while avoiding structurally connected but irrelevant regions. These query-specific reasoning subgraphs enable the first statistical guarantees for query-aware graph retrieval, showing that QAFD-RAG recovers relevant subgraphs with high probability under mild signal-to-noise conditions. The algorithm converges exponentially fast, with complexity scaling with the retrieved subgraph size rather than the full graph. Experiments on question answering and text-to-SQL tasks demonstrate consistent improvements over state-of-the-art graph-based RAG methods.

Abstract: Reasoning-based Large Language Models (LLMs) like PO4ISR have set new benchmarks in session-based recommendation. ### [241] [Trust or Abstain? A Self-Aware RAG Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18792)
*Xi Zhu,Ziqi Wang,Kai Mei,Wujiang Xu,Minghao Guo,Bangji Yang,Jiajun Fan,Dimitris N. Metaxas*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对RAG中检索知识与模型内置知识的冲突问题，本文提出了一种无需微调的自我意识信念估计器（SABER），通过分析推理路径并结合轻量级预测器，实现了更精准的冲突决策与风险控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检索增强生成（RAG）在引入外部知识时，常因检索到的上下文知识（CK）与大语言模型内置的参数化知识（PK）不一致或两者均不可靠而引发知识冲突。现有的研究多关注于简单的来源协调，缺乏对回答路径正确性的深入自我反思，因此需要赋予LLM识别自身知识局限性的“自我意识”。

Method: 1. 构建了一个包含约69K条查询-上下文实例的基准测试，用于评估LLM在仅依赖参数化知识（PK）与结合检索上下文知识（CK）两种路径下的表现；
2. 提出了SABER（Self-Aware Belief Estimator）框架，无需对LLM进行微调；
3. SABER利用多轨迹推理获取PK侧和CK侧的条件推理表示，并结合自先验（Self-prior），通过两个轻量级预测器进行置信度评估；
4. 采用“四格决策”策略（信任PK、信任CK、信任两者或弃权）来优化最终输出。

Result: SABER在四个LLM骨干模型上均优于十种推理时或微调基准模型，特别是在高冲突数据集上表现显著。此外，SABER在弃权机制下的风险-覆盖曲线优于现有的所有基于提示（prompt-based）的弃权方法，实现了覆盖率与回答风险之间的有效平衡。

Conclusion: 本研究表明，通过引入SABER这种基于模型自我认知的评估机制，RAG系统能够更有效地处理参数化知识与检索上下文知识之间的冲突。这种无需微调的方法不仅显著提升了回答的准确性和忠实度，还通过提供可调节的风险覆盖曲线，使模型在决策时更加稳健和可控。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) improves large language models (LLMs) by incorporating external evidence, but it also introduces knowledge conflicts when retrieved contextual knowledge (CK) and parametric knowledge (PK) disagree or are both unreliable. Existing approaches mainly coordinate which source to use, without explicitly asking whether each answer path is correct. We argue that faithful RAG requires LLM self-awareness, namely the ability to recognize the limits of its own knowledge and reasoning. To ground this problem, we construct a model-specific, ground-truth-aligned knowledge-conflict benchmark by evaluating LLM backbones on PK-only and CK-conditioned answer paths over approximately 69K query-context instances per backbone, drawn from five conflict-QA datasets. We then introduce SABER, a Self-Aware Belief Estimator for RAG that requires no LLM fine-tuning. SABER combines a self-prior with PK-side and CK-side conditional reasoning representations from multi-trace inference, then estimates reliability beliefs with two lightweight predictors to drive a 4-cell decision over trust PK, trust CK, trust either, or abstain. Across four LLM backbones, SABER improves end-to-end accuracy and conflict-specific faithfulness over ten inference-time and fine-tuning baselines, with the largest gains on conflict-heavy datasets. Under abstention, SABER's risk-coverage curve Pareto-dominates every prompt-based abstainer, providing a tunable balance between coverage and answer risk. Our code is available at https://github.com/xizhu1022/SABER.

</details>


### [242] [Towards FairRAG: Preventing Representational Harm in Retrieval-Augmented Generation by Enforcing Fair Exposure at Retrieval Time](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18806)
*Riddhi Tikoo*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文探讨了检索增强生成（RAG）系统中偏见的传播问题，证明了检索排序阶段的偏差是导致下游生成偏见的主要原因，并提出了一种“代表性随机”排序策略来有效平衡曝光公平性与系统效用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管检索增强生成（RAG）被用于缓解大语言模型（LLM）的幻觉问题，但 RAG 的多组件流水线引入了潜在的偏见。现有排序算法通常假设初始检索得分无偏，从而导致代表性偏差在检索和生成环节中累积传播。

Method: 本研究评估了四种排序策略：两种现有的效用导向策略（标准排序和随机排序）以及两种本文提出的曝光感知策略（强制曝光和代表性随机）。研究利用 TREC 2022 公平排名数据集，通过 LLM 在四种问答场景中测试这些排序方法，并对比了检索排序与生成结果中的曝光偏差与效用。

Result: 研究发现，检索阶段的代表性偏差会直接传播到生成阶段，导致生成结果的人口统计学失衡。实验证明，本文提出的“代表性随机排序策略”能够实现近乎平等的曝光度，显著优于传统假设检索得分无偏的排序方法。

Conclusion: 检索排序阶段是缓解下游生成偏见的关键环节。本文提出的“代表性随机排序策略”（Representative Stochastic）通过在排序中重新引入公平性，能够有效降低检索导致的代表性偏差，并最终缓解生成输出中的人口统计学偏差。

Abstract: As Large Language Model (LLM) integration has accelerated in high-stakes domains, model hallucination is a critical issue. Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) is a technique for addressing hallucination; however, RAG's multi-component pipeline introduces vulnerabilities where biases can be introduced. This study considers two previously developed utility-focused ranking strategies (Standard and Stochastic) alongside two proposed exposure-aware approaches (Forced-Exposure and Representative Stochastic). Using the TREC 2022 Fair Ranking Dataset, which contains Wikipedia articles annotated as protected or non-protected, the LLM was asked to identify relevant articles with citations for four scenario-based Q&A prompts. The retrieval rankings and the generated outputs were evaluated for exposure bias and utility across all ranking methods. Overall, the Representative Stochastic ranker resulted in a statistically significant near-parity average exposure, acknowledging that relevance scores initially produced during retrieval are already shaped by representational bias, whereas the other rankers assume those scores are unbiased. Across all the methods of document ranking, generation demographic parity closely mirrored the exposure parity, reinforcing that representational bias in RAG systems is driven by retrieval and propagates to generation. These findings highlight that retrieval ranking is a critical point for mitigating downstream bias and propose a Representative Stochastic ranker that reintroduces fairness in RAG systems.

</details>


### [243] [Code-Guided Reasoning for Small Language Models: Evaluating Executable MCQA Scaffolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18827)
*Prateek Biswas,Dhaval Patel,Vedant Khandelwal,Shuxin Lin,Amit Sheth*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出了“代码引导推理”（CGR）协议，旨在评估外部代码辅助如何提升小语言模型在多项选择问答中的表现。研究表明，辅助推理能显著提高模型准确率，同时也为理解和追踪模型推理过程提供了标准化的评估工具和资源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的多项选择问答（MCQA）基准测试往往将小语言模型（SLMs）视为孤立的直接回答者，而忽略了实际部署系统中广泛使用的外部工具（如代码、反复推理调用等）对模型性能的增强作用。因此，需要一套能够衡量并评估这些“推理脚手架”对模型能力提升效果的标准化协议。

Method: 作者提出了“代码引导推理”（Code-Guided Reasoning, CGR）评估协议。该协议包含六个标准化组件：归一化项目接口、直接求解器提示、生成器提示、Python辅助代码、求解器调用与结果提取辅助工具，以及三通道结果记录系统。研究通过对比直接回答与通过Python代码辅助生成的回答，量化了性能差异。

Result: 在包含20,498条结果的MCQA数据集上，实验显示辅助推理使宏观准确率从38.11%提升至66.21%，提升了28.10个百分点。在更严格的条件筛选下，准确率提升幅度仍达14.11个百分点。实验同时指出，该方法存在资源开销大、提取过程脆弱及部分生成的代码违反指令等问题。

Conclusion: CGR协议有效地量化了通过代码执行辅助推理对小语言模型（SLMs）在多项选择问答（MCQA）任务中的性能提升。虽然辅助推理显著提高了准确率，但该评估框架也揭示了其在计算成本、答案提取稳定性和指令遵循方面的局限性。CGR为未来构建更稳健、可解释的语言模型评估系统提供了标准化的工具和数据集。

Abstract: Multiple-choice QA benchmarks usually evaluate small language models (SLMs) as direct answerers, but deployed language-model systems increasingly rely on external scaffolds such as tools, code, and repeated model calls. We introduce Code-Guided Reasoning (CGR), an evaluation protocol and generated-program resource for measuring when executable reasoning scaffolds improve SLM performance on MCQA tasks. CGR standardizes six components: a normalized item interface, a direct solver prompt, a generator prompt, a Python scaffold, solver-call and extraction helpers, and a three-channel result record. On 20,498 retained result rows from a locally prepared MCQA bundle and six metadata-registered solver models, the observed non-zero-baseline partition shows 66.21% macro assisted accuracy versus 38.11% direct accuracy, a +28.10 percentage-point difference with a pair-bootstrap interval of [20.32, 36.43]. Under a stricter Ab > 30% direct-signal gate, the macro difference is +14.11 points. These estimates are descriptive. Assisted inference uses a larger solver-call budget, answer extraction is brittle, Time-MQA contains the observed regressions, and some generated programs violate the no-hard-coding instruction. CGR provides the trace package needed to interpret these results, including direct, assisted, and generator-side answers, partition definitions, generated programs, response metadata, and audits.

Abstract: We introduce KadiAssistant, a privacy-by-design AI assistant integrated into the Kadi research data ecosystem, enabling researchers to efficiently access, aggregate, and synthesize information from heterogeneous, privacy-sensitive research data. Interdisciplinary fields such as materials science bring together disciplines with their own terminology and standards. While this convergence fuels innovation, it also makes it increasingly difficult to connect and access knowledge, as data are distributed across disciplines, organizations, and individuals. For example, battery research combines electrochemical measurements, materials characterization data, physics-based simulations, and manufacturing parameters, each using different formats, vocabularies, and standards. Efficiently storing and sharing such heterogeneous data via research data platforms, such as Kadi4Mat, demands domain knowledge, technical expertise, and familiarity with metadata schemas and interfaces. Research data also vary in sensitivity: newly generated 'warm' data are often private, whereas published 'cold' data are usually openly accessible. The Kadi ecosystem offers fine-grained access control needed for sensitive data. A solution for efficient information retrieval in Kadi must therefore respect the fine-grained access permissions. To address these intertwined challenges of information retrieval, strong data privacy, and complex access control, KadiAssistant combines a self-hosted large language model (LLM) with a privacy-preserving semantic search, inspired by retrieval-augmented generation, that can access files and record metadata on Kadi. This allows the assistant to screen, aggregate, and structure information into a highly informative answer. KadiAssistant therefore bridges terminology and standards, lowers access barriers for researchers, and strengthens the Findable pillar of FAIR data principles.
